- **⚠️ BOOT BLOCKER for the owner — DEFINITIVELY isolated to uncommitted `sched_proof` WIP:** the main working tree livelocks the boot (`[sched] CPU0 deadline-starvation guard tripped` flood, marker never prints) due to a concurrent session's UNCOMMITTED work (untracked `kernel/src/sched_proof.rs` + `main.rs:1587 sched_proof::run_inline()` + dirty `scheduler.rs`/`perf.rs`/`procfs.rs`). **PROVEN it is the SOLE cause:** committed HEAD (no sched_proof) boots clean 7/7 HEALTHY in the clean worktree above. Nothing in committed `main` livelocks. **Action: the sched_proof author must fix/revert it before the next iron flash or any main-tree QEMU boot will hang.** Route to athena-debugger / the sched_proof author.
- **Beta-tester drove the live desktop (clean worktree) — found why the cars aren't usable yet.** athena-beta-tester booted the clean worktree (7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panics, SMP1+SMP2) and drove it via QMP. The Start menu renders all 18 apps with crisp AA type (no tofu), and the **launch path is PROVEN end-to-end** (control app `hello_window`: Start→Enter→`spawn_app_from_vfs`→ELF spawn→`surface 45 created` user window). But a real user CANNOT reach the 9 cars due to input defects (all 9 ELFs confirmed bundled + registered):
  - **SEV-1: xHCI HID input ring wedge — FIXED + LIVE-VERIFIED [~] (commit `c064651`).** Root cause: HID transfer ring drained to zero outstanding TDs → no queued TD → no completion event could re-arm → permanent silent stall. Fix: `outstanding_tds` tracking + `top_up_hid_endpoints()` re-posts the shortfall every drain cycle (self-healing). Beta-tester live: **539 HID events, 0 wedge** (was ~16). `[xhci] HID-ring recycle model -> PASS`.
  - **SEV-2: arrow/nav keys — FIXED + LIVE-VERIFIED [~] (commit `c064651`).** Added 10 nav usages as EXTENDED (0xE0-prefixed) set-1 scancodes so `shell_runner::handle_key`'s `(true,0x50)` arms fire. Beta-tester live: Start-menu/palette selection moves bidirectionally (was stuck on item 0). `[usb-hid] nav-keymap model -> PASS`.
  - **OOBE: use-without-account + render-race + menu-close — FIXED [~] (commit `0551cda`).** "Skip — use without an account" (Esc→guest session; honors Concept "no forced account" vs Windows 11) + setup-card render-race guard + Start-menu-closes-on-launch. `[oobe] skip smoketest -> PASS`.
  - **App-launch crash — FIXED + LIVE-CONFIRMED [~] (commit `1f53d46`).** Native ELF spawn mapped only 5 pages (20 KiB) user stack → big athkit apps overflowed (Files faulted just below the base; `hello_window` fit). Grew to 256 pages (1 MiB) + const-assert invariant. Beta-tester: Files now spawns + relocates with NO launch page-fault (the old crash is gone).
  - **Start-menu visibility — FIXED + LIVE-CONFIRMED [~] (commits `5d71267` twin, `7e26282` LIVE).** The live `lib.rs` StartMenu painted bare `GLASS_TINT_DARK` (deprecated, no frost/WCAG-cap/rim) → invisible over the aurora. Now routes through `athgfx::glass::draw_glass_surface(GLASS_POPOVER_DARK)` (same stack as Control Center). Beta-tester: panel now clearly visible + populated with the app list. FAIL-able KAT (interior luma spread 26.6→0.8). Also fixes "washed-out contrast".
  - **SYS_SESSION_INFO deadlock — ROOT CAUSE of both the triple-fault AND the window-stall — FIXED [~] (commit `f530a67`, athena-debugger verified).** Not a fault: `session::write_info` (syscall 92) held `SESSION.lock()` then called `home_dir()→username()→SESSION.lock()` again — re-entered a non-reentrant spin::Mutex → CPU0 spins forever (IF=0, no preempt) → wedge → CPU reset (looked like a triple-fault). Same hazard `dump_text` was already fixed for; `write_info` was missed. Newly reachable once the 1 MiB stack let apps reach `session_info()` at launch → EVERY app-launch deadlocked. Fix: hoist `home_dir()` before the lock. **Debugger SMP=1 verified: Files now LAUNCHES + WINDOWS (`surface 45 created: 760x480` — the window that "never appeared"), SESSION_INFO completes clean, 0 faults.** + defensive `interrupts.rs` guard against silent triple-faults from kernel null-call→panic-fmt recursion (raw-serial + halt). - **Browser app — render + execute + interactive + fetch [~] (commits `2b86cf3`, `9e7005c`, `20ca851`, `ca2792f`).** New `apps/browser` wiring orphaned `athweb` (HTML/CSS engine) + `ath_js` (real ECMAScript interpreter): (1) renders local `.html`/`about:home` via athweb parse→cascade→layout→paint, executes inline `<script>` in ath_js (6 KATs); (2) **closed the JS↔DOM engine gap** — new public `ath_js` embedder host-object API + `athweb::DomDocument`, so `document.getElementById(id).textContent = …` mutates the real DOM and re-lays-out (12 KATs, FAIL-demonstrated); (3) **http:// URL fetch** via athweb's injectable `HttpTransport` seam — mock-proven fetch→render→JS + honest error pages (404/conn-error/malformed) + bounded body + chunked framing, `RaeSocketTransport` wired for live (19 KATs); (4) soft-float-clean number formatting (dropped std `f64::trunc/abs`). **Built + host-proven; NOT yet bundlable** — blocked on the pre-existing `athnet` poly1305 SIMD bare-build codegen issue (components/athnet, held by a concurrent agent) + needs `shell_runner.rs`/`config` registration. Deferred (honest): `addEventListener`/click→event-loop, `createElement`/`appendChild`, `https://` (TLS), live connectivity (iron DHCP-Bound). **CSS color completeness 2026-06-23 (commit `62d8e6a`):** athweb now parses `hsl()`/`hsla()` (was dropped to an inert Function — only rgb()/rgba() worked) via a libm-free HSL→RGB conversion that links on `x86_64-unknown-none`; and `parse_css_color_value` (PWA manifest theme/background colors) now resolves named colors + 8-digit hex + rgb()/hsl() instead of silently returning white. +2 KATs (13 total). Note: `cargo build -p athweb --target x86_64-unknown-none` now **Finished** clean — the earlier poly1305 bare-build blocker did not reproduce here (re-verify before relying on it for bundling). **CSS custom properties 2026-06-23 (commit `0f6cafc`):** `var(--token)` / `var(--token, fallback)` now resolve — athweb didn't handle them at all (fell through to an inert Function). `parse_css` runs a post-parse pass collecting `--name` defs into a global pool (last-wins; documented simplification vs per-element scoped cascade — covers the dominant `:root` design-token pattern) and rewriting consumers, with bounded var→var recursion + undefined→None. +1 KAT (14 total). **Box shorthand bug fixed 2026-06-23 (commit `5601dbd`):** `margin`/`padding` 2/3/4-value shorthand (`padding: 10px 20px 30px 40px`) parsed to `CssValue::Multiple`, which hit `to_px()`'s `_ => 0.0` arm — so resolve_edge silently zeroed ALL four sides on every page using multi-value box shorthand (near-universal). Now expands per the CSS clockwise rules. +1 KAT (15 total). **HTML named entities 2026-06-23 (commit `c12aa44`):** the entity table had only 16 named entities (numeric `&#nnn;`/`&#xhhh;` already worked) — added ~90 high-frequency ones (full Latin-1 accented set + smart quotes + currency + math/symbols/arrows), so `caf&eacute;` / `&ldquo;…&rdquo;` / `&times;` render as real glyphs instead of literal `&eacute;` garbage. +1 KAT (16 total). **CSS combinators fixed 2026-06-23 (commit `e6efe27`):** descendant/child combinators (`div p`, `ul > li`, `.nav a`) matched on ONLY the rightmost compound — so every such rule applied to every matching element page-wide regardless of ancestry (a top-tier style-fidelity bug). New `selector_matches_ctx` flattens the chain + walks the ancestor chain right-to-left (descendant=search-upward, child=one-level); `build_styled_tree` threads the ancestor chain. Sibling combinators keep the prior lenient match (no regression). +1 KAT (17 total). The DOM query path (`querySelectorAll`/`querySelector`) got the same ancestor-aware matching in `84aae9b` (+1 KAT, 18 total) — `document.querySelectorAll('div p')` no longer returns every `<p>`. Sibling combinators (`+`/`~`) landed in `6e0cb34` (+1 KAT, 19 total) via a recursive `match_subchain` that walks ancestors AND preceding siblings — all four CSS combinators now resolve correctly on both the styler and the query path (only `sibling-left-of-ancestor` like `h1 + div p` safely under-matches). **@media queries 2026-06-23 (commit `bd51aad`):** responsive CSS was parsed but DROPPED in the cascade (`CssRule::Media(_) => {}`) — now `expand_media_rules` flattens matching `@media (min/max-width)` blocks to top-level rules by viewport width (RenderPipeline render paths). +1 KAT (20 total). **text-transform 2026-06-23 (commit `a4c23e3`):** the property was inherited but never APPLIED to rendered text — now `uppercase`/`lowercase` transform the text in build_layout_tree (correct despite per-character text fragmentation). `capitalize` left a documented no-op (needs word boundaries the per-char fragmentation hides — a render dump shows `hello world` = 11 single-char boxes; a render dump showed `hello world` = 11 single-char boxes). +1 KAT (21 total). **Text-run coalescing 2026-06-23 (commit `9060e61`):** root-caused the per-char fragmentation to parse_html creating one text node PER CHARACTER — now consecutive `Character` tokens coalesce into one text node. Two wins: `capitalize` re-enabled + correct (`hello world`->`Hello World`), and a measured perf cut — render smoketest dom_nodes 29->8, styled 29->8 (fewer boxes = less layout/paint). **box-sizing: border-box 2026-06-23 (commit `8b313a6`):** was unhandled (width always content-box) — block layout now subtracts padding+border from the content box for an explicit width/height under border-box (the modern reset default `* { box-sizing: border-box }`). +1 KAT (22 total). **white-space: nowrap/pre 2026-06-23 (commit `0a152b5`):** layout_inline ignored white-space, so `nowrap` (nav items/buttons) still wrapped — now forces a single line (pre-wrap/pre-line still wrap). +1 KAT (23 total). **CSS calc() 2026-06-23 (commit `4ec72f3`):** the canonical responsive primitive, previously unsupported (the tokenizer swallowed a lone `-` as Number(0)) — now a tokenizer fix + recursive-descent evaluator (px/%/number, * before +, parens) with a new `CssValue::Calc{px,pct}` resolved against the container at layout. `calc(100% - 250px)` works; em/rem/vw left unevaluated (honest). +1 KAT (24 total). **flex-grow 2026-06-23 (commit `296b47b`):** layout_flex applied direction/justify/align/gap but never flex-grow (`flex: 1`, the most common flex behavior) — row flex now distributes leftover main-axis space by grow factor. +1 KAT (25 total). Honest gap: auto-basis flex items still take block auto-width (full container) not shrink-to-fit content; column-axis grow not yet handled. **text-align 2026-06-23 (commit `53fd4ec`):** inherited but never applied — `text-align: center`/`right` (headings/buttons/nav) rendered left; now shifts a single text line within its available width. +1 KAT (26 total). Gap: per-line alignment of wrapped multi-line text. **text-decoration: underline 2026-06-23 (commit `4f7634d`):** the FillText paint command dropped underline, so links (underlined by default via the `<a>` style) + `<u>` rendered as plain text — FillText now carries `underline` and the backend draws a baseline rule. +1 KAT (27 total). (font-style: italic still not carried — needs athgfx glyph slanting.) **List markers 2026-06-23 (commit `7678ec2`):** `<li>` had display:list-item but NO marker drawn — and the deeper bug was `display()` never mapping `list-item` -> `DisplayMode::ListItem` (the mode was dead). Now `<ul>` draws bullets, `<ol>` draws 1./2./3. (numbered via a new LayoutBox.list_index), `list-style-type: none` suppresses. +1 KAT (28 total). **visibility: hidden 2026-06-23 (commit `4dcca20`):** inherited but never applied — paint now skips a hidden box's own content (keeping its layout space, unlike display:none) while still recursing children so a `visibility:visible` descendant overrides. +1 KAT (29 total). **text-decoration: line-through 2026-06-23 (commit `4260cd3`):** completes the decoration story — FillText now carries `strikethrough`, backend draws a rule through the text middle; `<u>`/`<ins>` get default underline + `<s>`/`<del>`/`<strike>` default line-through (split from the generic inline arm). +1 KAT (30 total). **linear-gradient backgrounds 2026-06-23 (commit `b24f1b6`):** `background: linear-gradient(...)` (modern UI everywhere) was dropped (paint_background only handled solid colors) — now a new FillGradient command paints vertical gradients (default / to bottom / to top) via athgfx fill_rect_gradient; horizontal/angle degrade to solid first color. +1 KAT (31 total). **Nested CSS functions 2026-06-23 (commit `d5a0790`):** the value parser's flat function-arg loop broke at the first `)`, so `rgb()`/`hsl()` inside another function (gradient stops!) lost their args — now a recursive parse_func_args resolves nested colors at any depth (the gradient named/hex-only limitation is lifted). +1 KAT (32 total). **Integration verified 2026-06-23:** the browser app is fully wired — `apps/browser` in `config/base.toml` (bundled) + registered in `shell_runner.rs` + bare-builds clean (old poly1305 blocker gone). So the session's render-engine work feeds a launchable Browser. **HTML rawtext bug fixed 2026-06-23 (commit `5bc6720`):** the tokenizer had no rawtext state, so a `<` inside `<script>`/`<style>` (a JS comparison `a < b` / CSS `>` combinator — extremely common) started a spurious tag and TRUNCATED the script/style body — a real break for inline JS execution. Now a `rawtext` mode consumes content verbatim until `</tag`. +1 KAT (33 athweb total). **Implicit tag closing 2026-06-23 (commit `50b25ca`):** the parser never closed optional-end-tag elements, so `<li>a<li>b` nested the 2nd <li> INSIDE the 1st and `<p>text<div>` nested the div in the p — authors omit these end tags constantly. New `implies_close` pops elements whose end tag a start tag implies (li/p/dt/dd/option/table cells). +1 KAT (34 athweb total). **@import swallow bug 2026-06-23 (commit `bd8ca5f`):** skip_until_next_rule (for unhandled at-rules) only stopped at a block's `}`, so a STATEMENT at-rule with no block (`@import "x";` — at the TOP of most stylesheets) ran past its `;` and consumed the FOLLOWING style rule. Now breaks at a depth-0 `;`. +1 KAT (35 athweb total). **`border` shorthand + value-list nested fns 2026-06-23 (commit `a90f782`):** `border: 1px solid red` (the standard border syntax) set only a `border` prop while layout reads border-width/-style/-color longhands — so it rendered NO border. Now apply_declaration expands it (cascade-correct); and the space-separated value branch recurses into nested functions so `border: 1px solid rgb(...)` / `box-shadow: 0 0 4px rgb(...)` resolve. +1 KAT (36 athweb total). **background shorthand color 2026-06-23 (commit `1324f21`):** paint_background only matched a bare Color, so `background: #fff url(x) no-repeat` (a Multiple) painted no bg color — now extracts the color component. +1 KAT (37 athweb total). **font shorthand 2026-06-23 (commit `a58b2ea`):** `font: italic bold 16px Georgia` set only a `font` prop while paint reads the longhands — now apply_font_shorthand expands style/weight/size/family (font-size is the pivot). Completes the shorthand set (margin/padding, border, background, font). +1 KAT (38 athweb total). **inherit/initial keywords 2026-06-23 (commit `10f010c`):** parsed but never resolved, so `color: inherit` (links/buttons matching their container) set an inert keyword that readers ignored — now the cascade resolves `inherit` to the parent's computed value and `initial` to a reset. +1 KAT (39 athweb total). **border-color default = currentColor 2026-06-23 (commit `89dec51`):** paint_borders defaulted an unset border-color to BLACK, but CSS defaults it to `currentColor` (the element's color) — so a colored element with `border: 1px solid` drew a black border. Now resolves to the element's `color`; `currentColor` keyword handled. +1 KAT (40 athweb total). **Loader text decoding 2026-06-23 (commit `0cbbb83`):** Resource::as_text assumed UTF-8 and DROPPED every non-ASCII byte on failure — so a legacy ISO-8859-1/Windows-1252 page lost all accented chars; a UTF-8 BOM survived as a stray U+FEFF. Now strips a leading BOM + decodes non-UTF-8 as Latin-1 (preserves the text). +1 KAT (41 athweb total). **text-shadow 2026-06-23 (commit `a5fbb71`):** unhandled (no effect) — now paint_text draws an offset shadow copy behind the text (hard shadow; blur≈none), parallel to box-shadow. +1 KAT (42 athweb total). **Presentational attrs + inline-block size 2026-06-23 (commit `6fdecb6`):** `<img width=200>`/`<td bgcolor>`/`<font color>` (legacy HTML/email) were ignored — now mapped to low-priority CSS. The fix surfaced a deeper bug: layout_inline OVERWROTE an inline-block's explicit width (->container) and height (->0), discarding any explicit size; now preserved. +1 KAT (43 athweb total). **inline-block min/max clamp 2026-06-23 (commit `27abfcc`):** layout_inline never applied min/max-width/-height (so `button { min-width }` was ignored); now clamps like layout_block. +1 KAT (44 athweb total). **Integration re-verified 2026-06-23:** full OS image (`xtask build --release`) builds with ALL session athweb work (44 KATs) and QEMU-boots clean — `System successfully booted`, 0 real `[PANIC]`s — so the hardened render engine remains integrated + bootable. **Whitespace collapsing 2026-06-23 (commit `04af598`):** athweb never collapsed whitespace, so source-formatted HTML (every real page) rendered its inter-tag newlines + indentation literally — now runs of whitespace collapse to a single space (CSS white-space: normal); `<pre>` split out with white-space:pre + monospace. +1 KAT (45 athweb total). **URL parse bug fixed 2026-06-23 (commit `189feae`):** athnet's live `HttpUrl::parse` split authority/path on '/' only, so a query-without-path (`http://host?q=1`, common with tracking params) folded the query INTO the host and dropped it — now splits at the first '/' or '?' (bare query -> origin-form `/?...`). +1 KAT (109 athnet KATs). **Redirect resolution RFC 3986 2026-06-23 (commit `eda0e16`):** `resolve_redirect` joined relative `Location`s verbatim, so `../page` sent a non-normalized `/a/b/../page` and a protocol-relative `//host/path` folded into the BASE host — now normalize_path resolves `.`/`..` and `//host` switches host. +1 KAT (110 athnet KATs). **Cookie Expires parsing 2026-06-23 (commit `67cc6d3`):** Cookie::parse skipped `Expires` (documented limitation), so a persistent cookie set via `Expires` (no `Max-Age`) was demoted to session-only and lost on restart — now parse_http_date (IMF-fixdate + RFC 850, Hinnant date math, epoch-anchor-tested) makes them persistent; Max-Age still wins. +2 KATs (112 athnet KATs).

### PRODUCTION POLISH PUSH (2026-06-16, owner directive — pause iron iteration, code backwards from "shipped")

Owner directive: stop QEMU/flash iteration for now; code everything codeable toward a Windows-level-polished, Apple-attention-to-detail consumer OS, then resume testing. North star = `LEGACY_GAMING_CONCEPT.md` + rival Windows/macOS ([[goal-rival-windows-macos]]). Five workstreams:

- **WS1 — Production build mode (clean silent boot).** A `production` cargo feature: skip the boot-smoketest RUNNER (after separating real-init from pure-test — several `run_boot_smoketest`s also DO init, e.g. xHCI arms HID + spawns the drain thread, so they can't be naively removed → that would brick boot), force the console mirror OFF from boot, minimize screen logging. Dev build keeps full smoketests + logs for verification. **Decision: GATE, don't delete** — the FAIL-able smoketests are the only proof the OS works; deleting the proof infrastructure makes "perfect/optimized" unverifiable. Reversible, standard debug-vs-release practice. *(in progress)*
- **WS2 — Unified userspace bare-metal self-test [~] (code-complete).** `user_init::run_selftest()` (gated by `const RUN_SELFTEST`): one userspace program that exercises every claim through the REAL syscall surface — graphics (compositor surface), memory (heap grow), security (capability query), filesystem (write/stat/read+verify round trip), processes (spawn+wait a real ELF), networking (UDP socket API) — and renders a PASS/FAIL report on screen PLUS durable serial sentinels (20xxx → BOOTLOG.TXT/netlog). Flip the flag, build `--safe`, flash = a dedicated claim-verification harness. Replaces the scattered boot smoketests as the single on-iron acceptance test. Compiles clean (no warnings in the touched code). *Landed in the shared tree under commit 893bc92 (multi-agent sweep — [[multi-agent-shared-worktree]]).*
- **WS3 — MasterChecklist codeable-item completion pass.** Code every `[ ]`/`[~]` item not blocked on iron/Mesa/external; mark honestly `[~]` (never fake `[x]` — iron proof is paused). Externally blocked: real GPU submit (needs Mesa via the other agent's userspace LinuxKPI), Steam (Proton + GPU), real-HW `[x]` proof.
- **WS4 — Userspace apps + UI polish.** Make the bundled app crates real + launchable; Windows-level chrome, Apple-level detail.
- **WS5 — Optimization + correctness review.** Leak/bug hunt (severity + live-vs-dead path), hot-path allocations, lock contention, portability.

### Lead-orchestrated non-UI subsystem wave (2026-06-21, /goal — exclusive isolated slices alongside the concurrent UI session)

A second session owns the Liquid Glass UI/kernel lanes (below), so this session took exclusive ownership of isolated component crates (no UI/kernel deps, host-KAT-verifiable, zero collisions, explicit-path commits, architecture-gate verdict checked each time). All `[~]` (host-KAT-proven; iron/QEMU-integration gated). The audit-then-implement loop found+fixed **34 real bugs** across the session.

**Closing state (HEAD green sweep: 986 tests across 20 component crates, 0 failures).** This wave comprehensively covered the *provable, non-UI* surface: full image stack (BMP/GIF/PNG/JPEG/WebP-VP8L decode + PNG/JPEG encode + the ath_image dispatcher), full audio (WAV/FLAC/MP3/AAC/Opus + the player open/decode path), office (DOCX/XLSX/PDF read + DOCX/XLSX write + XLSX formula compute), mail (SMTP/IMAP/POP3), calendar/contacts (iCal/vCard + RRULE + TZ), the complete auth/security story (passkeys EdDSA+ES256 + 2FA HOTP/TOTP + keychain over a full crypto suite), sync, backup/export (tar.gz + zip writer), KV persistence, content-sniffing, a hardened JS engine (parse+execute+collections+RegExp+Promise/event-loop), and the LinuxKPI driver path (ww_mutex/drm_exec). Plus #3's arch-HAL foundation + #2's SCHED_BODY telemetry (both verifier-PASS) + 3 independent #1 visual-QA passes (→~86% CLOSE) + 7 deep security reviews (the 3 biggest hostile-input surfaces — JS engine, media decoders, network parsers — all hardened) + full merged-OS integration verified (boots 7/7 HEALTHY both SMP). The remaining work is genuinely gated: the convergence items belong to the concurrent UI session (#1 polish/light-theme, #5 app-wiring), to iron (#2 input/#4 GPU on real HW), or to a clear kernel for invasive #3 — and the unbuilt codecs (zstd/brotli/VP8-lossy/H.264) are unprovable here without reference frames the host-KAT discipline requires.

- **AthAudio — game-priority mixer + windowed-sinc SRC [~] (commits `e59792c`, `e7c01ce`).** New `GameMixer` (SCHED_BODY hot path: per-stream gain/mute, StreamPriority ducking, allocation-free steady-state mix, soft-knee limiter) + fixed 3 real DSP bugs (CRITICAL integer clip-wrap → `saturating_mix`; AudioRouter muted-route leak; output-gain compounding). + no_std soft-float windowed-sinc polyphase resampler (near-Nyquist alias −43dB, 83× quieter than linear). `cargo test -p athaudio --features dsp` 33/33. Criterion #2.
- **AthNet — TLS 1.3 handshake + server authentication [~] (commits `5204fb4`, `8a05a15`).** Full TLS 1.3 client handshake (record layer, RFC 8446 key schedule, transcript, ClientHello/ServerHello/Finished) + cert-chain validation + CertificateVerify + hostname binding, fail-closed (Connected requires valid chain→trusted anchor + hostname + CertVerify + Finished, else no app keys). **TLS now MITM-safe.** `cargo test -p athnet --features tls13` 157/157 (was 105 — hardened 2026-07-04: the previously-UNTESTED `cert_time_valid` validity-window check and `cert_public_key` SPKI extractor now have FAIL-able host-KATs oracle'd by real `openssl req -x509` Ed25519+P-256 certs with fixed validity windows; mutation-verified — neutering the `now>na` expiry arm or the P256 SPKI variant makes the tests fail). Criterion #4/#5. + DNS/HTTP1/websocket fuzz (78) — no defects. **Open follow-up:** the HTTPS client threads `now_unix` from the daemon and currently passes `None` (validity check skipped in production) — wiring AthNet's wall clock so expiry is always enforced is the next slice.
- **RaeUpdate — verified transactional A/B delta engine [~] (commit `76d3823`).** Fixed 2 real defects (NO signature verification existed; `apply_patch` was a stub never applying deltas). `SignedDeltaPayload` (SHA-256 + Ed25519 verify BEFORE apply) + `UpdateSession` (stage-to-inactive → atomic flip → auto-rollback → one-click revert → power-loss recoverable). 16/16 KATs. Concept pillar "atomic CoW updates + one-click rollback".
- **AthStore — .athpkg codec + fail-closed verify [~] (commit `ae9dc66`).** Closed the missing untrusted-bytes→trusted-package boundary: bounds-checked TLV codec (never-panic, 256MiB cap) + `parse_and_verify` (parse → integrity → signature → Ed25519). 20/20 KATs. Criterion #5.
- **ath_linuxkpi — list/hlist/klist/rculist/xarray/llist C-ABI facades [~] (commits `352d8fc`, `ce612fb`, `9b065ce`).** The pervasive Linux-driver structures (BO/DRM/fence lists, GEM-handle/fence maps, scheduler free-job lists) — `#[no_mangle]` C-ABI, BTF-verified layouts, klist refcount-pinned iterator (deferred-free contract), rculist no-op read-side, xarray alloc/cyclic, llist lock-less. 23/23 KATs (incl. a fixed parallel-test flakiness defect). Criterion #4 (LinuxKPI driver-breadth path).
- **athhid — gamepad controller parsing [~] (commit `9ad583f`).** Cross-controller GamepadState + DualSense/Xbox/generic-HID parsers + rumble encode + deadzone/normalization. Found+fixed 2 real hidreport panics (empty/short report — latent in mouse/keyboard too). 25/25 KATs (concrete decodes; truncated never-panic). Criterion #2 (embodiment-first controllers).
- **ath_pwa — manifest URL resolution + InstallDescriptor [~] (commit `85523dc`).** RFC-3986 reference resolution + origin extraction + maskable-icon selection + the end-to-end installable record (absolute URLs + origin) — makes a parsed manifest actually launchable. 23/23 KATs. Criterion #5 (installable web apps).
- **athvpn — real Noise_IKpsk2 WireGuard handshake [~] (commit `928b74d`).** Fixed a CRITICAL defect: the prior handshake sent the static key in CLEARTEXT + never derived matching keys. Now spec-correct (HMAC-BLAKE2s/KDF_n, mix_hash, encrypted static/timestamp, MAC1 constant-time verify, PSK, direction-correct key split). 9/9 KATs (matching keys + static-not-cleartext + tamper/forge rejected). Concept "built-in WireGuard". **Transport anti-replay LANDED 2026-06-23 (commit `2483a28`):** `TransportSession::decrypt_packet` had NO anti-replay (it tracked `receiving_counter_max` but never rejected a replayed counter) — a captured encrypted data packet could be replayed and re-accepted indefinitely. Now a proper RFC 6479 64-counter sliding window (`spin::Mutex<ReplayWindow>`, &self-safe): authenticate first, then drop replayed / >64-behind counters while tolerating in-window UDP reordering. 18/18 KATs (window in-order/replay/reorder/too-old/jump + decrypt_packet replay-dropped + reordering-still-accepted); bare build + full xtask + QEMU clean. **IPsec SPD lookup ALSO fixed (commit `b0e33e1`):** `Spd::lookup` ignored its src/dst args (matched protocol only -> wrong policy applied); now matches src/dst CIDR + protocol via a new `cidr_match` (20/20 KATs). **IPsec ESP anti-replay ALSO fixed (commit `ff9b185`):** `esp_decrypt`'s `seq % 64` toy (false-rejected seq>=64, broke after 64 packets, checked replay before auth) replaced with a proper RFC 6479 sliding window (authenticate-first, `recv_highest` + bitmap), 22/22 KATs. **athvpn anti-replay/policy now FULLY hardened across both protocols** — WireGuard transport (2483a28) + IPsec SPD CIDR lookup (b0e33e1) + IPsec ESP anti-replay (ff9b185); no open VPN security findings.

- **athcloud client-side encryption de-stubbed — was plaintext [~] (security, /goal 2026-06-22, commit `ffa831e`).** `athcloud::KeyManager::encrypt_blob` did NOT encrypt: it stored the plaintext in the clear wrapped with a zero `// nonce placeholder` + zero `// tag placeholder`, and `decrypt_blob` just stripped them — RaeCloud's "client-side encryption" for multi-provider cloud sync sent user data to the cloud in **plaintext with no confidentiality or integrity**. Now real ChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD via `ath_crypto` (new no_std dep): blob = `nonce(12) || ciphertext || tag(16)`, caller supplies a unique 96-bit nonce (documented entropy dependency); `decrypt_blob` verifies the Poly1305 tag and fails closed (`CorruptedData`) on a tampered ct/tag/nonce or wrong key; AES-256-GCM/XChaCha keys error rather than emit fake output. - **SCHED_BODY/EDF frame-deadline adherence PROVEN under load [~] (commits `fe4aa57` sched_proof + `6ad3710` harness fix; criterion #2 "strong gaming performance via SCHED_BODY/EDF").** Built a live workload proof (`kernel/src/sched_proof.rs`): a real SCHED_BODY EDF frame task (16.67ms period / 14ms deadline) vs 3 competing SCHED_NORMAL CPU-hogs, run a bounded window, asserts via the deadline telemetry. **athena-verifier ran 10 boots (5×smp1 + 5×smp2): frame_misses=0 + worst_lateness=0ns on EVERY boot, EDF preempting the live Normal load (picks.game 184–252 vs normal 6–105), 7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panic** — SCHED_BODY provably meets its frame deadline under load. NO regression (frame_misses 0–1 ≤ budget, frame worst_late=0us, 6 boots both SMP). The short EDF periods are now live + self-measure real lateness, and the correct wall-clock HONESTLY reveals what the old tick-clock hid: **sub-3ms audio (2.67ms) + 6ms input can't keep cadence under QEMU-TCG because the LAPIC tick is 10ms (HZ=100) > those periods** (~18ms lateness) — a real TCG-floor finding, NOT a fake PASS. **So sub-3ms audio is genuinely iron-gated** (finer tick + real HW audio round-trip, AthAudio Phase 7); a high-res/tickless one-shot LAPIC timer would let sub-10ms EDF hit 0 in QEMU too (deferred). Net #2: frame-deadline PROVEN in QEMU + the EDF clock now correct (wall-time); sub-3ms honestly iron-gated. (Independent athena-verifier CONFIRMED at clean HEAD: 7/7 HEALTHY both SMP, 10/10 smoketests, 0 panic, all markers incl. `EDF wall-clock active`, frame_misses 1-2 <= budget = no regression. INFO (out of #6 scope): MP3/AAC are per-stage-referenced not bit-exact — a future bit-exact KAT would close that correctness gap. - **athnet network-parser security review + TLS-stream DoS fix [~] (review + commit `a0c4301`).** athena-reviewer hard-audited the remote attack surface (TLS record/handshake, HTTP/1, WebSocket, DNS/mDNS, SSDP on attacker-controlled bytes). 5 parsers SHIP (TLS handshake state machine fail-closed re-confirmed; DNS compression-pointer loop capped; WebSocket 64-bit length pre-checked; HTTP chunked bounded). 1 FIX-FIRST fixed (31 bugs total): a HIGH remote DoS reachable on byte-1 of any HTTPS fetch — `TlsRecord::parse` returned `None` for both "need more" and "oversized length", so the read loop hung/OOM'd on an `0xFFFF` record header (no crypto needed, MITM). Fixed: 3-state `parse_state` (Invalid→hard-reject) + `in_buf`/handshake-flight byte caps + RFC-8446 16640 cap + SSDP service cap. 121 KATs (+7 incl. the oversized-header test that OOMs/hangs on old code). Criterion #6 ("hostile network bytes never crash/hang the host") now HOLDS — the three biggest hostile-input surfaces (JS engine, media decoders, network parsers) are all reviewed + #6-safe.
- **Auth story COMPLETE — passkeys (ES256 wired) + 2FA [~] (commits `b827e94`, `313b3cc`).** (1) ES256 wiring: athid's verify_assertion now verifies ES256 assertions via ath_crypto::p256_ecdsa (was UnsupportedAlgorithm) — the algorithm every hardware security key uses; 31 athid KATs (ES256 RFC-6979-vector verifies + tamper/malformed fail-closed). EdDSA + ES256 both work. **Second path closed 2026-06-22 (/goal, commit `a21b4a6`):** a SEPARATE ceremony login path, `PasskeyCeremony::verify_auth_response`, was STILL a stub (`if response.signature.is_empty()` only — "we verify structural correctness only" = any non-empty signature passed = auth bypass); now it cryptographically verifies the ES256 assertion over `authenticator_data || client_data_hash` via `ath_crypto::p256_ecdsa::verify`, fail-closed. 32 athid KATs (+1: a real openssl-generated P-256 assertion verifies; tampered-sig / tampered-auth-data / wrong-pubkey / empty-sig all -> InvalidSignature). Full xtask build + QEMU CI clean (7/7 HEALTHY). (2) 2FA: ath_crypto += SHA-1 (RFC 3174, OTP/legacy-compat-only documented) + HMAC (RFC 2104, +11 KATs), and new `ath_otp` crate — HOTP (RFC 4226) + TOTP (RFC 6238 SHA-1 & SHA-256) + base32 + otpauth:// QR import + skew-verify, proven against the published RFC App-D/App-B vectors (15 KATs, airtight). **Auth now: passkeys + 2FA + password** — the full daily-driver authentication surface. Criterion #5.
- **THIRD passkey-verify path closed — the LOCK SCREEN [~] (2026-07-04, `fake-crypto-stub-epidemic` class).** After athid's two ceremony paths, a THIRD passkey verifier lived in `athshell::lock_screen::PasskeyManager::verify_response` — the desktop's front door — and it did NO cryptography: it ignored the `_credential_id` (underscore-unused), took no signature at all, and returned `Verified` whenever *any* credential with a non-empty id was registered. `PasskeyCredential` didn't even store a public key, so it structurally could not verify. Currently DEAD (no callers, `PasskeyStatus::Verified` never consumed to unlock) but a latent lock-screen bypass the moment someone wires it trusting the name. Fixed: `PasskeyCredential` now stores the authenticator's ES256 public key (registration refuses a key our verifier can't parse); `verify_response(credential_id, authenticator_data, client_data_hash, signature, now)` matches the named credential and verifies a real ES256 assertion over `authenticator_data || client_data_hash` via `ath_crypto::p256_ecdsa::verify` (the already-RFC-proven primitive — NOT a athid-ceremony twin; RP-ID-hash/flags/counter checks documented as follow-up), fail-closed on expired-challenge / unknown-id / short-hash / bad-sig. 7 FAIL-able host-KATs (real openssl/Python-generated ES256 assertion verifies; tampered-sig / tampered-authData / wrong-credential / <32B-hash / timed-out-challenge / malformed-key-can't-register all rejected) — mutation-verified: reintroducing the always-true bypass fails the tamper tests. `cargo test -p athshell --lib` clean; full xtask build + QEMU CI 0-panic `System successfully booted`. Concept "security by default, not by friction."
- **Full integration boot verify at clean HEAD — PASS both SMP (criterion #6).** With the whole tree clean (this session's ~46 non-UI slices + the concurrent UI session's work all committed), athena-verifier built + booted the MERGED OS: build exit 0 (both images), smp1+smp2 boot exit 0, `System successfully booted`, boot health **7/7 HEALTHY**, **9/9 smoketests**, **0 panics**, procfs snapshot (99 endpoints) clean. No new WARN/FAIL (only the known QEMU-TCG boot-time WARN + benign baseline). The integrated OS is healthy.
- **ath_keychain secure credential store [~] (commit `120a67a`).** The OS keychain (macOS Keychain / Win Credential Manager equivalent): Credential{service,account,secret,metadata} encrypted-at-rest via ath_crypto argon2id master-key KDF + chacha20poly1305 AEAD, the AEAD AAD binding the entire header (no downgrade/swap). Wrong passphrase → fail-closed Err (no oracle); secrets zeroized + Debug-redacted; list() exposes only (service,account). Honest no_std entropy (caller/seed salt+nonce). Found+fixed an exploit-class bug (32nd): `open` ran argon2 with the UNTRUSTED header's cost params before any tag check → a hostile header forced a ~3 TB alloc (OOM-DoS); fixed with hard caps before derive. 25 KATs (round-trip, wrong-pass, tamper, AAD-swap, list/Debug-no-leak, absurd-cost-rejected, 5k-fuzz). Completes the security/auth story: **passkeys + 2FA + keychain** over the full crypto suite. Criterion #5/#6.
- **ath_webp VP8L decoder [~] (commit `b3afc03`).** Completes the image-decode stack (BMP/GIF/PNG/JPEG + WebP) with the dominant modern web format. RIFF/WEBP container + VP8L LOSSLESS fully decoded: canonical Huffman (simple/normal/single-symbol), 5-codes/meta-group + meta-Huffman entropy image, LZ77 backrefs w/ the 2-D distance map + color cache, all 4 transforms reversed (predictor 14 modes / color / subtract-green / color-indexing 1-8bpp). ARGB8888, same model as the other decoders. VP8 lossy honestly deferred (UnsupportedLossy — a separate intra-video-decoder slice). #![forbid(unsafe_code)], bounded → never panic/OOM/hang. 14 KATs (end-to-end exact-pixel VP8L via hand-built bitstream + transform reversal + hostile battery + 60k-iter fuzz). Criterion #5.
- **ath_image unified decode/encode dispatcher [~] (commit `2e160e2`).** The cohesion seam: `decode(bytes) -> Image` sniffs the format by MAGIC bytes (ath_formats, not extension) and dispatches to PNG/JPEG/BMP/GIF/WebP; `encode(&Image, Png|Jpeg{q})` for the two encoders (others UnsupportedEncode by construction). Unified `Image{w,h,pixels:Vec<u32> ARGB8888}` (the athgfx Canvas model). Thin (no decode logic — sniff + field-move + exhaustive error mapping), #![forbid(unsafe_code)], never-panic. 13 KATs (per-format dispatch exact-pixel, the magic-not-extension proof [PNG named .jpg decodes as PNG], encode round-trips, hostile→Err, 4k fuzz). Photos/athplay/athgfx now have one "open/save any image" call — the image stack is realized end-to-end. Criterion #5.
- **Image-decoder security review — bmp/webp SHIP, gif OOM fixed (criterion #6).** athena-reviewer audited the 3 not-yet-reviewed untrusted-image decoders (png/jpeg already done). ath_bmp SHIP, ath_webp SHIP (Huffman/backref/transform/color-cache bounded). ath_gif FIX-FIRST (33rd bug): a HIGH frame×canvas OOM — frames each cloned the full canvas, capped only by MAX_FRAMES + MAX_PIXELS *separately*, never their product → a crafted large-canvas×many-frame GIF pinned ~1 TB from ~80 KB (762 MB reproduced; fuzzers miss it). Fixed (`d5c5e28`): cumulative MAX_TOTAL_FRAME_PIXELS=256M (1 GiB) budget before each clone → Err, legitimate GIFs still decode. With this, ALL untrusted-input parsers this session (JS engine, media decoders, network parsers, office readers, all 5 image decoders) are reviewed + hardened — #6's "never crash/hang/OOM on hostile input" holds across the whole ingest surface.

- **Crypto-foundation security review — all SHIP (criterion #6).** athena-reviewer audited the session's crypto additions (sha1/hmac/p256_ecdsa) + the chacha20poly1305 open path + the auth consumers (ath_otp/ath_keychain/athid). ZERO findings (9th review): the two secret-comparisons (TOTP `ct_eq_str`, keychain AEAD-tag check) empirically traced to *accumulate-not-short-circuit* (genuinely constant-time, no oracle); no in-crate nonce-reuse (the safe `to_bytes_with_nonce` rotation API is provided + documented); transient plaintext + derived keys zeroized on all exit paths; HMAC long-key path hashes per RFC 2104; ES256 single-hash correct (no double-hash); p256 pubkey/sig parse rejects identity/off-curve/zero-r-s/non-canonical-DER without panic; SHA-1 is consumed ONLY by HMAC-SHA1 (grep-confirmed) — no SHA-1 in any signature/trust decision; no fake-verify (every failure path returns false/Err before releasing plaintext). 104 crypto/auth KATs green. ### Lead-orchestrated autonomous wave (2026-06-21, /goal — UI marquee + hardening + parity)

Green baseline confirmed by athena-verifier at HEAD `544a696` (build exit 0, marker present, 7/7 HEALTHY, 8/8 smoketests, 0 panics; only the standing >6s total-boot WARN red — known open item). Then fanned out across disjoint crates. Landed + committed:

FAIL-able `run_drop_shadow_penumbra_smoketest` renders over the exact blue backdrop the old bug leaked + asserts monotonic/soft/near-black/decays. Verifier: `[compositor] shadow-penumbra ... -> PASS` (skew=2, ramp=52px), glass blur 5/5 unregressed, 7/7 HEALTHY. `+shadow_penumbra:` in `/proc/athena/compositor`.

The FM_*/8x8 `athshell/file_manager.rs` confirmed DEAD → quarantined (rule 7), not re-skinned. `cargo test -p ath_tokens` 12/12, `ftype_proof` FAIL-able.

- **Multi-architecture strategy — spec + Concept clause + ADR (criterion #3, groundwork).** athena-researcher spec (`docs/research/multi-arch-abstraction.md`): no `arch::` boundary exists (kernel is monolithically x86_64 — 385 `x86_64::` refs, bootloader_api is x86-only = hard aarch64 wall). Proposed a monomorphized `arch::` seam (boot/MMU/interrupts/timers/SMP/ctx-switch/syscall/firmware-discovery), x86_64→aarch64→i686 order with per-arch QEMU acceptance lines, and a zero-behavior-change Slice 0 (arch:: skeleton → relocate seam files) → Slice 1 (arch-neutral MM types). Added a north-star "Architecture Reach" clause to `LEGACY_GAMING_CONCEPT.md` + **ADR 0007**. NO `ath_abi` change (user ABI arch-neutral). **Slice 0 (heavy serialized kernel refactor, ≥5-boot verify) deferred to its own focused round**; aarch64 boot/DTB needs a follow-up spec before coding. **TODO phase: Multi-architecture support** — sub-items: [~] Slice 0 arch:: boundary (x86_64 zero-change — Slice 0 landed `5079a90`; Slice 0b relocate-seams pending kernel-lane-clear), [ ] Slice 1 arch-neutral MM, [x] aarch64 boot spec (`docs/research/aarch64-bringup-spec.md` + ADR 0009), [~] aarch64 bring-up (A2-A9 per spec — pure-logic foundation `components/aarch64_logic` host-KAT'd 33/33 `a4c9f5b`; boot slices A2-A9 pending Slice 0b/kernel-lane), [ ] i686 bring-up.

Verify a download's integrity locally. Follow-up: Files "verify checksum" + AthStore `.athpkg` integrity check.

### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 33 — ath_deflate (compression primitive) (2026-06-18, host-KAT-verified [~])

- **`ath_deflate` — DEFLATE compress + inflate + gzip/zlib [~] (compression infra, commit `4807c53`).** New `#![no_std]`/`#![forbid(unsafe_code)]` zero-dep crate: a real DEFLATE compressor (greedy LZ77 32KiB hash-chain match-finder, RFC-1951 fixed-Huffman encoding, stored-block fallback so output never bloats incompressible input) + canonical inflate (stored+fixed+dynamic, so it round-trips real gzip/zlib) + gzip/zlib wrappers (CRC32 + Adler32, known-vector-verified). `inflate(deflate(x))==x` over empty/repetitive/text/random/binary; ratios >50x repetitive, ≤input+16 random. **20 host KATs**, FAIL-able. The inverse of extraction — enables "Compress to .zip/.gz". Follow-up: a zip/gzip container writer in Files (gz ready as `gzip_compress`; zip = local-header+central-dir+EOCD around `deflate()`).

### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 31 — ath_tar (.tar/.tar.gz reader) (2026-06-18, host-KAT-verified [~])

- **`ath_tar` — TAR + gzip reader [~] (daily-driver archives, commit `648c1dd`).** New `#![no_std]`/`#![forbid(unsafe_code)]` zero-dep crate: ustar/POSIX TAR (name+prefix long paths, octal + GNU base-256 sizes, typeflags, GNU `L`/`K` longname, PAX `x`/`g` overrides, signed+unsigned checksum, two-zero-block end) + gzip (RFC 1952 header, self-contained DEFLATE inflate, CRC32 **and** ISIZE verified) → `read_tar`/`read_tar_gz` (auto-detect magic). Hostile-safe (entry/total/ratio bomb caps, `is_safe_path` zip-slip guard). **23 host KATs**, FAIL-able (fuzz-swept). Complements ath_zip — `.tar`/`.tar.gz`/`.tgz` are ubiquitous downloads. ### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 19 — ath_regex (ReDoS-safe NFA engine) (2026-06-18, host-KAT-verified [~])

- **`ath_regex` — never-panic Thompson-NFA regex engine [~] (infra, commit `c1491ca`).** New `#![no_std]`/`#![forbid(unsafe_code)]` crate: recursive-descent parser → Thompson NFA → Pike-VM matcher (parallel-state, generation-deduped epsilon-closure → O(text×program), NO backtracking). Syntax: literals/escapes, `.`, char classes + ranges + negation, `dws`+negations, greedy `* + ? {n,m}`, alternation, capturing + `(?:)` groups, `^$` anchors; captures + `replace_all` with `$1`. **ReDoS-safe** (`(a+)+$` on a 50-char adversarial string returns instantly — the load-bearing guard) + compile-size bounds (`ProgramTooLarge`/`RepetitionTooLarge`). **19 host KATs**, FAIL-able, char-boundary-safe (UTF-8 + emoji). Powers regex find/replace, input validation, search.

### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 13 — mouse-first desktop: cursor ABI + Calculator hit-testing (2026-06-18, QEMU-verified [~])

- **`SYS_INPUT_CURSOR` (279) — absolute cursor position [~] [interface] (commit `7146189`).** athena-architect exposed the compositor's absolute cursor position as a single-register, never-blocking poll (`athkit::sys::cursor_pos() -> (x,y,buttons)`; position packed `x|(y<<16)`, buttons from the existing `poll_mouse`). No Cap (not privileged), ABI_VERSION unchanged (additive #279). FAIL-able `[compositor] cursor_position roundtrip=true lane_isolation=true -> PASS`, boots 7/7. **The cross-cutting unblock for mouse hit-testing across all 10 apps.**
- **Calculator mouse hit-testing [~] (proof-of-pattern, commit `7d84508`).** `apps/calculator` is now fully clickable: click-edge detection (drain `poll_mouse` → up→down edge → read `cursor_pos`, subtract window origin), and a **single `[Element;32]` list (rect+label+action) that both `render` draws and `hit` tests** so draw-rects==hit-rects can't drift. Clicking digits/ops/`=`/sci-functions/bitwise/mode-tabs fires the identical action as the key. Keyboard fully preserved. `design_proof()` asserts every element's rect-center hits itself + out-of-bounds → no-op + a tab-click switches mode + a `"7"`-click updates the display. Boots clean, `[gameos] gamebar -> PASS`. **A documented rollout recipe lets the other 5 apps (Files/Notes/Clock/Photos/Music) become clickable the same way.** Latent follow-up: a "query my window origin" syscall (apps currently assume a fixed present origin — correct while the WM doesn't move windows).

Built the web/PWA/content foundation as guaranteed-disjoint host-KAT'd crates (immune to a brief concurrent-session image red — their GameOS GameBar WIP, since committed+fixed `af7c925`, `[gameos] gamebar smoketest -> PASS` re-confirmed), then PIVOTED to integration once the image was green again.

- **RaeWeb browser surface — P2: a REAL on-screen web view [~] (Concept §3 "renders through AthUI" + §Core Principles #1 "No Electron tax", QEMU-verified).** New `kernel/src/webview.rs` — a kernel-drawn, compositor-presented browser surface (the LIVE `Settings`/`GameOS` surface pattern, NOT a userspace ELF: the `apps/web` build hits the known `poly1305`/`sha2` SIMD-split LLVM error; the kernel's build-std/soft-float config links `athnet` cleanly). Full chain: navigate → `loader::fetch_document` (real `athnet::http1::fetch_with`) → `parse_html`/cascade/layout → `backend::paint_displaylist_to_canvas` → `athgfx::Canvas` → compositor present. Minimal chrome: glass toolbar with back/fwd/reload chips + live-accent address bar (ath_tokens, `draw_text_aa`), scroll, link click→navigate (new engine helper `loader::link_href_at`), bundled page graph (home↔about↔welcome) served over the real fetch path via athnet `MockTransport` (`fetched=bundled`, deterministic), best-effort live `http://` fetch over the kernel smoltcp socket stack (bounded, error-page on net-down — iron live fetch gated on net-RX live fix #2). F7 toggles it from the desktop (modal, mirrors F11/GameOS); resilient (error page, never a panic, on bad HTML/net error). **NO new syscall** (kernel-side render). R10: `webview::init()` + boot smoketest + `/proc/athena/web` (URL + dom_nodes + paint_cmds + source) + Concept docstring. Host KATs: `cargo test -p athweb` **8/8** (incl. new `link_href_at` + a kernel-fetch-path repro that caught the `rae://` vs `http://` wire-form bug). Proof: `[web] browser smoketest: navigated=ok fetched=bundled dom_nodes=145 painted=ok presented=ok link_nav=ok -> PASS`; build exit 0, boots **7/7 HEALTHY**, 0 PANIC. Next: P3 styling depth + the standalone `apps/web` crate with `-Z build-std` flags; P5 = QuickJS/Boa.

- **`ath_pwa` — W3C Web App Manifest parser [~] (PWA pillar, commit `1b67e01`).** New `#![no_std]`/`#![forbid(unsafe_code)]` crate on `ath_json`: typed `WebAppManifest` (name/icons/display-mode/theme+bg color ARGB/scope/start_url), `best_icon`, `to_app_entry()` launch descriptor — the "install a web app to the desktop" foundation. **13 unit + 2 doctests**, never-panic, FAIL-able.

The lingua franca for Notes/docs/chat.
- **Notes app [~] (parity §T daily-driver, commit `4612ea2`).** New `apps/notes` ELF wiring `ath_markdown` into ON-SCREEN rich-text: sidebar note list (`<home>/Notes`), edit buffer + live Markdown preview (headings sized per level, bold/italic/code/list/blockquote/code-block/rule all drawn via `draw_text_aa`/JetBrains-Mono), New/Delete/Save (Ctrl+N/D/S), Tab edit⇄preview, never-panic. ath_tokens chrome + live `SYS_THEME_GET` accent (matches Photos/Music 1:1), `design_proof()` parse→render gate. ### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 7 — accessibility suite completed (magnifier + focus-follows) (2026-06-17, QEMU-verified [~])

The accessibility ship gate (parity §J/§H) is now a coherent, integrated suite — tree → reader → magnifier → focus-follows. Built in disjoint lanes (compositor.rs was clean; a11y.rs is ours) while the concurrent session worked settings/gameos/athweb.

- **Screen magnifier mechanism [~] (parity §J, commit `8b7b2f4`).** `compositor.rs` — `magnifier_set_enabled/zoom(1.0x–8.0x)/center` lock-free atomics; when enabled, the scanout-flush stage source-samples a `(fb/zoom)` window of the already-composited `scanout_ready` buffer (compositor-owned → UAF-safe, runs interrupts-enabled like the existing copy) and nearest-neighbor upscales it to fill the framebuffer; disabled = byte-identical 1:1 (zero normal-path cost), alloc-free, all 3 scanout backends (GpuFb/Virtio/Gop). FAIL-able `[compositor] magnifier smoketest: zoom2x_sampled=true center_ok=true identity_when_off=true edge_clamped=true -> PASS`, `/proc/athena/compositor` magnifier fields, both SMP. The Windows-Magnifier / macOS-Zoom mechanism, real.
- **Focus-follows integration [~] (parity §J, commit `30a577e`).** `a11y.rs` — the focus-change path now pans the magnifier to the focused node's bounds center (`compositor::magnifier_set_center`, guarded off when the magnifier is disabled + degenerate-bounds skip) alongside the existing reader announce, off the single `note_focus_if_changed()` detection. FAIL-able `[a11y] focus-follows smoketest: pan_to_node1=true pan_to_node2=true noop_when_off=true degenerate_skipped=true -> PASS`, magnifier confirmed OFF by default (desktop boots unzoomed), both SMP. **Tree + reader + magnifier now act as one experience.** Deferred (shell_runner concurrent-occupied): the magnifier toggle hotkey — the last leg to let a user enable the magnifier that focus-follows now drives.

### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 6 — web/net foundation + full-integration green checkpoint (2026-06-17, QEMU-verified [~])

Web pillar foundation built host-KAT-first (the full image build was briefly blocked by a concurrent session's GPU compile error — `ath_amdgpu/bringup.rs` E0499, since fixed by their commit `53e48c3`; pure-library work stayed verifiable throughout). Then the whole integrated tree was ratified booting.

- **Native HTTP/1.1 client [~] (web pillar, commit `1a4be7c`).** `components/athnet/src/http1.rs` — request builder + streaming response parser handling Content-Length AND `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` (chunk-ext/trailers), case-insensitive/folded/dup headers, a URL parser, a mockable `HttpTransport` seam, never-panic (network-facing parser = hostile input). **25 http1 KATs** (45 athnet total), FAIL-able. **`Content-Encoding` decoding LANDED 2026-06-22 (/goal):** `decode_content_encoding()` transparently inflates `gzip`/`x-gzip` + `deflate` (zlib-wrapped, raw-DEFLATE fallback) response bodies via the bomb-bounded `ath_deflate` (new athnet dep, no_std — full `xtask build` clean), applied in `send_request`/`fetch` (codings undone in reverse; `parse_response` stays raw); `identity`/absent pass through; `br`/`zstd` → clean `UnsupportedContentEncoding` (never silently-wrong plaintext); corrupt stream → `BadContentEncoding` (never panics). **Without this a real server's gzip'd HTML reached the browser as gzip bytes** — every modern site `Content-Encoding: gzip`s. Host-KAT-proven (`cargo test -p athnet`, 86/86): round-trips our own gzip writer AND decodes **real `gzip -9` CLI output** (cross-impl/real-server compat), deflate/zlib, case-insensitive/`x-gzip`, FAIL-demonstrated (br→error, corrupt gzip→error). Now 40 http1 KATs. Live fetch still iron/DHCP-gated.
- **Live TCP/DNS transport [~] (web pillar, commit `253367a`).** athkit `tcp_connect`/`sock_send`/`sock_recv`/`dns_resolve` wrappers over the EXISTING socket syscalls 121–125 + DNS 264 (no ABI change) + a `RaeSocketTransport` + `http_get(url)` taking `fetch` mock→live. **10 new wiring KATs** (50 athnet total), FAIL-able. Live fetch is network/iron-gated (needs DHCP `Bound` on the RTL8125).
- **WebSocket RFC 6455 handshake de-stubbed [~] (web pillar, /goal 2026-06-22, commit `68f72b6`).** `components/athnet/src/websocket.rs` had a STUB handshake: `compute_accept_key` returned a hardcoded placeholder, `connect()` discarded its own upgrade request, the client never validated the server's `Sec-WebSocket-Accept`, and every client frame was masked with ONE static key (`[0x37,0xfa,0x21,0x3d]` — an RFC 6455 5.3 violation). Now real: `compute_accept_key = base64(SHA1(key + GUID))` via new no_std deps `ath_hash` + `ath_encode`; `connect()` queues a real upgrade request with a freshly-generated `Sec-WebSocket-Key`; new `complete_handshake(response)` fail-closed-validates 101 + Upgrade/Connection + the Accept key; per-frame masking keys from a seedable xorshift PRNG (`set_entropy_seed` for production entropy). **Host-KAT-proven (`cargo test -p athnet` 91/91, +5):** the canonical RFC 6455 1.3 vector (`dGhlIHNhbXBsZSBub25jZQ==` -> `s3pPLMBiTxaQ9kYGzzhZRbK+xOo=`), full client<->server interop, wrong/missing-Accept rejected fail-closed, per-frame key variation, masked round-trip; removes the module's dead-code warnings. Full `xtask build` + QEMU CI clean (7/7 HEALTHY, 0 PANIC). **Now CONNECTABLE end-to-end (commit `2c4f87e`):** new `connect_over<T: http1::HttpTransport>(host, port, url, protocols, transport)` drives the whole handshake over a byte transport (reusing the HTTP client's transport abstraction — DRY): sends the upgrade request, reads the server's HTTP response (bounded 16 KiB so a non-terminating peer can't grow memory), validates it -> Open. Host-KAT'd (108/108 athnet): a full client<->server handshake over a bridging transport goes Open + sends a masked frame; a non-101 fails closed. So the de-stubbed handshake is now a usable client, not just pieces. Live socket connect still network/iron-gated.
- **HTTP/1.1 client matured to daily-driver-usable [~] (web pillar, /goal 2026-06-22, commits `cae82e0`/`ff2d2d4`/`f3fde88`/`4ea9cd2`/`0d8328e`).** The `http1` client gained the three things real `http://` browsing actually needs, all host-KAT-proven + hostile-input-safe: (1) **Content-Encoding** gzip/deflate response decoding via the bomb-bounded `ath_deflate` (decodes real `gzip -9` CLI output; br/zstd -> clean UnsupportedContentEncoding) + **Accept-Encoding** advertised on every fetch so servers actually compress; (2) **redirect following** (`fetch` follows up to 10 `http://` 3xx hops — relative + absolute-URL + absolute-path Location, hop-bounded so no infinite loop, https handed back for the TLS path); (3) **a correct RFC 6265 cookie jar** (`cookies.rs`, new) wired into `fetch_follow_jar` — host-only vs Domain match, the §5.1.4 path boundary the dead `https.rs` scaffolding got wrong (`/foo` !match `/foobar`), Max-Age expiry, secure-withheld-over-http, and the login-flow case (a 302 Set-Cookie is carried to the redirect destination). `cargo test -p athnet` 106/106; bare + full `xtask build` + QEMU CI clean (7/7 HEALTHY). **brotli `br` decode LANDED too (commit `a5d2de3`):** via the battle-tested `brotli-decompressor` v5 behind an OFF-by-default `brotli` feature (kernel/bare build never pulls it — verified brotli ABSENT from the kernel binary); `decode_brotli` decodes REAL `brotli -q 11` CLI output (full RFC 7932 incl. the static dictionary) back to the exact original (host KAT 48/48 with the feature), Accept-Encoding advertises `br` only when the feature is on, off it stays a clean Unsupported. So the client now decodes ALL common HTTP codings (gzip/deflate/br). The remaining web-fetch gap is just `https://` (TLS transport, iron-gated).
- **`ath_json` parser [~] (web/store/config infra, commit `b559025`).** New `#![no_std]` zero-dep crate — never-panic RFC-8259 JSON parse + serialize (full escape/surrogate-pair/number handling without libm, depth-limited for stack-safety). **21 host KATs + 2 doctests**, FAIL-able (31-input malformed battery panic-free). Foundational for web APIs + the AthStore manifest format.
- **FULL-INTEGRATION GREEN CHECKPOINT [~] (commit `86d36c2`).** athena-verifier ratified the entire integrated tree (this session's 15 lead waves + the concurrent session's GPU CP-enable `53e48c3` / procfs-storage `2b52b63` / two-pane Settings `86d36c2`) as ONE booting image: **both SMP=1 and SMP=2, 7/7 HEALTHY, 333-class smoketest tally, 0 PANIC/FAIL**, boot 1431/1500ms within budget. Every integrated smoketest PASSes (a11y tree+reader, capture+cap-gate, overview/snapshot/spaces/switcher, clipboard history+panel, palette, notify, gameos, settings, storage). The host-KAT-only libraries (jpeg/wav/exif/Photos/Music/http1/ath_json) are proven via `cargo test -p <crate>`, correctly not wired into boot. **The cumulative session is a coherent, green, fully-integrated OS image** — `[x]` for all of it remains iron-gated per rule 14 (iron paused this session).

### Lead-orchestrated parity wave 2 — command palette + clipboard-history ABI + PNG decoder (2026-06-17, QEMU/host-KAT-verified [~])

EM standup loop off the parity matrix (iron paused → QEMU/host-KAT work). Baseline first banked GREEN (athena-verifier PASS: 7/7 HEALTHY, 8/8 smoketests, boot 1597ms) in 4 clean commits (`e92d00c`/`05bad07`/`0b026f1`/`28dfd3a`), then two non-overlapping crates built in parallel.

Spec: `docs/design/command-palette.md`.
- **Clipboard-history ABI [~] [interface] (parity gap §E, commit `bbb3276`).** athena-architect landed the history-aware kernel clipboard: syscalls **268–273** (count/get/pin/delete/clear/promote) + additive extension of `108 SET` to append to a 64-entry RAM-only local-only ring with pinned-safe eviction; ABI_VERSION unchanged (additive), no Cap (user's own data, safe-mode-clean). R10 complete — init line, FAIL-able `[clipboard-history] smoketest: copied=3 pinned=1 evict_unpinned=1 pin_survives_clear=1 promote(0)_ok=1 -> PASS`, `/proc/athena/clipboard`, Concept §"user owns the machine" docstring. athkit `clip_hist_*` wrappers ready. **Unblocks the clipboard-history panel** (athena-shell-apps). Spec: `docs/design/clipboard-history.md`.
- **PNG decoder [~] (media foundation, commit `ddc161f`).** `components/athmedia/src/png.rs` — a `#![no_std]` zero-dep PNG decoder (color types 0/2/3/4/6, all 5 scanline filters, from-scratch DEFLATE inflate incl. dynamic Huffman, bounded alloc, never-panics on hostile input) → flat ARGB8888. **22/22 host KATs** (`cargo test -p athmedia`), proven FAIL-able (breaking the Paeth predictor flips the dedicated guard). ### Autonomous /goal session — ath_tokens + compositor leak fix (2026-06-17, QEMU-verified [~])

Charter loop (`docs/AUTONOMY_CHARTER.md`); iron paused → QEMU-verifiable work, UI marquee. Commits `c35e074`/`f197be9`/+; ADRs 0001/0002/0003/0004.
- **`ath_tokens` design-token crate [~] (infra).** New `#![no_std]` zero-dep crate (`components/ath_tokens`) = single source of truth for spacing/radius/type/motion/elevation/palettes + `derive_accent(seed,palette)` + WCAG `contrast_ratio`; re-exported as `athui::tokens`. Ends the ~30-file `const ACCENT` duplication; makes Vibe Mode's one-seed re-skin real (ADR 0003). **6/6 host KATs PASS** (`cargo test -p ath_tokens`). design-language.md §4.3 accent table reconciled to shipped behavior. *Unblocks the desktop-shell re-skin (Phase 8/13/14).*
- **CRITICAL compositor surface-frame leak FIXED [~].** athena-reviewer found `Surface` backing frames (~1.5 MiB/window close) were NEVER freed — `reclaim_task_resources` only dropped the Vec entry, no `Drop for Surface`. Fix: `impl Drop for Surface` + `ExclusiveFullscreen` (free contiguous frames once, order formula mirrors `alloc_contig_frames`, null/zero-guarded); 3 exclusive query fns routed through `lock_compositor()` (IF=0 footgun). New FAIL-able `[compositor] surface-leak smoketest: baseline=479225 after=479225 (created/freed 8) -> PASS` — free-frame count returns exactly to baseline. athena-verifier PASS, R10 + Drop order-formula audited, no new WARN/FAIL/PANIC.
- **Specs banked (docs):** `docs/design/settings.md` (Settings/Control-Center surface — control_panel.rs is already a 2446-line model; re-skin not rebuild). athena-perf boot-time analysis: Tier-7 `usb=2512ms` is `pci::refresh()` re-scanning all 256 ECAM buses (`max_bus=255`, real top 0xC5) — ~2s reducible (queued next).
- **Boot perf RANK 1 — ECAM scan bounded to bridge topology [~] (2026-06-17).** `pci::enumerate_inner` hardcoded `max_bus=255` whenever ECAM was active, so Tier-7 `pci::refresh()` round-tripped all 256 buses over ECAM MMIO; on Athena buses 0xC6..0xFF (~58 × 32 dev) are empty — the bulk of the iron `usb=2512ms`. KEY CORRECTION vs the initial athena-perf premise: **Athena's MCFG declares `buses=0-255`** (verified in every `logs/bootlog-*` `[acpi] MCFG: ... buses=0-255`), so the MCFG `end_bus` is 0xFF and yields NO saving. The real, still-safe ceiling is *topological*: a function can only live inside some PCI-PCI bridge's `[secondary, subordinate]` window, all rooted at bus 0. Fix: `pcie::init` → `derive_and_store_max_bus` does a cheap ECAM bridge-tree BFS from bus 0 (`max_subordinate_bus`, reads bridge subordinate-bus @0x1A), clamps to the MCFG ceiling, stores into `PCIE_ECAM_MAX_BUS`; `enumerate_inner` scans `0..=ecam_max_bus()` in ECAM mode (legacy 0..=8 unchanged). Added `parse_mcfg_end_bus` (returns the firmware hard ceiling). SAFETY: guards against a bogus/too-small bound by comparing to `pci::highest_bus_seen()` (Tier-1 high-water mark) → fall back to 255 + WARN, never under-scans. Logs: `[pci] Enumerating devices (ecam, max_bus=0xC5)..`, `[pcie] ECAM scan bound: max_bus=0xC5 (source: bridge subordinate, mcfg_end=0xFF, tier1-seen 0x08)`; `pcie` smoketest asserts `bound >= highest_bus_seen` (FAIL-able); `/proc/athena/pcie` exposes `scan_max_bus`/`highest_bus_seen`; `[tier1-prof]` split `pci+fb`→`pci`+`fb`. QEMU: device count IDENTICAL (flat bus 0 → no bridges → bound stays at MCFG ceiling, full coverage); the ~2s saving is iron-only (compare iron `[tier7-prof] usb=` before/after). Build/boot verification by lead.
- **Live taskbar/Start/tray re-skin [~] (commit `f197be9`).** `athshell::DesktopShell` (the on-screen shell; `desktop.rs` is dead code) — 16 hardcoded consts → `ath_tokens`; taskbar 36→44px mica, `radius_pill` Start, accent running-indicators, 560×640 glass Start menu, 32px tray. QEMU: `[shell] taskbar: h=44 mica=0xFF0E121F accent=0xFF4E9CFF (radius pill+xs) -> PASS`; 4/4 host KATs.
- **Window chrome + toast re-skin [~] (2026-06-17).** Fixed the `window_chrome::draw_char` NOISE defect (rendered `(row+col+glyph)%3` speckle) → real `Canvas::draw_glyph` (font8x8) — titles are readable. Titlebar 28→32px mica + macOS traffic-light controls (left, state_danger/warn/ok); `notify.rs` toasts → `material.glass` tint + token urgency bars + `RADIUS_MD`/`ELEV_2`. kernel→`ath_tokens` dep added. - **Settings/Control-Center re-skin [~] (2026-06-17).** `control_panel.rs` (2446-line model) — all 11 `CP_*` consts → `ath_tokens`; two-pane layout, full token-driven control-kit states (Toggle/Slider/Dropdown/RadioGroup/Button/TextInput/ColorPicker/etc. with default/hover/active/selected/disabled/focus-ring — high fan-out, reused by every app), `RADIUS_LG` group cards, and the **Appearance & Vibe showcase** (6-chip `derive_accent` ramp preview + Vibe grid sized to the LIVE 12-preset count). IA 10-category regroup deferred (routing risk). **Whole-shell cohesion now proven end-to-end: one accent `0xFF4E9CFF` + one mica `0xFF0E121F` across taskbar + chrome + toasts + Settings.**
- **Force-kill resource leak FIXED [~] (HIGH, 2026-06-17).** athena-reviewer found `kill_task` (force-kill, non-current branches) leaked the task's sockets/ports + sandbox entry — `exit_current_task` cleaned them but the kill path only called `reclaim_task_resources` (surfaces/buckets/event_bus). The "app misbehaves → kill it" case grew `SOCKET_TABLE`/sandbox unboundedly. Fix: folded `sandbox::forget_task` + `net::cleanup_task_sockets` + `ipc cleanup_task_channels` INTO `reclaim_task_resources` (single source of truth; all 3 verified self-contained, reusing the already-proven `SCHEDULER → {SANDBOX,SOCKET,NET_STACK,IPC}` IF=0 order) and removed the now-duplicate inline calls from `exit_current_task` — both paths now reclaim identically. New FAIL-able `[sched] kill-reclaim smoketest: sockets baseline=0 after=0 sandbox baseline=0 after=0 -> PASS` (plants a sandbox entry + UDP socket for a synthetic pid, reclaims, asserts cleared).
- **Dead VirtioNetDriver removed [x] (rule 7, 2026-06-17).** ~570 lines of never-constructed software-ring twin removed from `net_drivers.rs` (grep-verified zero live refs); `QUARANTINED_MODULES.md` row added; live NICs (lo/RtlDriver/E1000/igc) untouched. Capability-per-kLOC win.
- **Live accent wiring — Vibe Mode one-tap re-skin REAL [~] (2026-06-17, the marquee payoff).** Every surface previously hardcoded the RAEBLUE seed; now `theme_engine::active_accent()` is the single live source (current ThemeAbi.accent_argb, override-able), pushed to userspace via `athshell::set_active_accent()` (AtomicU32) on desktop activation AND every `theme_engine::apply()` / Vibe `apply_preset` / colour-set. `window_chrome`/`notify`/`athshell` taskbar/`control_panel` all derive from it. No `ath_abi`/syscall change. **Dynamic-cohesion proof (the Concept §6 test made real + FAIL-able):** `[theme] accent-cohesion: default=0xFF4E9CFF -> set 0xFFFF8800 -> all{chrome,notify,taskbar,settings}=0xFFFF8800 -> restored=0xFF4E9CFF -> PASS` — one accent change re-skins every surface together, then reverts. This is the literal mechanism behind "the desktop becomes a different place in one tap." Next: wire the Settings colour-picker control to `set_active_accent` (the user-facing entry to the same proven path).
- **OOBE/login/widgets tokenized [~] (2026-06-17).** The first screens users see now read the live accent + token palette like the rest of the OS. `login_ui.rs` (full migration — top bar/underline/avatar/footer track the accent), `setup_ui.rs` (OOBE — COLORS ONLY: accent + focus-ring + radius tokenized, the iron-verified light-glass card/gradient/blobs preserved verbatim per [[ui-glass-design-system]]), `widgets.rs` (shared kit — high fan-out).
