## Phase 6 — AthGFX → Vulkan demo (Year-1 deliverable)

The Concept §Year-1 milestone: "Boots, draws, plays a single Vulkan demo."

### 6.1 Kernel-side foundation

- [x] Userspace login screen renders at boot (supersedes boot triangle demo)
- [x] Compositor blits userspace surfaces
- [x] `SYS_SURFACE_CREATE/PRESENT/FOCUS/CLOSE`
- [x] Contiguous frame allocation for surfaces (Buddy Allocator integration)
- [x] virtio-gpu 2D driver (CPU→GPU on-ramp) — `kernel/src/virtio_gpu.rs`: in-kernel **modern virtio-pci** transport (PCI-capability walk → `COMMON_CFG`/`NOTIFY_CFG` BARs mapped via `map_mmio_region`, `VIRTIO_F_VERSION_1` negotiation, controlq desc/avail/used programmed into common-cfg, MMIO doorbell). Drives the full GPU present sequence — `GET_DISPLAY_INFO → RESOURCE_CREATE_2D → RESOURCE_ATTACH_BACKING → SET_SCANOUT → TRANSFER_TO_HOST_2D → RESOURCE_FLUSH` — the device-side equivalent of "VRAM → scanout → flip" with the CPU out of the copy path. INTx disabled + `VIRTQ_AVAIL_F_NO_INTERRUPT` (we poll). QEMU proof: `[vgpu] virtio-gpu up (modern): 1af4:1050 qsize=64 notify_mul=4`, `[vgpu] smoketest: display_info=true (1280x800) present_path_ok=true cmds_ok=5 -> PASS`; `/proc/athena/virtio_gpu`. **Compositor scanout seam landed (2026-06-15):** `compositor.rs` now dispatches presentation through an enum-`ScanoutBackend { GpuFb, VirtioGpu, Gop }` (no per-frame vtable/alloc) instead of the inline `gpu_fb`-vs-GOP `if`. `gpu_fb` (Bochs/iron linear scanout) is resolved dynamically every frame (behavior-preserving); the live virtio backend is upgraded lazily on first composite (compositor::init runs before virtio_gpu::init) and presents via new additive `virtio_gpu::{is_available, present_init, present_frame}` — a persistent full-screen B8G8R8A8 resource (distinct from the 256×64 `present_smoketest`): per frame it copies `comp_buf` into the backing (ARGB u32 == B8G8R8A8 LE, direct copy) → TRANSFER_TO_HOST_2D → RESOURCE_FLUSH. GOP is the fallback. QEMU build+boot clean, 0 PANIC, behavior-preserving (selects Gop, no display regression). **The same `match` arm is the drop-in slot for the native AMD page-flip scanout** (the native-driver path). NOT yet exercised: virtio is only *selected* on the first real composite (headless CI paints no frame before the marker), so virtio-present runs on an iron desktop or a non-headless QEMU run.
- [ ] virtio-gpu 3D commands implemented in QEMU path
- [ ] virtio-gpu resource sharing with userspace via shared memory or capability
- [~] AMDGPU DRM-equivalent driver hosted in userspace driver framework — `amdgpud/` daemon in initramfs; spawned (+waited) FIRST from `user_init` (sentinels 7600–7602). **Firmware loading now wired**: `firmware_preflight()` + per-stage `load_fw()` (PSP/SMU/GFX) call `request_firmware` (syscall 142); QEMU verified: `[amdgpu] firmware 'athena-selftest.bin' loaded (334 bytes)`, `firmware preflight: loader=ok amdgpu_blobs=0/9 present`, then `msg: 9099` (no Radeon on QEMU). **Signed Phoenix blobs LANDED (2026-06-12): all 12 real blobs + `LICENSE.amdgpu` fetched from linux-firmware into `firmware/amdgpu/` (sizes plausible, AMD ucode header first-dword == file size verified on toc/mec). The FW manifest had a latent bug — `smu_13_0_4.bin` does NOT exist in linux-firmware (APU PMFW ships in the system BIOS, loaded by the PSP bootloader) and `gc_11_0_1_imu.bin` (required for GFX11 APU bring-up) was missing — `FW_PHOENIX`/stage 5/stage 6 corrected (smu→imu), so preflight would have sat at 11/12 forever. Firmware choice validated against the physical GPU from Windows on Athena itself: `VEN_1002 DEV_15BF REV_C3` = Phoenix1 → GC 11.0.1 / PSP 13.0.4 / SDMA 6.0.1 / DCN 3.1.4 / VCN 4.0.2. PENDING (dev box — this session ran on the toolchain-less Athena box): `cargo test -p ath_amdgpu`, full build (`Firmware blobs bundled: N` should jump by 13), QEMU CI expect `amdgpu_blobs=12/12 present` + sentinel `9062`; then flash.** **VBIOS source SOLVED for the APU (2026-06-12, same session): Athena's GPU has no expansion ROM — the VBIOS comes from the ACPI VFCT table; the real image (16896 B, `ATOM` @ 0x194, 1002:15bf) was extracted from the captured `firmware/acpi/.../VFCT.dat` and vendored at `firmware/vbios/1002-15bf.bin`; `atombios::parse_vfct` (pure, bounds-checked, 4 synthetic KATs + a real-table KAT asserting byte-identity with the vendored blob) + `read_vbios` fallback via new `GpuOps::request_firmware_bytes` (default `None`, only amdgpud overrides). Stage 2 on iron should now log `ATOMBIOS OK: hdr@0x194` — also dev-box-pending.** Athena remaining: real BAR0/BAR5 + register-level PSP/SMU mailbox. LinuxKPI Phase 2–4 host + `ath_drm` KMS island ready. See `docs/LINUXKPI_PHASE2.md` **M1 IRON RESULT (2026-07-06, `docs/gpu-oracle/M1-VERDICT-20260706.md`): the REAL upstream amdgpu C (Strategy B, `ATHENA_AMDGPU_REAL=1`) runs on Athena and gets FAR past the native-Rust MES `0x7654` halt — firmware 12/12, IP discovery 39 blocks parsed, SMU responsive (`GetSmuVersion->Some(1)`), enters `amdgpu_device_init`, walks IP register-base setup — then WEDGES at CLKA (clock v13.0.3) instance #2 register-base enumeration (netlog sentinels 9000/9001/9002 fired, 9003 did NOT; `System successfully booted` present = OS healthy, only the daemon's C init hung). Never reaches MES this run. Primary hypothesis: the linuxkpi C `%lx` vararg-print facade faults on the #2 base-address print (the documented "C vararg printf formatter" gap), not hardware. Diagnostic infra `62ffb18`: `SYS_NETLOG_FLUSH` (296) + per-phase `flush_marker` fences + listener abs-path fix. Next (M1.1): fence INSIDE the discovery reg-base loop / route that print through Rust klog → one boot disambiguates printf-facade vs discovery-parse-OOB.** **M1.1 OFF-TARGET ROOT-CAUSE (2026-07-08, `tools/amdgpu_hostrun` — new): built a Linux-host RUNNER for the real C init (ath_linuxkpi `hostrun` feature: functional mmap/file/stderr syscall seam; links the m4c HOST object graph; the aml_probe of amdgpu). Findings: (1) **CLKA #2 EXONERATED** — the identical walk with the identical pristine blob + printf facade completes all 39 IPs on host (#2 prints `0x00017000/0x02402000` fine); the iron netlog merely *ended* there (last lucky broadcast). (2) **Implicit-declaration pointer-truncation class found+fixed**: TUs calling prototype-less functions made gcc assume `int f()` → `call ioremap; cltq` sign-extended the returned pointer — `adev->rmmio` corrupted (verified in the SHIPPED object; ~170 implicit fns audited, all pointer/64-bit returners now prototyped via force-included `linuxkpi-drm/include/linux/rae_implicit_fence.h` + TTM gets `-include linux/highmem.h`; cltq verified GONE). (3) **NULL `pdev->bus` deref fixed** — `amdgpu_acpi_vfct_bios` matches the VFCT VBIOS image against `pdev->bus->number` (=0xc4) which bringup_entry never allocated: on host a clean SIGSEGV *right after discovery* = prime iron-wedge candidate; fix = new supervisor op `SUP_DEVICE_BDF` (kernel handle→BDF query, non-ABI) + bringup_entry allocates the pci_bus + amdgpud passes the claimed BDF. (4) **Inert-weak-stub value bugs fixed**: `atomic_long_set` (stores silently dropped), `bitmap_read`/`bitmap_write` (amdgpu_utils caps) — real impls + FAIL-able host KATs. (5) `firmware_request_nowarn` was a hardcoded -ENOENT stub → wired to the live loader. Host run now: entry → discovery (39 IPs) → **VBIOS from VFCT (`ATOM BIOS: 113-PHXGENERIC-001`, = oracle)** → atombios → GPU post → gmc mc_init, returns -22 cleanly (fake BAR reads RCC_CONFIG_MEMSIZE=0 — next hostrun lever: oracle register model). Verified: 54+1 shim KATs, full build exit 0, `real_amdgpu_init` freestanding build green. **QEMU-gate blocker ROOT-CAUSED + FIXED (2026-07-08, same day): the "clean-HEAD boot panic" was a LATENT interrupt-stub bug, not a regression — the #GP/#PF naked stubs did `pop rdi` (error code → arg1) BEFORE saving rdi, so every RESUMING fault (armed-MSR #GP recovery, extable/uaccess #PF fixups) restored rdi = ERROR CODE into the interrupted context. QEMU 11's qemu64 (KVM injects #GP for feature-gated MSRs regardless of ignore_msrs) made `rdmsr_safe(SPEC_CTRL/ARCH_CAPABILITIES)` resume with rdi=0 exactly where the compiler kept `current_cpu_security_descriptor`'s sret pointer in rdi → NULL store → boot task killed → "no next task". Proven with QEMU gdbstub (rdi valid at fn entry, 0 at the fault). Fix: all four error-code stubs (gpf/page_fault/ssf/snp) save ALL GPRs first, load the error code from its stack slot, `add rsp,8` before iretq. Verified: the previously-deterministic panic config boots — KVM SMP=1 ×5 green + TCG green (rule 17); `-cpu host` still green. SMP=2 AP-bringup stall on this box is SEPARATE + pre-existing (task filed). The `ATHENA_AMDGPU_REAL=1` image then boots GREEN in KVM: 12/12 firmware, sentinels 9000→9062→9099 (clean no-Radeon self-skip), 0 panics.** Next: the REAL-GPU run — host reboot into the vfio-blacklist entry + `~/athena-vm/run-vfio.sh` (or bare iron) — expectation: real init passes discovery+VBIOS (wedge candidates fixed) and reaches PSP/SMU/MES with REAL registers.**
- [~] Intel i915-equivalent driver hosted similarly — `i915d/` daemon source + LinuxKPI `self_test_intel_gpu()` in `hello_linuxkpi` (9200/9299); **i915d ELF integration DONE (2026-06-10, Opus)**: workspace member (root `Cargo.toml`), `config/base.toml` package, initramfs pack verified (`tar -tf` lists `i915d`, osabi 0xAE), spawned + reaped from `user_init` BEFORE amdgpud (sentinels 7700/7701+pid/7735+code/7790; daemon's own 9200/9290/9299 prints unchanged). Build green, QEMU boots clean with it bundled. Remaining for `[x]`-grade QEMU proof: the 9200→9299 serial pair — currently blocked by the native-ELF spawn frame-collision bug (Phase 0 Latent kernel bugs): user_init #UDs before reaching the i915d spawn. On Intel iron it then needs the real VBT/GGTT path.
- [ ] Direct scanout from GPU buffer (skip CPU blit) for exclusive fullscreen

### 6.2 AthGFX userspace API

- [~] Component compiles with wgpu-types gated on `gpu_userspace` feature
- [~] Public Vulkan-equivalent API surface defined (textures, buffers, pipelines, command buffers) — `components/athgfx/src/vulkan.rs` ships `vk_*` types + create/destroy for instance, device, buffers, images, pipelines, swapchain, etc.; verified in `athgfx::run_boot_smoketest` 2026-06-03
- [ ] wgpu backend wired and tested on virtio-gpu
- [~] WGSL → SPIR-V shader toolchain: author AthGFX/effect shaders in WGSL, naga-compile to SPIR-V for the submit path (feeds 6.3's SPIR-V load). Concept §Language Stack — extended. **Landed 2026-06-22 (/goal): `components/athgfx/src/wgsl.rs` under a new lightweight `wgsl` feature (naga `wgsl-in`+`spv-out` ONLY — NOT the heavy wgpu stack, so userspace AthGFX/AthUI compile effect shaders without the full renderer; kernel build leaves it off, bare-metal `x86_64-unknown-none` athgfx + full `xtask build` both exit 0, naga absent from the kernel binary).** `compile_wgsl(source, entry, stage) -> Result<Vec<u32>, WgslError>` (parse→validate→entry-check→emit, typed error never panics) + `compile_wgsl_bytes` (LE blob for `vkCreateShaderModule`) + `compile_effect_shaders()` batch. Six real effect shaders authored in WGSL (`athgfx/shaders/`): `fullscreen.wgsl` (shared fullscreen-triangle VS), `glass.wgsl` (glassmorphism frosted-backdrop FS — the UI signature), `vibe_tint.wgsl` (Vibe Mode procedural background FS), `blur.wgsl` (separable Gaussian FS), `drop_shadow.wgsl` (soft elevation-shadow FS), `live_wallpaper.wgsl` (animated-aurora FS). **Host-KAT-proven (`cargo test -p athgfx --features wgsl`, 11/11):** each shader compiles → correct SPIR-V magic/bound → round-trips through the crate's OWN `SpirVModule::parse` at the right execution model (emitter + the parser the submit path uses agree) → **validates under `spirv-val` 1.4.341.1, the authoritative oracle (forced green with `RAEEN_SPIRV_VAL=1`)**. FAIL-demonstrated: garbage WGSL→Err(parse), wrong entry→Err(entry), wrong stage→Err, and a hand-corrupted SPIR-V word is REJECTED by spirv-val (proves the oracle gate is real). **Reflection landed too (`reflect_wgsl()` -> `ShaderReflection`):** extracts the module's entry points + every `@group(g)@binding(b)` resource with its `BindingKind` (UniformBuffer/StorageBuffer/Texture/Sampler), sorted — so the 6.3 submit path can build the matching `vkPipelineLayout`/descriptor-set layout without re-parsing (host-KAT'd: `glass.fs` -> texture@(0,0)+sampler@(0,1)+uniform@(0,2); fullscreen VS -> 0 bindings). `[~]` not `[x]`: CPU-side compile+reflect is proven now, but uploading the SPIR-V to a live `vkCreateShaderModule`/submit pipeline is still GPU-gated (Phase 6.3) and iron proof is paused.
- [~] Hello-triangle visible on boot path — `user_init` Session 6 (`user_init/src/main.rs`): R/G/B gradient triangle + 12-frame color-wheel animation → `sys_surface_present`; serial sentinels `6000`–`6900`. Same visual as canonical Vulkan hello-world; implementation is software barycentric raster, not `vkQueueSubmit`

### 6.3 Vulkan triangle on screen (GPU path)

QEMU proof 2026-06-11: `[ OK ] compositor effects selftest: 5/5 checks passed (HDR tone-map pipeline + box blur)` — alpha preserved, gray stays gray, black→black, monotone luminance ramp. Real 10/12-bit scanout to an HDR display pending hardware. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `compositor effects selftest: 5/5 checks passed (HDR tone-map pipeline + box blur)` on the Beelink.
- [x] VRR pacing (compositor honors monitor's variable refresh range) — BUILT: `FramePacer::optimal_present_us` clamps the predicted frame interval to `[1e6/max_hz, 1e6/min_hz]` so the pacer never drives the panel faster than `max_hz` or slower than `min_hz` (out of the VRR window). FAIL-able boot proof `compositor::run_vrr_pacing_smoketest` over a 48–144 Hz range: `[compositor] vrr-pacing: clamp_fast=true(>=6944us) clamp_slow=true(<=20833us) in_range=true -> PASS` (too-fast 1ms cadence clamps up to the 144Hz floor, too-slow 50ms clamps down to the 48Hz ceiling, in-range 10ms passes through). QEMU-proven 2026-06-25; live VRR on a real adaptive-sync panel is iron/EDID-gated. **Real-Athena (KVM `-cpu host`, Zen4) PROOF 2026-06-25** — see IRON VERIFICATION block.
- [x] Glassmorphism (blur + transparency) — the 3-pass box-blur kernel (`BlurEngine::box_blur_3pass`) behind glassmorphic surfaces is proven by `compositor::run_effects_smoketest` (a single bright pixel dims and bleeds into its neighbour). Live compositing of blur regions onto real surfaces exercised via `set_surface_blur`. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** same 5/5 iron proof (blur kernel spread verified on real silicon).
- [x] Drop shadows — BUILT: `render_drop_shadow` composites a soft penumbra under windows (used live in `recomposite`), proven by a FAIL-able boot smoketest `compositor::run_drop_shadow_penumbra_smoketest`: `[compositor] shadow-penumbra monotonic=true soft=true(ramp=52px) near_black=true(skew=2) decays=true(peak=27) -> PASS` (asserts the alpha ramp is monotonic, soft/wide, untinted, and decays to wallpaper — a hard block would FAIL). QEMU-proven 2026-06-25; iron-eligible (rides the same `compositor::run_boot_smoketest` that runs on the Beelink). **Real-Athena (KVM `-cpu host`, Zen4) PROOF 2026-06-25** — see IRON VERIFICATION block.
- [ ] Color management (display ICC profile honored)

### 6.5 Year-1 acceptance

Phase 6 is GREEN when:
- [~] User-visible hello triangle on screen (screenshot-capable) — **done on QEMU** via `user_init` Session 6 + AthGFX software rasterizer; caption `Year-1 demo: software-rasterized triangle`. Not yet **hardware Vulkan** (`vk_*` submit + SPIR-V on GPU); reserve `[x]` for Athena + real GPU path or explicit `vkQueueSubmit` demo

## Phase 7 — Audio

Concept §AthAudio: low-latency, sub-3ms round-trip, VoiceMeeter-class routing.

### 7.1 Hardware

- [~] HDA full init on Athena — **partial on iron (2026-06-11T23:31):** `[audio] test-tone smoketest: wrote_samples=960 hda_playback=1 -> PASS` — codec discovered and a PCM stream ran on the real HDA controller; the FULL codec walk (all widgets/pins, §7.2 items) + audible confirmation remain.
- [x] Codec discovery + widget walk — `kernel/src/audio.rs`: `HdaController::discover_codec` + function-group widget tree walk (`HdaCodec`/`HdaNode`, DAC/ADC/pin classification). **Now QEMU-proven 2026-06-12** — xtask adds `intel-hda` + `hda-output` codec, so the FULL CORB/RIRB verb walk runs under QEMU, not just iron: `[audio] codec-walk smoketest: codecs=1 widgets=2 dac=true output_pin=true stream_armed=true -> PASS`. **Found + fixed TWO real driver bugs the iron boot would have hit identically:** (1) RIRBSTS.RINTFL (W1C) was never acked, and (2) RIRBCTL.IRQ_EN was not set — with RINTCNT=1 the controller freezes CORB processing after the FIRST verb until a *set+acked* response interrupt, so the codec walk wedged at `RIRB response timeout` after NID 0. Both fixed; verb diagnostics added on the timeout path for iron. Athena re-confirm pending next flash.
- [~] PCM playback 48 kHz stereo — `audio.rs`: `AudioStreamFormat::DVD_QUALITY` (48k/16/2), BDL stream setup (`HdaStream`/`HdaBdlEntry`), `to_hda_format_register`. Code path complete; needs codec on iron.
- [~] PCM capture — audio.rs: capture ring + mmio_read_capture_pcm(); Athena pending
- [~] USB Audio Class playback + capture — `kernel/src/usb_audio.rs` (NEW 2026-06-10): UAC1/UAC2 config-descriptor parser (AC header/terminals + AS format-type-I PCM + isoch endpoints), `UacDevice`/`UacStream`/`UacFormat`, `best_match` format selection, defensive bounds-checked parse (hostile device can't panic the kernel). init-wired + `/proc/athena/usb_audio`. QEMU proof: `[usb-audio] run_boot_smoketest: uac1=true playback=true fmt48k_stereo=true isoch_ep=true -> PASS`. Live isoch transfer over xHCI wired when a real UAC DAC enumerates.
- [ ] Bluetooth A2DP playback (after BT stack)

### 7.2 AthAudio engine

- [~] In-kernel audio mixer (priority over background apps in game mode) — in-component logic verified in `athaudio::run_boot_smoketest` 2026-06-03; multi-channel up/down-mixing and `SCHED_BODY` priority via `SYS_NULL_LATENCY_ENTER` implemented.
- [~] Per-app volume + EQ — implemented in `athaudio` `EffectsChain` 2026-06-03
- [~] Routing matrix (input → effects → output) — VoiceMeeter-class `AudioRouter` verified 2026-06-03
- [~] Loopback monitoring — `audio.rs`: output-mix loopback ring (`loopback` feed + read, `use_loopback`/`loopback_read_pos`); QEMU-exercisable, artifact validation on iron.
- [~] Latency measurement harness reports sub-3ms on certified hardware — `audio.rs`: `HdaStream::latency_us()` computes ring depth → microseconds; harness exists, the sub-3ms *number* is an Athena measurement.

### 7.3 Phase 7 acceptance

- [ ] Plays a sine tone on Athena
- [~] Records from built-in mic — mic-detection logic BUILT + **validated against REAL hardware 2026-06-28** (`components/athaudio/src/hda_pin.rs` `PinConfig::decode`: decodes the HDA pin configuration-default dword — connectivity (jack/fixed/none), location (external/internal), device class, connection type — with `is_mic`/`is_input`/`is_connected`/`is_external`; the host-KAT-able extraction of the inline check in `kernel/src/audio.rs`). 2 FAIL-able KATs (`cargo test -p athaudio`) including one keyed to the **live Realtek ALC269VC read off the Athena over SSH** (`/proc/asound`: mic pin node 0x18 default `0x04a19020` → MicIn / External-Right / Jack) + input/output/unused classification + a Fixed built-in-mic case. `[~]` not `[x]`: the mic on this box is the external jack (it has no built-in mic), and the remaining work is the live capture path — route the mic pin → ADC (nodes 0x08/0x09), start the input PCM stream, and read samples; the detection that finds the pin is real-codec-grounded. (L1376 round-trip latency rides the same capture path.)
- [ ] Reports round-trip latency
- [~] Two apps mix without artifacts — `audio.rs`: `AudioMixer::mix_streams` sums per-app channels with per-app volume/balance/mute + master gain into the 10ms mix buffer; QEMU-provable, artifact-free validation on iron.

Remaining: a thin `athkit bundle` CLI front-end over `athpkg::Manifest::pack`.

QEMU proof: `[bundle] smoketest: parse+verify ok=1/bad=1 happy=true reject(trunc=true magic=true ver=true large=true short=true utf8=true) -> PASS`. KAT proves the button is declared in the tree (`find_button_action == 1`) and the click invokes the handler. The "fires syscall" leg is the only remainder: host-side athkit deliberately issues no syscalls, so the live handler→`athkit::syscalls` call is exercised when the app runs in the windowed shell (compositor surface + input — the same path the bundled apps use).

## Phase 9 — AthGuard (full security model)

Concept §Security model: "iOS-grade security without iOS-grade lockdown."

### 9.1 Foundations already in place

- [x] Capability syscalls (cap_grant, cap_revoke, cap_check)
- [x] Cap enum 14 variants
- [x] `/proc/athena/caps`

### 9.2 What's needed

- [x] Sandbox enforcement at the syscall edge (**device/network/install classes — NOT yet every syscall; see `docs/THREAT_MODEL.md` §5**) — `kernel/src/sandbox.rs` gates `syscall_handler_inner` for BOTH ABIs via AthGuard's `PolicyEnforcer`; per-task `SandboxLevel` (Trusted/AppSandbox/Strict), side-table with fast-path atomic so Trusted (default) tasks are unaffected. **Gated classes today:** device claim/DMA/PCI (109/111/113/117/132), net sockets (native 121/122 + Linux 41-45/49/50), install (256/257). The ~170 other syscalls (file I/O, IPC, mmap, sched, compositor) are NOT gated at this edge — those paths rely on capabilities + memory isolation, not this gate. **Linux-ABI gate fix (2026-06-10):** the Linux dispatch used to `return` before the sandbox check, so every sandboxed Linux binary bypassed AthGuard entirely; the gate now runs before ABI dispatch via `check_linux_syscall`. `/proc/athena/sandbox` + boot proof: `[sandbox] run_boot_smoketest: strict_deny=true trusted_allow=true benign_allow=true linux_gate=true app_classify=true -> PASS` + live `[sandbox] DENY pid=… syscall=… abi=… level=Strict`. Spawn-path level assignment from app manifests (see next item); per-pid `Grants` relax individual classes at AppSandbox (`grant_allows`). NEXT for the "every syscall" goal: add file/IPC/mmap classes for Strict tasks. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `[sandbox] strict_deny=true trusted_allow=true benign_allow=true linux_gate=true app_classify=true -> PASS` on iron.
- [x] App permission manifests in `RaeManifest.toml` per app bundle — `kernel/src/rae_manifest.rs` (2026-06-10): minimal no_std TOML-subset parser (comments, `[section]`, `key = "string"|true|false`; unknown keys/sections ignored for forward-compat, malformed input fails closed to the allowlist). Schema: `name`/`version`/`sandbox = "trusted"|"app"|"strict"` + `[permissions] network/devices/install` mapping 1:1 to the gated syscall classes. Bundles ship as `apps/<name>/RaeManifest.toml` in the initramfs (xtask bundles them; calculator=app+network, hello_window=strict, terminal=trusted). Spawn path (`shell_runner::spawn_app_from_vfs`) now assigns level+grants via `rae_manifest::assign_for_spawn`, falling back to the first-party allowlist when no valid manifest exists. **Trust rules until code signing:** non-first-party `sandbox="trusted"` is capped to AppSandbox (logged + counted); Strict never receives grants; manifest `name` must match the bundle dir (spoof guard). QEMU proof: `[ OK ] RaeManifest registry: 3 app manifest(s) in boot media`, `[manifest] run_boot_smoketest: found=true parsed=true trust_cap=true reject_garbage=true spawn_gate=true -> PASS` (spawn_gate = live syscall-gate check: manifest-granted network syscall allowed while device claim denied on the same pid), `/proc/athena/manifests` lists all bundles with levels+grants. Remaining for `[x]`: manifests for the rest of the first-party apps, AthFS-installed bundle lookup (post-initramfs), Athena. (Signing as the trust root landed same day — see "Code signing" below.) **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `[manifest] found=true parsed=true signed=true trust_cap=true reject_garbage=true reject_tamper=true spawn_gate=true -> PASS` on iron.
- [x] Runtime permission prompts via compositor UI — the consumer now exists (2026-06-12): `perm_ui.rs` renders a modal compositor dialog (login_ui visual language; kernel surface, never app-drawn — unspoofable) showing WHO requests WHAT; keyboard verdict ([Y]/Enter allow, [N]/Esc deny) routes through `perm_prompt::resolve` — the call that performs the real cap grant. Wired event-driven: `request_permission` kicks `pump()` (no polling), and `shell_runner::handle_key` gives the dialog modal keyboard ownership (keystrokes can't leak to the requesting app). QEMU proof: `[perm-ui] smoketest: dialog_opened=true key_consumed=true approved_with_grant=true dialog_closed=true deny_path=true -> PASS` + live `[perm-ui] dialog open:`/`user ALLOWED` lines. `/proc/athena/perm_ui`. Remaining: a requester syscall for userspace apps (perm_syscalls today covers the trusted-shell list/respond side; in-kernel subsystems call `request_permission` directly), mouse hit-testing on the buttons, iron.
- [x] Code signing for app store apps — end-to-end Ed25519 bundle signing landed 2026-06-10. Build side (xtask): generates/keeps a DEV keypair in `keys/` (committed on purpose — "free signing" dev trust root, see `keys/README.md`; production HSM/store chain replaces it), stages each `RaeManifest.toml` with the built ELF's `elf_sha256` injected, signs the staged bytes (`ed25519-dalek`), bundles detached `RaeManifest.sig`. Kernel side (`rae_manifest::lookup`): embeds `keys/dev-signing.pub`, verifies the signature with the KAT-proven in-kernel Ed25519 (`crypto.rs`), then verifies the ELF hash against the binary in the bundle — sig→manifest→ELF chain. Fail-close: BAD signature / hash mismatch / signed-without-hash rejects the whole bundle (tampered ≠ unsigned); absent `.sig` = unverified-developer posture. A **verified** signature is a sufficient trust root for `sandbox="trusted"` (no allowlist needed). QEMU proof: `[manifest] run_boot_smoketest: found=true parsed=true signed=true trust_cap=true signed_trust=true reject_garbage=true reject_tamper=true spawn_gate=true -> PASS`; `/proc/athena/manifests` shows `signed=true` for all 3 bundles. Remaining for `[x]`: real store/developer PKI (per-dev certs, revocation), key rotation, Athena. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `[bundle] smoketest: parse+verify ok=1/bad=1 happy=true reject(trunc/magic/ver/large/short/utf8)=all-true -> PASS` + Ed25519 KAT on iron.
- [~] "Unverified developer" sideload UX (clear warning, not punitive block) — kernel side of the posture exists (unsigned bundle ⇒ `verified=false`, trusted-cap + grants still honored at AppSandbox, logged — runs, not blocked); the compositor warning UI is the open part
- [x] Secure boot chain end-to-end: bootloader → kernel → init → compositor verified — **the verify + measure halves are built + real-Ryzen proven (2026-06-25).** Bootloader→kernel: `kernel::secure_boot` verifies the Ed25519-signed boot manifest (`[secboot] trust-anchor verify ... -> PASS`, pubkey-only — no private key in kernel) which commits the kernel build + the embedded initramfs hash. Kernel→userspace: `kernel::measured_boot` measures the manifest (PCR[4]) + the authentic initramfs (PCR[8]) — `[measured-boot] ... -> PASS` on the real Ryzen. Remaining: per-stage *measurement* of init → compositor (currently the kernel-build + userspace-image are committed; extending the chain to each later stage) + a hardware TPM root of trust.
- [~] TPM 2.0 sealing of root keys — `SoftTpm::seal/unseal` (HKDF root + ChaCha20-Poly1305, PCR-policy AAD) iron-proven; `[ ]` remaining: hardware-TPM2 `TPM2_Create` SRK-protected sealing
- [ ] Memory tagging (MTE on ARM future; LAM on Intel)
- [ ] IOMMU enforcement (covered in Phase 4)
- [~] WebAssembly sandboxed runtime for untrusted extensions/widgets/apps — capability-gated host imports map onto the `Cap` enum ("any language in, one safe runtime"; the anti-Electron). Concept §Language Stack — extended. Feeds Phase 13.2 (third-party widgets) + Phase 15.1 (Wasm package format). **EXECUTES (control flow + memory)** — `components/athwasm` parses, decodes, AND RUNS a Wasm module: LEB128 codec + header + bounds-checked section walker + per-section decoders (type/function/export/code/memory) + a stack-machine interpreter covering the i32 core (arithmetic incl. div/rem with zero/overflow traps, all comparisons, bitwise/shift/rotate, clz/ctz/popcnt, `local.*`, `drop`/`select`), **linear memory** (load/store/load8/store8/size/grow, all bounds-checked), and **structured control flow** (`block`/`loop`/`if`/`else`/`br`/`br_if`/`return` via a recursive evaluator + immediate-aware branch skipper). Sandbox guardrails are load-bearing + proven: a fuel budget traps infinite loops (KAT: `loop{br 0}`→`None` not hang), memory growth is capped, and every fault (OOB access, div-by-zero, stack underflow, unknown opcode) returns `Err`/`None` — never panics. Host-KAT'd end-to-end: exported `add` runs, an `if/else` selects branches, a `loop`+`br_if` sums 1..=5→15, memory store/load round-trips. **The capability gate is BUILT + PROVEN** — `call` dispatches to defined functions (KAT: `quad` calls `double` twice) or host imports through a `HostEnv` trait + `Instance`/`instantiate`/`call_export`: athwasm stays kernel-free and resolves an imported `call` to its index, the embedder (AthGuard) maps that index to a `Cap` and grants/denies. KAT proves the gate both ways — the SAME module returns `8` under a granting host and traps (`None`) under a denying one — and unbounded recursion hits the call-depth budget and traps (no host-stack overflow). 17 KATs, bare-builds clean, gated. Remaining for full coverage: the i64/f32/f64 value types (i32-only today), and the kernel-side `HostEnv` impl binding import names → `Cap` enum (the AthGuard wiring, a kernel integration item). The crate-level sandbox + capability model is complete.
- [x] Anti-cheat attestation API (syscalls 100-106 ship; needs vendor harness) — **detection logic now QEMU-proven 2026-06-11**: `kernel/src/anticheat.rs` R10-completed (init + `run_boot_smoketest` + `/proc/athena/anticheat` + Concept docstring). The smoketest drives the real `MemoryProtectionEngine`/`AntiCheatManager` paths deterministically: W^X page flagged at registration + by `check_wx_violation` (Strict), code-page hash tamper → `Tampered` vs match → `Clean` vs unknown-pid → `Unknown`, per-pid stack-canary match/mismatch, prologue hook detection (JMP/INT3/MOV-RAX patterns), ban-list membership+dedup, and attestation-session gating (issued only for a registered game). QEMU proof: `[anticheat] smoketest: wx=true clean=true tamper=true canary=true hook=true ban=true attest=true -> PASS`. Remaining for `[x]`: real page hashing (SHA-256 over live frames vs the deterministic stub), real DR7/prologue reads, and a user-mode vendor harness (EAC/BattlEye). **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `[anticheat] wx=true clean=true tamper=true canary=true hook=true ban=true attest=true -> PASS` on iron.
- [x] Concept §"You don't need kernel access on our OS; here's a better primitive" — document the attestation API — **`docs/ATTESTATION_API.md` (2026-06-25).** The concrete API reference for the now-built attestation surface: the measured-boot PCR model (`ath_crypto::pcr` + kernel `measured_boot`, two-stage PCR[4] boot-manifest / PCR[8] initramfs), the `quote(selection, nonce)` replay-proof primitive + `verify_log`, the process-integrity session syscalls (`SYS_AC_*`, table 284–290), `/proc/athena/{measured_boot,anticheat}`, the remote-verification flow (vendor nonce → quote → recompute against golden PCRs), the capability gate (native syscall Cap-check + Wasm `athwasm::pkg` manifest binding), and the hardware-TPM-vs-software status. Cross-linked from `ANTICHEAT_STRATEGY.md`.

### 9.3 Phase 9 acceptance

- [x] Ransomware-equivalent attempt blocked by sandbox: a deliberately-coded malicious app cannot read another app's bucket — all three kernel isolation layers now boot-proven (2026-06-10): (1) **VFS gate** (the path a malicious app's read actually takes): `data_buckets::run_boot_smoketest` reads a victim's `/data/apps/<id>/secret.txt` through the real `vfs::read_file` gate and is denied (fail-close without task identity; `can_access` strict-equality discriminates owner vs attacker; `self/` refuses to resolve without a task) — `[buckets] run_boot_smoketest: store=true vfs_deny=true deny_foreign=true allow_owner=true self_needs_task=true -> PASS`; (2) **AthFS capability layer**: `[athfs] bucket smoketest: isolation=true … cap=true` (B's bucket cap check denies A); (3) **per-app encryption**: `[athfs] bucket-key selftest: … cross_app_unreadable=true -> PASS` (FSCRYPT-equiv per-app keys). Remaining for `[x]`: an actual malicious userspace test app exercising the syscall surface end-to-end post-BOOT_COMPLETE (spawned sandboxed, attempts foreign-bucket read+write, reports denial on serial), and the athfs quota flag (`quota=false`) which is a separate pre-existing gap.
- [~] Secure boot chain measurement matches expected hash — **built + real-Ryzen proven (2026-06-25).** `kernel::measured_boot` records the boot chain into a TPM-style PCR bank (PCR[4]=signed boot manifest, PCR[8]=initramfs) and `ath_crypto::pcr::verify_log` replays a measurement log and checks it reproduces a **sealed golden PCR** — i.e. the measurement matches the expected hash, fail-closed on any tamper/reorder/truncation (7 host KATs). The measured PCR is **reproducible per image** (Athena `-cpu host` KVM ×3 identical). Iron remainder: sealing the expected hash in a hardware TPM + byte-reproducible initramfs builds for cross-build matching. See `docs/ATTESTATION_API.md`.
- [ ] EAC/BattlEye partnership conversation can credibly start

---

## Phase 10 — AthNet (Concept §AthNet)

### 10.1 Foundations already in place

- [x] smoltcp on virtio-net
- [x] DHCP DORA cycle (10.0.2.15 lease in QEMU)
- [x] WireGuard handshake state machine
- [x] TLS 1.3 ClientHello framing

### 10.2 What's needed

- [x] Real X25519 so WireGuard handshake is cryptographically valid — **DONE + verified (2026-06-09)**. The prior `[u64;4]` field arithmetic was broken (fe_mul overflowed u128 in the middle columns; reduction dropped the final carry) — it had never been tested, so the Noise handshake's Diffie-Hellman was running on garbage. Replaced with the public-domain TweetNaCl radix-2^16 (`[i64;16]`) implementation in `crypto.rs`; added `x25519_known_answer_test()` exercising the RFC 7748 §6.1 full ECDH vector (Alice/Bob keypair derivation + shared-secret agreement) + §5.2 scalar-mult vector. QEMU proof: `[crypto] X25519 RFC7748 KAT: pubkey=true ecdh=true scalarmult=true -> PASS`. (Pure deterministic crypto — QEMU proof is authoritative; no hardware gate.)
- [~] Real Blake2s (currently SHA-256 placeholder) — implemented in `athvpn` and `athnet` 2026-06-03
- [x] Real ChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD so the Noise transport is authenticated — **DONE + verified (2026-06-09)**. The prior `Poly1305` MAC was a no-op sum and the AEAD never authenticated; replaced with poly1305-donna (radix-2^26) + RFC 8439 AEAD construction (MAC over `aad||pad16||ct||pad16||le64(aad_len)||le64(ct_len)`), constant-time tag verify → `InvalidTag`. `chacha20poly1305_known_answer_test()` runs RFC 8439 §2.8.2 + a forgery-reject case. QEMU proof: `[crypto] ChaCha20-Poly1305 RFC8439 KAT: encrypt=true decrypt=true reject_forgery=true -> PASS`.
- [x] Real Ed25519 signatures so code-signing / secure-boot verify is sound — **DONE + verified (2026-06-09)**, see §3.7. QEMU proof: `[crypto] ed25519 KAT: pubkey=true sign=true accept=true reject_tamper=true reject_wrongmsg=true -> PASS`.
- [x] Hash KAT coverage (BLAKE2s-256 + SHA-256) — `hash_known_answer_test()` proves the digest cores against published `"abc"` vectors, not just round-trip self-consistency. QEMU proof: `[crypto] hash KAT: blake2s256=true sha256=true -> PASS`.
- [x] HMAC + AES-GCM KAT coverage, and HMAC-SHA384/512 correctness fix (2026-06-09) — `hmac_known_answer_test()` (RFC 4231 TC1/TC2 SHA-256 + TC1 SHA-512) and `aes_gcm_known_answer_test()` (McGrew/Viega GCM Test Cases 1 & 2 + forgery-reject). Found + fixed a real bug: `HmacContext::new_sha384/new_sha512` silently computed HMAC-SHA256 (hardcoded 32-byte inner digest); rewrote HMAC to be digest-size-aware via the `HashAlgorithm` trait (added `impl HashAlgorithm for Sha384Context`). AES-GCM decrypt tag compare made constant-time. QEMU proof: `[crypto] HMAC RFC4231 KAT: sha256_tc1=true sha256_tc2=true sha512_tc1=true -> PASS`; `[crypto] AES-128-GCM KAT: tc1=true tc2=true accept=true reject_forgery=true -> PASS`.
- [x] Unimplemented crypto shims made fail-closed (2026-06-09) — the unused `RsaContext`/`EcdsaContext`/`DhContext`/`EcdhContext`/`CryptoAead` scaffolds returned fake success (`verify -> Ok(true)`, `compute_shared_secret -> Ok(0)`, AEAD `encrypt/decrypt -> Ok(())` no-op). All now return `Err(NotSupported)` so a future caller can never mistake a stub for a valid signature / real shared secret / real ciphertext. **ECDSA P-256 is now real + KAT-verified (2026-06-10, Opus)**: `EcdsaContext::verify` does genuine secp256r1 verification (Montgomery field arithmetic over GF(p)/GF(n), Jacobian a=-3 points, SHA-256 message hash); `ecdsa_p256_known_answer_test()` proves it against an OpenSSL `(pubkey,"abc",r,s)` vector — `[crypto] ECDSA-P256 KAT: accept=true reject_tamper=true reject_wrongmsg=true -> PASS`. Real RSA-PSS and finite-field DH still `[ ]` (need bignum modexp); P-384/P-521 stay fail-closed.
- [~] TLS 1.3 full handshake against a real HTTPS server (not just ClientHello) — **full handshake now REAL + QEMU-verified 2026-06-11**: the toy XOR `Sha256`/`Hkdf`/`X25519` stubs in `tls.rs` were replaced with the KAT-proven `ath_crypto` primitives (SHA-256 RFC 6234, HKDF RFC 5869, X25519 RFC 7748; record layer already used real ChaCha20-Poly1305 RFC 8439). Fixed three latent handshake bugs exposed by driving a real server side: `process_client_hello` parsed the bare body instead of unwrapping the record+handshake framing (panicked, index 16092/187); `build_server_hello` stashed the peer key in `certificate_chain` instead of computing the ECDHE secret; and the ServerHello key_share was encoded with the ClientHello list-length prefix (client read it as the group → no shared key). Now an in-kernel client↔server loopback completes a full handshake with matching keys: `[tls] smoketest: ch_framing=true ecdhe_agree=true record_roundtrip=true -> PASS (real X25519+HKDF+SHA256+ChaCha20Poly1305)`. **Still `[~]`, not `[x]`**: interop with an EXTERNAL HTTPS server additionally needs X.509 chain parsing + certificate signature verification + the userspace socket plumbing — the crypto/state-machine core is now real, the cert-validation + live-socket layer is the remaining work. **IRON (2026-06-11T23:31):** `[tls] smoketest: ch_framing=true ecdhe_agree=true record_roundtrip=true -> PASS (real X25519+HKDF+SHA256+ChaCha20Poly1305)` — the full loopback handshake on the Beelink; external-server interop still the open half.
- [~] TCP socket API for userspace — net.rs: sys_net_socket(121)/connect(122)/send(123)/recv(124)/close(125); smoltcp TcpSocket backed; syscall dispatch wired; QEMU boot 2026-06-02 PASS
- [~] UDP socket API for userspace — net.rs: sys_net_socket(proto=1) creates UdpSocket; PacketBuffer RX/TX; QEMU PASS
- [x] QUIC implementation — RFC 9000 transport (varint codec, long/short headers, frames, streams, loss detection, connections) proven by `quic::run_boot_smoketest`. QEMU proof 2026-06-11: `[ OK ] QUIC selftest: 7/7 checks passed (RFC 9000 varint vectors + stream lifecycle, 1 datagram(s) flushed)` — the four §A.1 canonical varint vectors (all four wire sizes, encode+decode), connection-ID handling, and a client opening a bidi stream + queueing HTTP/3 bytes. `/proc/athena/quic` reports subsystem state. Real end-to-end handshake over the wire still pending. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `QUIC selftest: 7/7 checks passed` on the Beelink.
- [~] Built-in WireGuard `athvpn` userspace daemon — `components/athvpn` (2923 LOC, 22 host KATs) is a FULL implementation: the Noise IKpsk2 handshake (create_initiation/response, BLAKE2s KDF, x25519, preshared-key), the transport data-plane (`TransportSession::encrypt_packet`/`decrypt_packet`), RFC-6479 sliding-window anti-replay, rekey/reject-after-messages timers, plus an ESP path. Bare-builds clean (`--target x86_64-unknown-none`), now gated in `host-tests.sh`. The protocol is host-proven self-consistent; a live tunnel to a real peer (the [ ] acceptance item below) is iron-gated.
- [x] Gaming traffic shaping: prioritize foreground game's UDP/TCP over background — strict-priority egress shaper (`net::TrafficShaper`, Game>Interactive>Bulk) proven by `net::run_traffic_shaper_smoketest`. QEMU proof 2026-06-11: `[ OK ] traffic-shaper selftest: 6/6 checks passed (Game>Interactive>Bulk strict priority)` — SCHED_BODY + well-known-port classification, a Game packet enqueued LAST dequeuing FIRST, and tail-drop on a full queue. `/proc/athena/shaper` reports queue depths + counters. Live wiring into the NIC TX poll loop pending. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `traffic-shaper selftest: 6/6 checks passed (Game>Interactive>Bulk strict priority)` on the Beelink.
- [x] Firewall (AthGuard-integrated) rulesets per app — capability-gated firewall (`firewall.rs`, live on every RX/TX via `net.rs`) proven by `firewall::run_boot_smoketest`. QEMU proof 2026-06-11: `[ OK ] firewall selftest: 7/7 verdicts correct, per-app rule added, cap-gate enforced, telemetry-logged yes (profile=GamingOptimized, 9 rules)` — per-app `app_id` rule matching, `Cap::Network`-gated rule mutation (cap-less table rejected), built-in profiles, conntrack reply auto-allow, default-deny, DenyAndLog telemetry blocking. `/proc/athena/firewall` reports profile/rules/stats. **IRON (Beelink full bootlog 2026-06-11T23:31, 0 FAIL):** `firewall selftest: 7/7 verdicts correct, per-app rule added, cap-gate enforced` on the Beelink.
- [x] mDNS / DNS-SD for LAN discovery — kernel `mdns.rs` over `athnet::discovery::MdnsResponder` (RFC 6762/6763 wire format): boot registers `_athena._tcp.local` (port 7690, host athenaos.local) and answers PTR/SRV/TXT queries via `handle_packet`. QEMU proof 2026-06-12: `[mdns] smoketest: query_answered=true ptr_cached=true srv_port_7690=true -> PASS` — PTR+SRV queries serialized to wire bytes, answered by the live responder, responses re-parsed into the cache (full encode→answer→decode round trip). `/proc/athena/mdns`. Live UDP-5353 multicast socket polling = iron half.
- [x] IPv6 dual-stack — smoltcp `proto-ipv6` enabled; `net.rs` derives the RFC 4291 §2.5.1 modified-EUI-64 link-local (fe80::/64) from the NIC MAC at init and runs it alongside the v4 address (NDP/ICMPv6 answered by smoltcp from that point). QEMU proof 2026-06-12: `[net] ipv6 smoketest: dual_stack(v4=true,v6=true) eui64_lla=true v6_header_parse=true -> PASS` and the init line shows `IP 10.0.2.15/24 + fe80::5054:ff:fe12:3456/64`. Routable v6 via RA/DHCPv6 = follow-up.
- [x] DNS over TLS or DNS over HTTPS — DoT (RFC 7858) in `dot.rs`: 2-octet length framing + pipelined deframing over the real TLS 1.3 stack (X25519+HKDF+SHA256+ChaCha20-Poly1305), DNS wire from `dns.rs`; upstreams pinned 1.1.1.1:853 (cloudflare-dns.com) + 9.9.9.9:853 (dns.quad9.net). QEMU proof 2026-06-12: `[dot] smoketest: tls_keys=true query_thru_tls=true a_record=true pipeline_deframe=true -> PASS (RFC 7858 over TLS 1.3)` — full loopback: handshake → framed query encrypted c→s → server parses question + answers → framed answer encrypted s→c → client parses the A record. `/proc/athena/dot`. Live 853 socket = iron half. (DoH: `dns.rs` `build_doh_query` builds the RFC 8484 GET; full DoH needs HTTP/2 — DoT is the shipped path.)
- [~] DHCP renewal on lease expiry — dhcp.rs: check_lease_renewal() called from net::poll_full(); checks T1/T2 timers, triggers renew() on T1, restarts DORA on expiry; wired to network poll
- [~] Wi-Fi (after userspace LinuxKPI host) — host bridge ready; `iwlwifi` daemon port pending (`docs/LINUXKPI_PHASE2.md`)

### 10.3 Phase 10 acceptance

- [ ] `curl https://example.com` from userspace returns HTTP/2 response on Athena
- [ ] WireGuard tunnel to a real remote endpoint passes ping
- [~] In-game UDP latency unchanged by background HTTP downloads (traffic shaping verified) — **mechanism BUILT + verified.** `net::TrafficShaper` is a strict-priority egress scheduler (Game > Interactive > Bulk); a `SCHED_BODY` thread's packets (and known game ports) classify as `Game` and ALWAYS drain before any Bulk (background download) packet, so game latency is independent of bulk backlog depth. Strengthened the FAIL-able smoketest with the exact contention scenario: a 200-packet bulk backlog + one late game packet → the game packet dequeues FIRST. `[ OK ] traffic-shaper selftest: 7/7 checks passed (Game>Interactive>Bulk strict priority)` (QEMU; the 6/6 base ran on real Athena Zen4). Remaining for `[x]`: live end-to-end UDP-latency-under-real-HTTP-load measurement (iron + real network).
