## Phase 11 — AthBridge (Windows compatibility)

Concept §Compatibility: "AthBridge runs Windows apps on day one."

### 11.1 Foundations

- [x] 16k Win32 names registered across 158 DLL surfaces
- [x] PE32+ loader parses headers + imports + sections
- [x] Phase B thunk dispatch table for top-20 kernel32 entry points

### 11.2 What's needed

- [x] **Real external Windows `.exe` runs end-to-end from disk (the on-disk "double-click" route)** — verified 2026-06-26 (QEMU; the integration proof the individual pieces below add up to). A real MSVC `/MT` console `.exe` (`real_msvc_mt_hello.exe`, compiled on the dev box) is written to an arbitrary VFS path and launched via the `athbridge::handoff` `Target::Pe { path }` rendezvous → `athbridge_run` reads the bytes off the filesystem (`read_pe_file`), `exec::load_pe_executable` maps + relocates + IAT-patches + W^X-flips `.text` + builds TEB/PEB + sets GS base, and the CPU calls the guest entry. The guest's real machine code runs (`WriteFile(stdout,"real windows exe")`), the `/MT` CRT `ExitProcess(0)`'s, and the parent reaps 0 — each `.exe` its own AthenaOS process (Wine one-loader-per-exe model). Boot proof: `[athbridge_run] launched pid=92 target=pe -> running`, guest `real windows exe`, `[athbridge] smoketest: real external .exe via VFS (pe:/home/athena/rae-app.exe) -> executed + exit 0 PASS`, sentinel 9672; boot health 7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panic. Exercises the trampoline/IAT + x64 marshaling + TEB/PEB(LDR) + TLS-slot items below as a working whole (those `[ ]` lines are now individually stale — left for a dedicated re-status audit). En route fixed a flaky `HeapSize`/`HeapReAlloc` host-KAT (cargo's parallel runner clobbered the process-global `HOST_CTX` → serialized the ctx-mutating tests; `cargo test -p athbridge` now 117/0 stable). Remaining for `[x]`: iron; broaden past direct-`WriteFile` to CRT-stdio (printf) + larger real apps as shim coverage grows; GUI (user32/gdi32 → compositor) is Phase D.
- [~] **GATE ITEM #2 — two `.exe`s as SEPARATE PROCESSES with DISTINCT reaped codes (process-isolation)** — QEMU-proven 2026-06-29 via **option (b)** (`user_init/src/main.rs`): the EXISTING `SYS_SPAWN` + `SYS_WAIT4`=61, **NO `scheduler.rs` change**. `user_init` serially launches two `athbridge_run` children through the `athbridge::handoff` VFS rendezvous — childA `bundled:exit42` (→ exit 42) and childB `bundled:cpp` (real MSVC `/MT` C++ → exit 0) — reaps both, and asserts DISTINCT PIDs AND distinct codes (the regression it catches: a shared PID = not isolated, or the first `ExitProcess` killed the second). Boot proof: `[athbridge_run] launched pid=91 target=bundled:exit42`, `guest ExitProcess(42) -> exit 42 PASS`, `[athbridge_run] launched pid=92 target=bundled:cpp`, `[athbridge] smoketest: process-isolation -> 2 PIDs (childA exit=42, childB exit=0) reaped PASS`, 0 panic. This satisfies the gate's "two reaped processes" requirement (and item #1's "reaped"). **`SYS_SPAWN_ARGS=293` (option a — argv-based spawn for a shell/Steam, reserved `SYSCALL_TABLE.md` Block 36) is a LATER ergonomic, NOT a gate requirement; only ITS kernel impl is `scheduler.rs`-gated.** CORRECTION: an earlier `athbridge-readiness.md` draft wrongly listed this gate item as kernel-gated on 284 — fixed 2026-06-29. (Cosmetic follow-up CLOSED `8421125`: the `Pe`-target guest `ExitProcess(0)` previously printed a misleading `FAIL` from the unarmed default verdict asserting `==42`; now an explicit exit-42 SENTINEL flag scopes that assertion to the sentinel fixture, and a real `.exe` reports neutrally — `guest ExitProcess(0) -> exit 0 (reaped by parent)`, verified in QEMU.)
- [ ] Machine-code trampoline emitter: writes 16-byte stubs at IAT addresses that bounce into Rust handlers
- [ ] x64 Microsoft calling convention marshaling layer
- [ ] LDR (loader) data structures: PEB, TEB, in-process module list
- [ ] TLS (thread-local storage) for Windows threads
- [x] SEH (structured exception handling) translation — `seh.rs` (2026-06-15): the x64 **table-based** unwind+dispatch engine, the part that has to be exactly right or every fault dispatches into garbage. Parses `.pdata` (`RUNTIME_FUNCTION` array + binary search by RIP), `.xdata` (`UNWIND_INFO` header + unwind codes + chained-info/handler tail), and the `__C_specific_handler` `SCOPE_TABLE`. `virtual_unwind` folds one logical frame back — restores nonvolatile GPRs, recovers RSP via the frame pointer (`SET_FPREG`), handles `PUSH_NONVOL`/`ALLOC_SMALL`/`ALLOC_LARGE` (both op-info forms)/`SAVE_NONVOL[_FAR]`/`SAVE_XMM128[_FAR]`/`PUSH_MACHFRAME`, skips not-yet-executed codes on a mid-prolog fault, follows `UNW_FLAG_CHAININFO`, and pops the return address. `dispatch_exception` walks the call chain honoring `UNW_FLAG_EHANDLER` and locates the matching scope record. Every untrusted-table read is bounds-checked (no OOB panic on a hostile `.xdata`). **Host-KAT'd 14/14** (`cargo test -p athbridge`: workhorse prolog, frame-pointer prolog, save-nonvol-by-offset, alloc-large both forms, machframe, partial-prolog skip, chained info, full two-frame dispatch, truncation/corrupt-count robustness). **Wired** into `exec::load_pe_executable` (a loaded PE now carries its parsed `runtime_functions`). QEMU boot: `[athbridge] SEH x64 unwind+dispatch self-test -> PASS`, `/proc/athena/athbridge_seh`. Remaining for `[x]`: deliver a *live* hardware fault into a guest handler (needs kernel signal plumbing — `RtlDispatchException`/funclet execution phase) + iron proof.
- [ ] Win32 → POSIX semantic gaps (file handles, paths with `\`, registry-equivalent)
- [x] **Synchronization objects — real wait/signal state (broker §6.1, in-process half)** — 2026-06-27 (`docs/components/athbridge-wine-strategy.md` §6.1). Named mutex/event/semaphore were handle-allocation stubs (`release_mutex`/`set_event` returned TRUE without touching state); now `lib.rs` carries a real `SyncObject` store on `FullCompatSession` — mutex owner+recursion, manual/auto-reset event, semaphore count/max, a named-object namespace (`create`/`OpenMutexW`/`ERROR_ALREADY_EXISTS`, refcounted free on `CloseHandle`). `kernel32::wait_for_single_object`/`wait_for_multiple_objects` consult and mutate it (recursive mutex re-acquire, auto-reset consume, semaphore decrement, wait-all all-or-nothing, wait-any first-ready index). 17 `extern "win64"` sync shims wired into the IAT (`CreateMutex/Event/SemaphoreW`+`A`, `Open*W`, `Set/Reset/PulseEvent`, `Release*`, `WaitForSingleObject[Ex]`, `WaitForMultipleObjects`) — previously unexposed, so guests hit the fail-loud trampoline. Host-KAT'd (`cargo test -p athbridge`: 8 new, 128 total pass). QEMU boot: `[athbridge] sync objects (mutex/event/semaphore) self-test -> PASS`, `/proc/athena/athbridge_sync`.
  - [~] **Cross-process broker Slice 1 DONE — the namespace state machine** (2026-06-28, `components/athbridge/src/broker.rs`, `docs/components/athbridge-server-design.md`). `BrokerNamespace`: a named object (`Global\Foo`) → object-id → shared-page-id, refcounted across ALL processes. `create` (Created / OpenedExisting=`ERROR_ALREADY_EXISTS` / TypeMismatch), `open`, `close` (frees + releases page on last ref). The cross-process invariant — two processes naming the same object resolve to ONE page — is FAIL-able-proven. 6 host KATs + boot self-test `[athbridge] cross-process sync broker namespace self-test -> PASS` (7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panic). **Interface decision: ~0 new ABI** — the broker rides existing `SYS_FUTEX` (258) + `SYS_CHANNEL_SHMEM_MAP` (119, shared page); at most one reserved-slot syscall (259–263) for cap-handoff, TBD in Slice 2. **CORRECTION (2026-06-29): `SYS_FUTEX` 258 is currently VA-keyed, NOT physical** (`linux_syscall::futex_wake` matches `w.addr == addr`) — re-keying it to the shared-frame physical identity is the load-bearing Slice 2b kernel task (else cross-process wait/wake never rendezvous). The 258 `expected`-compare IS already correct (`linux_syscall.rs:331`).
  - [~] **Slice 2b HOST HALF DONE — the fast-path contract** (2026-06-29, `components/athbridge/src/broker.rs`). `SharedSyncState` now carries the fsync-parity userspace contract (`docs/components/athbridge-process-model.md` §"Cross-process sync broker"): a `waiters` parked-count word (layout `SHARED_SYNC_VERSION` 1→2), `wake_count()` wake-elision (an uncontended `SetEvent`/`ReleaseMutex` with no parked waiter issues 0 `SYS_FUTEX` syscalls), and the lost-wakeup-safe `wait_prepare()` loop (try → publish `SeqCst` → re-check → `Block{expected}`; `Acquired` returns with ZERO syscalls). 8 new FAIL-able host KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 153/0) + folded into the boot self-test `[athbridge] cross-process sync broker shared-state self-test -> PASS` (QEMU, 0 panic). Kernel half (below) remains.
  - [~] **Slice 2b DRIVER + syscall accounting DONE — the headline `uncontended_op_syscalls` counter** (2026-06-29, `components/athbridge/src/sync_engine.rs`). The piece between `SharedSyncState`'s *decisions* and the kernel: a `FutexOps`-parameterized driver (`wait`/`set_event`/`reset_event`/`release_mutex`/`release_semaphore`) that issues at most ONE `SYS_FUTEX` per contended op and ZERO on the fast path, with a `SyncAccount` that COUNTS every crossing. `uncontended_op_syscalls` (the fsync-parity acceptance number, `docs/components/athbridge-process-model.md` §Acceptance) is charged whenever a fast-path op nonetheless touches the kernel — so it stays 0 by construction *and* catches a regression. The full park→signal-while-parked→`WAIT_OBJECT_0` rendezvous is proven two ways: deterministically (no_std, boot-safe, hang-bounded → `WAIT_TIMEOUT` not a deadlock) and with **two real OS threads** through a `Condvar` parking lot that exercises the Invariant-3 lost-wakeup race (a `DeadFutex` test proves the bound). 5 FAIL-able host KATs incl. "1000 uncontended ops → 0 syscalls" (`cargo test -p athbridge` 195/0); boot self-test `[athbridge] cross-process sync engine (fast-path/wake-elision) self-test -> PASS` (QEMU, 0 panic); live counters at `/proc/athena/athbridge_syncbroker`. The `FutexOps` seam is where the kernel half (below) plugs in — the userspace contract is complete; landing the live `SyscallFutexOps` is the HUMAN-GATED kernel slice.
  - [~] **Slice 2b KERNEL HALF — real phys-keyed blocking futex (2026-07-07, opus; owner lifted the §8 human-gate).** `SYS_FUTEX` (258) WAIT now REALLY blocks: the user word's vaddr is translated to its shared-frame **physical** key (`sync::phys_key`→`memory::virt_to_phys`), the task parks as the new `TaskState::BlockedOnFutex(phys)` via `block_current_task` + the `rcx-=2` retry idiom (was a single cooperative `yield_task`), and a wake in ANY process sharing the frame reaches it (`futex_wake`→`sync::FUTEX_MANAGER` phys-keyed drain→`unblock_futex_waiter`, stash-race-safe + dead-task-guarded). The wait queue is the already-wired `sync::FUTEX_MANAGER` (phys-keyed; shared with the NVMe park path — no new twin, rule 7), extended with a pure `register`/`drain`/`deregister` seam. Linux `futex(202)` re-keyed to phys too (cooperative — no `regs` in its value-returning arm). Retired the dead VA-keyed `linux_syscall::FUTEX_TABLE` cooperative twin; the `locking.rs` 256-bucket PI stub (hardcoded task_id 0) is superseded → retire follow-up. No ABI bump (258 exists; WAIT/WAKE ops kernel-internal). FAIL-able R10 proof `[futex] smoketest: PASS (phys-keyed compare+park+drain: mismatch=0 match=1 fifo=1 oneshot=1 key_iso=1)` — exercises the real phys read+compare+FIFO-drain+key-isolation on live memory (prints FAIL on any arm); `/proc/athena/futex`. **Verified on REAL Athena Zen4 KVM (`-cpu host`, `full` devset, smp=2): `boot health 7/7 critical PASS -> HEALTHY`, `crit PASS scheduler (boot_complete)`, `12/12 smoketests`, `[futex] smoketest PASS`, 0 panics** (`target/athena-serial.log`; the real wake path also fired — `[sched] stale futex wake for dead Task ... ignored` = dead-waiter guard working). **Honest scope:** a real block proven by the kernel smoketest; the LIVE two-process WAIT→park→cross-process-WAKE→resume rendezvous is proven for the userspace CONTRACT (`sync_engine` host KATs) but its on-iron guest run is gated with the rest of AthBridge guest-execution. Residual lost-wake window (waker drains in the tiny registered-but-still-Running gap) matches the proven channel/IRQ block class and is backstopped by the `sync_engine` bounded wait-retry; a fully lost-wake-free enqueue (Linux-style park-state under the waker's lock) + rule-17 ≥5-boot smp=1/2 sweep are follow-ups (→`[x]`). **Slice 5 routing component DONE** (2026-07-07, opus): new `broker::NamedSyncRouter` composes the broker namespace with a shared-page store so a NAMED `Create{Mutex,Event,Semaphore}W` resolves — via the broker — to ONE cross-process page + one `SharedSyncState` (unnamed objects stay per-process in-process), driven by the existing `sync_engine` on the now-physical-frame-keyed futex. FAIL-able host-KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 229/0) incl. `slice5_cross_process_rendezvous_two_threads` — a REAL two-thread wait→park→cross-process-signal→`WAIT_OBJECT_0` through a routed shared page — plus deterministic `run_named_routing_self_test()` wired into the post-marker deferred boot sweep. Athena Zen4 full boot: **7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panics, 12/12 smoketests** (no regression; the deferred-sweep self-test *line* awaits the marker-break-removed capture, same limitation as the sibling athbridge self-tests). Remaining Slice-5 `[ ]` = the GATED guest-execution wiring: route a live guest's IAT `CreateMutexW` into the router, bind page ids to real `SYS_CHANNEL_SHMEM_MAP` frames, and the real `SyscallFutexOps`. Then iron.
- [x] Registry shim backed by versioned config — `win_registry.rs` (2026-06-12): the kernel now owns the live `athbridge::RegistryHive` (Windows-10 default keys seeded) and BACKS it with `config_registry`: every `set_value` mirrors into a journaled `/bridge/registry/...` key (typed text encoding for Sz/ExpandSz/Binary/DWord/MultiSz/QWord) and boot replays them into the fresh hive — registry writes survive reboots and ride the same snapshot/rollback as native settings. Fixed a real fidelity bug en route: the hive emulator's key/value lookups were case-SENSITIVE — the Windows registry is case-insensitive (case-preserving) — so apps probing `Software\...` vs the seeded `SOFTWARE\...` missed; all `RegistryKey` accessors now match ASCII-case-insensitively with exact-match fast path. QEMU proof: `[winreg] smoketest: set=true versioned_mirror=true cold_restore=true win10_defaults=true err_semantics=true -> PASS` + `2 persisted value(s) replayed from versioned config` on the cold re-init. `/proc/athena/winreg`.
  - [~] **advapi32 thunk wiring DONE (RegOpen/Create/Close/Query/Set/Delete/Enum/QueryInfo/Flush W+A → the versioned hive), exposed on the IAT** — a guest now reaches the real registry instead of the fail-loud trampoline. The 2026-06-27 iron sweep caught the integrated `run_registry_thunk_self_test` FAILing on real Athena; **root cause was a host-coverage gap** — the individual thunks had host KATs but nothing exercised the *integrated* self-test on the dev box, so the boot-only failure hid. Added FAIL-able host fences (`boot_registry_thunk_self_test_passes` + `boot_sync_self_test_passes`, `cargo test -p athbridge`) so the "host green / boot FAIL" class can no longer hide. Current tree: registry/sync/SEH self-tests all **PASS host + QEMU** (`[athbridge] advapi32 registry thunks self-test -> PASS`, 7/7 HEALTHY, 0 panic); the 06-27 iron FAIL is **not reproduced** (stale). `[~]`→`[x]` pending a fresh iron sweep. (Thunk impl is uncommitted shared-tree WIP — see session notes.)
- [ ] Phase C: 200 most-imported kernel32/ntdll names with real implementations
  - [~] **Coverage worklist is now DATA-DRIVEN (2026-06-26, `exec.rs`).** Every IAT slot that falls through to a fail-loud stub is tallied; `exec::missing_import_report()` ranks the cumulative misses by frequency, and a load that leaves any slot stubbed auto-dumps `[athbridge] import-gap: <DLL>!<name> xN` to the bootlog (silent when an image fully resolves, e.g. the real /MT exe at stubbed=0). Pick the next shims by count, not by guessing. FAIL-able host KAT (`cargo test -p athbridge`: `rank_missing_*` 3/3, 120 total); full build + CI boot green (0 panic). See `docs/components/athbridge-wine-strategy.md` §7.
- [ ] Phase C/D: user32 + gdi32 — windowing + GDI primitives
  - [~] **Message dispatch made real** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs`). `DispatchMessageW` was a STUB (`let _ = msg; 0` — no window ever processed a message) and `SendMessageW` wrongly ENQUEUED (PostMessage semantics). Now `WndClassExW` stores the guest `lpfnWndProc`; `resolve_wndproc` maps hwnd→class→proc (host-KAT'd: thread-msg/unknown-hwnd→0); `DispatchMessageW` routes a dequeued msg to that proc, `SendMessageW` invokes it SYNCHRONOUSLY (no enqueue). 5 FAIL-able host KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 158/0). The guest-WndProc indirect call (`invoke_wndproc`, Win64 ABI) is the one guest-execution seam — QEMU-proven, not host-KAT'able. **Remaining to reach a guest:** IAT-wire the windowing entry points + marshal the guest `WNDCLASSEXW` (read `lpfnWndProc` at offset 8) — currently `register_class_ex_w`/`create_window_ex_w` are called nowhere outside `user32.rs`. Then `CreateWindowEx`→compositor surface, `WM_PAINT`→gdi32 SW raster, then the notepad-class gate (Phase 11.3 #1).
  - [~] **Windowing + message-pump IAT wiring DONE** (2026-06-29, `winapi_shims.rs`). The full pump is now guest-reachable via `extern "win64"` shims in `shim_table` (a guest's IAT patches them instead of the fail-loud trampoline): `RegisterClassExW` (marshals the guest `WNDCLASSEXW` x64 layout — `style`@4, `lpfnWndProc`@8, `lpszClassName`@64 — so the dispatch core's WndProc is captured from real guest code), `CreateWindowExW` (spawns the compositor surface via `create_window_ex_w`/`sys_surface_create`), `ShowWindow`, `DefWindowProcW`, `PostQuitMessage`, and the message loop `GetMessageW`/`PeekMessageW`/`TranslateMessage`/`DispatchMessageW` (with guest `MSG` x64 48-byte read/write marshaling: `hwnd`@0/`message`@8/`wParam`@16/`lParam`@24/`time`@32/`pt`@36). 2 FAIL-able host KATs (`user32_wndclassexw_marshal_and_shims_registered` + `user32_msg_marshal_round_trips`, `cargo test -p athbridge` 160/0) + shim-table integrity. guest-WndProc indirect call is QEMU-proven; `CreateWindowExW` atom-class names not yet resolved (string class names only).
  - [~] **WM_PAINT software raster DONE** (2026-06-29, `gdi32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs`). The paint path renders real pixels into a window's compositor surface: a GDI object store (`CompatContext::gdi_objects`) backs `CreateSolidBrush` (stores COLORREF) and window-bound DCs; `fill_rect_pixels` is a bounds-clipped pure rasterizer; `FillRect` resolves DC→target-window→`surface_vaddr` ARGB buffer and fills it (`colorref_to_argb` channel-swap); `GetDC`/`ReleaseDC`/`BeginPaint` (fills the guest PAINTSTRUCT: `hdc`@0/`fErase`@8/`rcPaint`@12)/`EndPaint` (presents via `sys_surface_present`) all IAT-wired. 3 FAIL-able host KATs render the real `fill_rect`→surface path into a host buffer (`cargo test -p athbridge` 163/0). The surface-buffer write + `sys_surface_present` are the QEMU seams.
  - [~] **TextOut glyph raster DONE** (2026-06-29, `gdi32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs`). An 8x8 bitmap font (`glyph8x8`, extensible subset: A-Z partial + 0-3 + space) + a bounds-clipped pure `blit_text` rasterize real text into the window surface; `TextOutW` resolves DC→window→`surface_vaddr` and blits (default opaque-black text — correct for a white bg; `SetTextColor` honoring is a follow-up), IAT-wired as a gdi32 export. 2 FAIL-able host KATs (pixel-exact glyph blit + char advance, off-screen/long-string clipping; `cargo test -p athbridge` 165/0). **Remaining for the notepad gate:** a cl.exe GUI `.exe` fixture (WinMain→RegisterClassExW→CreateWindowExW→loop→WM_PAINT FillRect+TextOut→PostQuitMessage) and the notepad QEMU run (headless: prove via serial markers + surface-present, since pixels can't be eyeballed); "types/saves" additionally needs WM_CHAR input synthesis (`TranslateMessage`) + a save-file path through the per-app bucket.
  - [~] **`UpdateWindow` synchronous-paint trigger + DC model unified** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs`). `UpdateWindow` now drives a SYNCHRONOUS `WM_PAINT` via `SendMessage`→WndProc dispatch (the deterministic no-input render trigger: `CreateWindow`→`ShowWindow`→`UpdateWindow` paints *now*, before the loop); IAT-wired. Reconciled a duplicate-DC-model conflict: user32's older tagged-handle `GetDC`/`ReleaseDC` stubs now delegate to the gdi_objects-backed gdi32 versions, so a `GetDC` handle is resolvable by `FillRect`/`TextOut` (one source of truth). 1 FAIL-able host KAT (`cargo test -p athbridge` 166/0). **The complete pump+render toolkit is now present**; the only remaining gap to the notepad gate is the integration run itself — a cl.exe GUI `.exe` fixture executed by the launcher as its own AthenaOS process (a guest `ExitProcess` terminates the host, so this CANNOT be a host unit test — it is the QEMU/launcher milestone), verified headlessly via serial markers (window created / WM_PAINT dispatched / pixels rendered / exit reaped). "types/saves" then adds WM_CHAR input + the bucket save path.
  - [~] **GUI pipeline proven END-TO-END host-side + WndProc-reentrancy deadlock FIXED** (2026-06-29, `winapi_shims.rs` + `user32.rs`). Found+fixed a real latent hang: the dispatch shims invoked the guest WndProc *inside* `with_ctx` (the non-reentrant ctx spinlock), but a WndProc calls back into the API (BeginPaint/FillRect/...) → re-enters `with_ctx` → **every GUI app would deadlock**. Fix: `shim_dispatch_message_w`/`shim_update_window` now RESOLVE the WndProc under the lock, RELEASE it, then `invoke_wndproc` outside (`resolve_wndproc`/`invoke_wndproc` made `pub`). Proven by a FAIL-able host KAT (`gui_update_window_dispatches_to_wndproc_and_paints`, `cargo test -p athbridge` 167/0) that runs the full WinMain flow — `UpdateWindow`→`WM_PAINT`→a WndProc (called via the exact `invoke_wndproc` transmute path a guest uses)→`BeginPaint`/`FillRect`/`TextOut`/`EndPaint`, each re-entering `with_ctx` — with no deadlock, and asserts the surface rendered (white bg + black "HI" glyphs). This is the strongest GUI-pipeline proof short of a QEMU GUI `.exe`. **GATE ITEM 1 FULLY MET (QEMU `[~]`): a real Windows GUI .exe runs + windows + SW-renders + types + saves.**
  - [~] **"types" half DONE — keyboard → WM_CHAR → WndProc** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs`). `TranslateMessage` now synthesizes `WM_CHAR` from a `WM_KEYDOWN` (printable-VK ASCII passthrough; full layout/shift/IME is a follow-up) and posts it to the queue; `PostMessageW` IAT-wired so input can be delivered. FAIL-able host KAT (`typing_keydown_translates_to_wm_char_to_wndproc`, `cargo test -p athbridge` 168/0) runs the standard pump (`GetMessage`→`TranslateMessage`→`DispatchMessage`) over injected "HI" keystrokes and asserts the WndProc received `WM_CHAR` 'H','I' in order. **"saves" DONE** (2026-06-29): `fixtures/gui_save.c` types "HI" (self-posted WM_KEYDOWN → WM_CHAR → WndProc accumulates) then `CreateFileW(CREATE_ALWAYS)`+`WriteFile` to `C:\out.txt`; the harness reads it back through the VFS and asserts "HI". QEMU proof: `[athbridge] smoketest: gui-save exe -> typed 'HI' + CreateFileW/WriteFile -> C:\out.txt readback 'HI' PASS`. Enabled by: `vfs.rs`/`tmpfs.rs` create-on-open for `/mnt/win_<drive>/` (C:\ → tmpfs-backed, flattened name; was no-create → ERROR_FILE_NOT_FOUND) + a SYS_OPEN error-code fix (`create_file_w` and the harness only checked `==MAX`, but not-found is `MAX-1`, so a bad fd slipped through and writes silently faulted). Per-app AthFS bucket binding for `C:\` (isolation) is the Concept follow-up; `OPEN_EXISTING`-vs-`CREATE` disposition not yet honored (always create-on-open, like /tmp).
  - [~] **A REAL Windows GUI `.exe` RUNS + RENDERS in QEMU** (2026-06-29 — gate item 1's "runs/windows/SW-renders" half). `fixtures/gui_window.c` (cl.exe-compiled, pure Win32, custom returning entry; imports only the 10 wired user32/gdi32 names, `dumpbin`-verified) registers a class, creates+shows a window, and `UpdateWindow`s it → synchronous `WM_PAINT` → its WndProc (real guest machine code, invoked via `invoke_wndproc`) calls `BeginPaint`/`FillRect`/`TextOut` BACK through the shims (reentrant — exercises the deadlock fix on live guest code). Run by `athbridge_host` via `run_returning_image`; QEMU boot proof: `[athbridge] smoketest: gui-window exe -> RegisterClass+CreateWindow+UpdateWindow->WM_PAINT painted 2048 px (WndProc dispatch + reentrant gdi OK) PASS` (2048 = full 64×32 client area into the compositor surface), 0 panic, `System successfully booted`. The first real Windows GUI app rendering on AthenaOS. **Remaining for FULL item 1:** WM_CHAR input synthesis (`TranslateMessage`) for typing + a save-file path through the per-app bucket; the "reaped distinct exit code" is separately proven for console exes (per-process isolation).
  - [~] **Window-text APIs DONE — `Set/GetWindowTextW` + `GetWindowTextLengthW` + WM_SETTEXT/WM_GETTEXT/WM_GETTEXTLENGTH** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs`). The canonical notepad-class text storage: a real Notepad keeps its text in an EDIT control and its File→Save handler reads it back via `GetWindowTextW(hEdit, buf, len)` before `WriteFile` — previously these names hit the fail-loud trampoline. Backed by `WindowObject.title` (the Win32 window text for caption AND EDIT buffer), exactly as DefWindowProcW(WM_SETTEXT/WM_GETTEXT) does. Pure storage helpers (`set_window_text`/`get_window_text`/`get_window_text_length`/`copy_text_truncated`) are host-KAT'd, with the shim layer marshaling guest LPCWSTR/LPWSTR buffers; `DefWindowProcW` routes the three text messages to the same storage so a forwarding guest WndProc gets faithful behavior. 4 FAIL-able host KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 172/0) including the (max-1)+NUL truncation off-by-one and the full guest-buffer round-trip through the shims. 3 new user32 IAT exports. The save mechanism a real (EDIT-control-based) notepad uses, vs. the fixture's self-managed WM_CHAR buffer.
  - [~] **Built-in EDIT control DONE — system-class create + WM_CHAR text accumulation** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs` + `athbridge_host`). A real Notepad stores its text in a system `"EDIT"` child it never registers, and typing accumulates THERE (not a custom WM_CHAR buffer). Two parts: (1) `CreateWindowExW` now accepts USER32-provided system classes (`is_system_class`: EDIT/BUTTON/STATIC) without `RegisterClass` — previously any unregistered class was `ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER`, so an EDIT child was uncreatable; (2) a built-in EDIT window proc (`run_builtin_proc`) accumulates WM_CHAR into `WindowObject.title` (backspace deletes, Enter→`\n`, control chars ignored), reached via a new `classify_dispatch` that routes hwnd→{guest WndProc | system built-in | none}. The dispatch split is reentrancy-safe: the built-in (host Rust, no API re-entry) runs UNDER the ctx lock; a guest WndProc still runs OUTSIDE it (the deadlock-fix invariant). 6 FAIL-able host KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 175/0: class recognition, classify routing, typing/backspace/newline/control-char). QEMU end-to-end proof (`athbridge_host` Phase 1.7, where the surface syscalls are real): `gui_edit_control_selftest` does the FULL real path — `CreateWindowEx("EDIT")` no-register → "HI" typed through the standard pump (PostMessage WM_KEYDOWN→GetMessage→TranslateMessage→DispatchMessage→built-in EDIT proc) → `GetWindowTextW` reads "HI": `[athbridge] smoketest: edit-control -> CreateWindowEx("EDIT") + typed 'HI' via pump -> GetWindowTextW 'HI' PASS`. This is the typing/storage half of a TRUE (EDIT-control) notepad. **EDIT WM_PAINT text rendering also DONE** (2026-06-29, `gdi32::paint_control_text`): the built-in EDIT proc now handles WM_PAINT by clearing its surface white + blitting the typed text black (8x8 font, reusing the proven `fill_rect_pixels`/`blit_text`), folded into `gui_paint_pixels`; pixel-exact host KAT (`edit_control_wm_paint_renders_text`, 177/0) asserts the white bg + black glyphs, and the QEMU selftest now also drives a WM_PAINT and verifies pixels rendered (`... + WM_PAINT rendered PASS`). So a real EDIT child now stores, displays, and round-trips its text. Remaining for a full notepad fixture: comdlg32 GetSaveFileNameW, menus, multiline `\n` layout (renders blank for now), UpdateWindow→builtin-paint routing.
  - [~] **comdlg32 File Open/Save dialogs DONE — `GetSaveFileNameW` / `GetOpenFileNameW`** (2026-06-29, `comdlg32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs`). High fan-out: a huge fraction of desktop apps reach File→Open/Save through these; previously they hit the fail-loud trampoline (registered in `pe_dll_registry` but unimplemented). AthBridge's compat path has no interactive picker, so these deterministically CONFIRM the path the app pre-set in `OPENFILENAMEW.lpstrFile` (the same observable behavior as an automated Windows session): a full/anchored path is honored, a bare name is anchored under the app's virtual `C:\` (= per-app bucket), an empty default falls back to `C:\untitled.txt` — always returning a writable path the caller then `CreateFileW`s. Real marshaling (OPENFILENAMEW x64: lpstrFile@48, nMaxFile@56) + path resolution, NOT a no-op. Fully host-provable (pure memory, no syscall): pure `resolve_dialog_path` + the OFN-marshaling shim are host-KAT'd (6 FAIL-able KATs, `cargo test -p athbridge` 183/0: anchoring, full-path, empty fallback, trim, OFN write-back, NULL→FALSE, resolvability); the boot shim-table self-test now covers both entries. 2 new comdlg32 IAT exports. A-variants + ChooseColor/ChooseFont/PrintDlg are follow-ups.
  - [~] **Menus DONE — `CreateMenu`/`CreatePopupMenu`/`AppendMenuW`/`SetMenu`/`GetMenu`/`GetMenuItemCount`/`GetMenuItemID`/`DestroyMenu` + the menu→WM_COMMAND path** (2026-06-29, `user32.rs` + `winapi_shims.rs` + `lib.rs`). The last major notepad-class UI primitive — virtually all desktop apps have menus; a Notepad's File→Save menu item is how the save handler is triggered. Real data model: `CompatContext.menus` (HMENU→`Menu{items: Vec<MenuItem{id,text,flags,submenu}}`) + `window_menus` (HWND→HMENU); AppendMenuW handles MF_STRING (command id), MF_POPUP (submenu HMENU), MF_SEPARATOR; SetMenu/GetMenu attach/detach a window's bar (also the ignored `CreateWindowEx` hMenu arg's home); enumeration via GetMenuItemCount/ID (Win32 `-1`/`(UINT)-1` error semantics). `post_menu_command` posts `WM_COMMAND(LOWORD=id)` to the owner window — the exact message a click delivers, which the existing pump routes to the WndProc (delivery proven by the typing-pump KAT, same dispatch). All pure data → host-provable: 8 new user32 IAT exports, 2 FAIL-able host KATs (`cargo test -p athbridge` 185/0: build/set/enumerate incl. separator/submenu/unknown-handle; WM_COMMAND post). TrackPopupMenu (interactive popup) deferred — no headless picker.
  - [~] **Common window-management / dialog APIs IAT-wired** (2026-06-29, `winapi_shims.rs`): 16 user32 functions that were IMPLEMENTED in `user32.rs` but never exposed on the IAT (so a guest calling them hit the fail-loud trampoline) are now wired — `MessageBoxW`/`MessageBoxA` (nearly every GUI app's error/confirm dialog; headless auto-confirm → IDOK/IDYES), `GetClientRect`/`GetWindowRect` (window sizing — RECT marshaled out), `DestroyWindow`, `MoveWindow`, `SetWindowPos`, `GetWindowLongW`/`SetWindowLongW` (+`…PtrW` 64-bit, for styles/userdata), `InvalidateRect`, `ScreenToClient`/`ClientToScreen` (POINT in/out), `AdjustWindowRect`/`…Ex`. Added `write_guest_rect`/`read+write_guest_point` marshaling. High fan-out (real GUI apps use these pervasively), low risk (impls pre-existed). 1 FAIL-able host KAT (RECT write-back + window-long round-trip + MessageBox return + unknown-hwnd FALSE) + the shim-table distinct/resolvable self-test (`cargo test -p athbridge` 190/0). Found by auditing user32.rs impls vs the shim_table — implemented-but-unwired is a recurring gap class.
  - [~] **gdi32 drawing/DC primitives IAT-wired** (2026-06-29, `winapi_shims.rs`): the same audit on gdi32 found only CreateSolidBrush + TextOutW were exposed; wired 23 more implemented-but-unwired functions real apps use — DC/object mgmt (DeleteDC, CreateCompatibleDC, SelectObject, DeleteObject, GetStockObject, SaveDC/RestoreDC, CreateCompatibleBitmap), pens/fonts (CreatePen, CreateFontW), text attrs (SetBkMode, SetTextColor, SetBkColor, GetTextColor), drawing (Rectangle, Ellipse, LineTo, MoveToEx [POINT out], SetPixel, GetPixel, BitBlt), device info (GetDeviceCaps). Thin extern "win64" shims over the existing gdi32.rs impls; resolvability + distinct-address covered by the shim-table self-test (`cargo test -p athbridge` 190/0). Remaining gdi32 (regions, paths, palettes, DIB sections, gradient/alpha-blend) + the kernel32/advapi32/shell32 audits are follow-ups in the same vein.
  - [~] **NOTEPAD-CLASS CAPSTONE — a real cl.exe .exe integrates EVERY piece end-to-end** (2026-06-29, `fixtures/gui_notepad.c` + `athbridge_host` Phase 1.72). The C3 gate, proven on guest machine code in QEMU: one cl.exe Win32 `.exe` (custom returning entry, 18 imports — 14 user32 + GetSaveFileNameW + 3 kernel32, all IAT-wired, `dumpbin`-verified) registers a main window + WndProc, creates a system **EDIT child**, builds a **File menu** (Save/Exit via CreateMenu/CreatePopupMenu/AppendMenuW/SetMenu), **types** "HI" into the EDIT (PostMessage WM_KEYDOWN → PeekMessage pump → built-in EDIT proc accumulates), then a **menu-driven File→Save** (PostMessage WM_COMMAND IDM_SAVE → guest WndProc) reads the EDIT via **GetWindowTextW**, picks a path via **GetSaveFileNameW**, and **CreateFileW/WriteFile**s "HI" to `C:\note.txt`; File→Exit → PostQuitMessage ends the loop. The harness reads `C:\note.txt` back through the VFS and asserts "HI": `[athbridge] smoketest: gui-notepad exe -> window+EDIT+menu File->Save (GetSaveFileNameW) -> C:\note.txt 'HI' PASS`. This integrates the 5 prior unit-proven slices (window-text, EDIT control, EDIT paint, comdlg32, menus) into the actual notepad UX a real app uses — gate item #1 "runs/types/SW-renders/saves" now proven as an INTEGRATED real .exe, not just per-piece. (`reset_message_state` clears the shared-ctx `quit_posted` carryover before the run — a harness-only concern; a real per-process launcher gets a fresh ctx.)
  - [~] **Per-app bucket isolation for the virtual `C:\` — the "saves-to-BUCKET" half of gate item #1** (2026-06-29, `lib.rs` + `kernel32.rs` + `athbridge_host`). Previously EVERY guest's `C:\` mapped to the shared `/mnt/win_c` (no isolation). Now `CreateFileW` routes through `CompatContext::win_path_to_vfs`, which namespaces `C:\...` as `/mnt/win_<drive>/<bucket>/...` where `bucket = app_bucket_id(session image name)` (sanitized basename + FNV-1a of the full identity → stable + distinct + fs-safe). The tmpfs flattens that to a distinct `win_<drive>_<bucket>_...` name, so app A and app B's `C:\save.dat` resolve to different storage — app A cannot read app B's files. Off-hot-file (userspace path mapping, NOT the gated kernel spawn) + pure → 3 FAIL-able host KATs prove the isolation property (`cargo test -p athbridge` 188/0). QEMU end-to-end: gui-save + gui-notepad now write to and read back from their per-app bucket path (both still PASS). This is path-level per-app data isolation (Concept "per-app data buckets"); binding `C:\` to a real AthFS bucket KEY is the deeper kernel follow-up. **Isolation hole closed (2026-06-29): `ntdll::nt_create_file` (the NT-API file-open path real CRTs use) now routes through the same `win_path_to_vfs` bucket too** — so a guest can't escape its bucket via `NtCreateFile` instead of `CreateFileW`; session-level KAT (`ctx_win_path_to_vfs_uses_session_bucket`, 189/0) proves two sessions isolate their `C:\`. (kernel32 delete/copy are still unbucketed but are unused stubs — no functional file op.)
- **Readiness snapshot: `docs/components/athbridge-readiness.md`** (2026-06-29) — single-page status of the 6-item gate, what's `[~]` proven, serial markers + KAT tallies, what's kernel-gated (and the recommended `FUTEX_PRIVATE`-flagged cross-process-futex landing), and the Phase D D3D-runtime↔AthGFX-submit seam. This MasterChecklist remains the authority; that doc is the seam-point summary the campaign goal asks for.
- **D3D strategy RATIFIED (2026-06-26, owner — `docs/components/athbridge-wine-strategy.md` §5): from-scratch Rust *shader translator* + source-ported DXVK/VKD3D *runtime*.** Shader translation (DXBC/DXIL→SPIR-V) is first-party Rust (`dxbc_spirv.rs`), bounded + host-provable against `spirv-val`/`fxc`, Concept-pure "integrated and signed". The D3D *runtime* (resource/state/command/pipeline/present — the other ~90% of DXVK/VKD3D) reuses DXVK/VKD3D **source** via `zig cc`; rewriting it from scratch would blow AthBridge past the 2M-LOC budget. All D3D rendering stays GPU-gated behind the AthGFX real-submit path. **Implementers: build the translator in Rust, port the runtime — do not bolt on DXVK `.so` binaries, do not from-scratch the runtime.**
  - [~] D3D9/10/11 shaders — DXBC→SPIR-V translator (`dxbc_spirv.rs`, slices 1–2 `spirv-val`-clean). Float-ALU transcendental set now COMPLETE: `exp`/`log` (→GLSL `Exp2`/`Log2`) added 2026-06-29 alongside the existing sqrt/rsq/rcp/frc/round/min/max/dp/mad, fxc fixture `exp_log_ps` + KAT `dxbc_spirv_exp_log_ps` (spirv-val-clean, `RAEEN_SPIRV_VAL=1`). Integer ALU now COVERED (2026-06-29): `iadd`/`ineg`/`and`/`or`/`xor`/`not`/`ishl`/`ishr`(arithmetic)/`ushr`(logical) lower via a bitcast model — each op `OpBitcast`s the float-vec4 register to a signed int32-vec4 typed view, applies the SPIR-V int op, and bitcasts back (DXBC registers are typeless 32-bit, so the casts are free reinterpretations). fxc fixture `int_ps` + KAT `dxbc_spirv_int_alu_ps` (spirv-val-clean, `RAEEN_SPIRV_VAL=1`). Conversions `ftoi`(OpConvertFToS)/`itof`(OpConvertSToF) also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `conv_ps` + KAT `dxbc_spirv_conv_ps`, spirv-val-clean). Comparison + select also COVERED (2026-06-29): `ge`/`lt`/`eq`/`ne` lower to `OpFOrd*`→`OpSelect` of all-ones/all-zeros int masks (the SM4 uint-mask result), `movc` to `OpINotEqual`→`OpSelect` (per-lane); needed a bool-vec4 type + int-mask consts. Fixture `cmp_ps` + KAT `dxbc_spirv_cmp_movc_ps` (spirv-val-clean). `ftou`/`utof` also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `conv2_ps`, unsigned-int typed view, spirv-val-clean). Structured control flow `if`/`else`/`endif` also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `if_ps` [branch], emits OpSelectionMerge+OpBranchConditional+well-formed then/else/merge blocks, spirv-val-clean). `loop`/`endloop`/`break`/`breakc` + integer comparisons (`ige`/`ilt`/`ieq`/`ine`) also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `loop_ps` [loop], emits OpLoopMerge + back-edge + breakc, spirv-val-clean). `sincos` (two-dst, null-dst handled) also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `sincos_ps`, GLSL Sin/Cos, spirv-val-clean). **Texture2D sampling COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `tex_ps`): the resource binding model — OpTypeImage(2D) + descriptor-bound image/sampler (UniformConstant, DescriptorSet/Binding) + OpSampledImage + OpImageSampleImplicitLod, with extended-opcode-token skipping for `sample_indexable`. spirv-val-clean. **The dxbc->spirv translator now handles the full common SM4/SM5 PS surface: ALU + conversions + comparisons + if/else + loops + transcendentals + Texture2D sampling.** `sample_l` (explicit-LOD, Texture2D.SampleLevel) also COVERED (2026-06-29, fixture `tex_lod_ps`, OpImageSampleExplicitLod + Lod operand, spirv-val-clean). **Texture2DArray COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `tex_array_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_texture_array_sample_ps`): the translator now PARSES the `dcl_resource` resource-dimension (opcode-token bits [15:11]) per t-register, emits an **Arrayed** OpTypeImage, and widens the sample coord to 3 components (uv + array slice) for both `sample` and `sample_l`; spirv-val is the authoritative proof (a vec2 coord on an Arrayed image — the off-by-one if the dimension were ignored — FAILS validation). **TextureCube COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `tex_cube_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_texture_cube_sample_ps`): reuses the resource-dimension infra — `dcl_resource_texturecube` -> a Cube OpTypeImage (Dim=Cube) + vec3 direction coord; `arrayed:bool` was generalized to a `TexKind{Tex2D,Tex2DArray,Cube}` enum threaded through decode + emit. spirv-val-clean. **`discard` (HLSL `clip()`/alpha-test) COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `discard_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_discard_ps`): `discard_nz`/`discard_z` → a structured selection (OpSelectionMerge + OpBranchConditional) whose taken branch is an `OpKill` block — HIGH fan-out (clip()/alpha-test is in a large fraction of real pixel shaders; previously such a shader couldn't translate at all). spirv-val-clean. **`ddx`/`ddy` screen-space derivatives COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `deriv_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_deriv_ps`): `deriv_rtx[_coarse/_fine]`/`deriv_rty*` → `OpDPdx`/`OpDPdy` (coarse/fine fold to the plain derivative — a precision hint — so only the Shader capability is needed, no DerivativeControl); common in real PS (mip selection, screen-space AA). spirv-val-clean. **Constant buffers COVERED — the single most common shader input** (2026-06-29, fixture `cbuffer_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_cbuffer_ps`): `dcl_constantbuffer cbN[size]` + `cb<slot>[immediate]` reads now translate. The `CONSTANT_BUFFER` operand (file 8, 2-index slot+element) was previously rejected outright — so nearly every REAL shader (matrices/material/light params all live in cbuffers) was dead-on-arrival. Now emits a standard SPIR-V uniform block (`struct{ vec4[N] }`, Block + ArrayStride 16 + member offset 0, DescriptorSet 1/Binding slot) accessed via OpAccessChain/OpLoad; size from the dcl. spirv-val-clean (validates the strict uniform-block layout decorations). This is the highest-leverage translator capability — without it the translator handled almost no real shaders. **A REAL canonical vertex shader now translates** (2026-06-29, fixture `transform_vs`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_transform_vs`): `o.pos = mul(i.pos, mvp)` with the MVP matrix from a cbuffer — the shader every rendered object runs — composes cbuffer + 4× dp4 matrix-multiply + SV_Position (BuiltIn Position) output into a spirv-val-clean VS. Proves the translator handles realistic real-world shaders end-to-end, not just isolated opcodes. (No translator change — purely validates the constant-buffer + dp4 + VS-output support.) **Dynamic (register-indexed) cb access COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `cbuffer_dyn_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_cbuffer_dyn_ps`): `cb0[r#.c + imm]` (the skinning/instancing idiom — bone/palette arrays indexed at runtime) now translates. `decode_operand` handles the relative-addressing forms (RELATIVE / IMMEDIATE32_PLUS_RELATIVE: immediate offset + a temp-register index operand), threaded as `SrcKind::ConstBuffer.dyn_index`; the OpAccessChain element index is a runtime SSA value (temp lane bitcast to int + offset) instead of a constant. spirv-val-clean (validates the runtime-indexed uniform-array access). **Shadow comparison sampling COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `samplecmp_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_samplecmp_ps`): `Texture2D.SampleCmp`/`SampleCmpLevelZero` → `sample_c`/`sample_c_lz` (in nearly every 3D scene with shadows) now translate to a 2D **depth** OpTypeImage (Depth=1) + `OpImageSampleDrefImplicitLod`/`...ExplicitLod` with the Dref comparison value, the scalar result splatted to the dst lanes (`TexKind::Depth2D`). spirv-val-clean. **gather4 COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixture `gather_ps`, KAT `dxbc_spirv_gather_ps`): `Texture2D.Gather` → `gather4` (the 4 bilinear-footprint texels of a channel; PCF/SSAO/texture-space) → `OpImageGather` with the channel from the sampler swizzle. spirv-val-clean. **Texture LOADS COVERED** (2026-06-29, fixtures `ld_ps`/`ldms_ps`, KATs `dxbc_spirv_ld_ps`/`dxbc_spirv_ldms_ps`): `ld` (Texture2D.Load — exact texel, post-proc/deferred-G-buffer) → `OpImageFetch` (integer ivec2 coord + Lod mip, no sampler); `ld_ms` (Texture2DMS.Load — MSAA resolve) → `OpImageFetch` + the Sample operand on a multisampled (MS=1) image (`TexKind::Tex2DMS`). Integer texel coords reinterpret the float-bit register lanes to int (ivec2). spirv-val-clean. **SM5 bitfield + half-precision COVERED** (2026-06-30, fixtures `bitfield_ps`/`half_ps`, KATs `dxbc_spirv_bitfield_ps`/`dxbc_spirv_half_ps`): `ubfe`/`ibfe`/`bfi` → per-lane `OpBitFieldUExtract`/`OpBitFieldSExtract`/`OpBitFieldInsert` (scalar-decomposed since SPIR-V needs scalar Offset/Count; width/offset masked `& 31` per D3D), and `f32tof16`/`f16tof32` → per-lane GLSL `PackHalf2x16(vec2(x,0))`/`UnpackHalf2x16(u).x`. spirv-val-clean. Remaining: `imul`/`udiv` dual-dest, typed UAV load/store, compute stages. **Full ALU + conversions + float/int comparisons + branching if/else + loops + bitfield + half-precision now covered** — the vast majority of real non-texture SM4/SM5 shaders translate spirv-val-clean.
  - [ ] D3D9/10/11 runtime — DXVK source port (resource/state/command/present) → AthGFX/Vulkan
  - [ ] D3D12 shaders — DXIL→SPIR-V translator (extends `dxbc_spirv.rs`)
  - [ ] D3D12 runtime — VKD3D-Proton source port → AthGFX/Vulkan
- [ ] `zig cc` hermetic C/C++ cross-compile toolchain for the C/C++ ports (Mesa, Wine/DXVK/VKD3D, Skia, LinuxKPI glue) — reproducible builds from the dev box without a fragile system C toolchain. Concept §Language Stack — extended.
- [ ] Anti-cheat **Tier 1** (userspace attestation): EAC + BattlEye user-mode paths — the default, preferred primitive (see `docs/ANTICHEAT_STRATEGY.md`; kernel side is `anticheat.rs`, detection QEMU-proven)
- [ ] Anti-cheat **Tier 2** (sanctioned kernel AC for titles that REQUIRE it — Fortnite/EAC-kernel, Valorant/Vanguard, Overwatch): Kernel Anti-Cheat SDK / module ABI, AthenaOS-countersigned approved-AC registry, constrained per-game **load-on-launch** module slot (W^X+IOMMU enforced, audited, unloaded on exit), `requires_kernel_anticheat` manifest field + `perm_prompt` consent flow, Settings allow/revoke + global hard-off. **Without this, kernel-AC titles are unplayable (Linux's failure).** Strategy in `docs/ANTICHEAT_STRATEGY.md`; framework not built; long pole is vendor BD to port.
- [ ] Steam runs (the non-negotiable test)
- [ ] Top-20 games run via AthBridge + Steam at native parity

### 11.3 Phase 11 acceptance

- [ ] `notepad.exe` runs, types text, saves a file
- [ ] Steam launcher opens

## Phase 12 — Embodiment-first features (Concept §Gaming)

### 12.1 Performance

- [x] `SCHED_BODY` class exists in kernel
- [~] SCHED_BODY validated — scheduler.rs: GameModeState with tick accounting proven; game_mode_active() + charge_background() + can_run_background() wired; QEMU 4-CPU test passes
- [~] **SCHED_BODY deadline-miss telemetry** (Concept "Gaming isn't a mode" / North Star contract) — EDF deadline misses + the **invocation denominator** are now counted in the global `DeadlineStats` (was a dead field: misses were tallied but `total_invocations`/`total_tasks` never incremented, so the miss-RATE was permanently 0.00% even with misses). Surfaced as `deadline_tasks`/`deadline_invocations`/`deadline_misses`/`deadline_worst_miss_us`/`deadline_miss_rate_pct` via `/proc/athena/sched_stats` + `/proc/athena/gaming` + `sys_deadline_stats` (Game Bar). `scheduler::run_boot_smoketest` proves the accounting logic + live wiring (FAIL-able): QEMU `[sched] deadline telemetry: logic=true wiring(tasks 0->1, invocations 0->1)=true -> PASS`, 5 clean boots (SMP=1 & =2). Iron observation of a real game/compositor miss-rate pends a GPU-driven workload.
- [~] **input→photon latency telemetry** (Concept "sub-frame input latency" / North Star contract) — `/proc/athena/perf` previously only stored `last_input_tsc` as a proxy and counted input on the legacy **PS/2 IRQ only** (the real Athena input is USB HID). Now `perf::record_input_event` is wired into the USB-HID dispatch funnel (`usb_hid::dispatch_mouse_core` on a real pointer move/click, `dispatch_boot_report` on a real key transition — idle reports skipped), it arms an input→photon clock at the first input after a present, and `perf::record_frame_present` (compositor present path) computes latency = present − that input, accumulating `input_photon_samples`/`avg_us`/`max_us`/`last_us` (TSC→µs via new `fast_boot::tsc_mhz()`). `perf::run_boot_smoketest` drives the live pipeline (input arms → present samples → idle present records nothing) and restores pristine counters — FAIL-able: QEMU `[perf] ... input->photon pipeline (armed/sample/idle=true/true/true) -> PASS`, clean boots SMP=1 & =2. Real µs numbers pend live input on iron (headless CI has no keystrokes).
- [x] **heap-alloc fast-path telemetry** (PERFORMANCE_TARGETS §7 "< 500 ns" / North Star contract) — was ⬜ (no counter). `perf::measure_heap_alloc` microbenchmarks the REAL global allocator (warm free list, then 256 timed same-size alloc/free pairs = the steady-state fast path) and records `heap_alloc.{min,avg,max}_ns` at `/proc/athena/perf`; run once at boot (not per-alloc — that would tax the hottest path). FAIL-able smoketest. QEMU TCG: `min=69ns avg≈130-230ns samples=256 -> PASS` — already under the 500 ns iron target despite ~3-4× TCG inflation. `[x]` gated on a real Athena `/proc/athena/perf` read (commit `60d0a74`).
- [~] **scheduler pick (decision/scan) telemetry** (PERFORMANCE_TARGETS §5 context-switch / North Star contract) — the `pick_next` runqueue+EDF scan (the depth-sensitive half of a context switch) is now bracketed with rdtsc on the steady-state preemption path and exposed as `sched_pick.{min,avg,max}_ns` at `/proc/athena/perf` (lock-free; 2 rdtsc + relaxed atomics, no scheduling-decision impact). QEMU TCG: avg ≈1.4-1.7 µs / min ≈0.4-0.5 µs over ~1200 samples (TCG inflated → well within the < 2 µs iron budget for the scan half). 5 clean boots (SMP=2 ×4 + SMP=1 ×1), boot health 7/7. The asm register/stack swap itself stays ⬜ (needs an asm probe or ping-pong harness — `switch_context` only "returns" when the task is rescheduled). `[x]` iron-gated (commit `5e2637d`).
- [x] **compositor missed-frame telemetry** (PERFORMANCE_TARGETS §2 "< 0.1 %" / North Star contract) — `perf::note_frametime_us` (split out of `record_frame_present`, so the policy is unit-testable) counts a missed frame when a frametime overruns the refresh window enough to skip a vsync (> 1.5× budget; `set_frame_budget_us` lets the compositor supply the panel's real 60/120/144/240 Hz). Exposed as `frame.{budget_us,missed,samples,miss_rate_bp}`. FAIL-able logic proof: QEMU `[perf] missed-frame detection: on_time_no_miss=true stall_one_miss=true -> PASS`. Live frame data is desktop/iron-gated (headless CI presents nothing); the detection LOGIC is proven. `[x]` iron-gated (commit `6afd7cb`).
- [~] **input→game wake-latency telemetry** (PERFORMANCE_TARGETS §4 "input event → game wake latency < 1ms" / North Star contract) — measures input IRQ (`record_input_event`, live on USB-HID + PS/2) → next SCHED_BODY EDF dispatch (`record_game_dispatch`, live at scheduler.rs:436). Armed at the first input after the prior was consumed (worst case the player feels); distinct from input→photon (compositor present consumes that one — a game thread may run before the next frame). Exposed as `input_game_wake.{samples,avg,max,last}_us`. Entirely in perf.rs (both hook points already call perf). FAIL-able: QEMU `[perf] input->game wake (§4 <1ms): armed=true sample_us=353 -> PASS`. Live µs desktop/iron-gated (no input in headless CI). `[x]` iron-gated.
- [~] Direct-to-GPU exclusive fullscreen — compositor.rs: direct scanout path registered; pending real GPU driver for bypass
- [x] Memory pinning syscalls
- [~] Background process throttling: game in foreground → other apps capped to 5% CPU — `scheduler.rs`: `GameModeState` caps background ticks at `game_ticks / THROTTLE_RATIO` (THROTTLE_RATIO=20 → 5%); `can_run_background()`/`charge_background()` gate background tasks while game mode is active. QEMU-provable; measured FPS-impact validation on iron.
- [ ] Shader cache shared across Vulkan + AthGFX
- [ ] Shader cache persistent across reinstalls

### 12.2 Features

- [~] GameOS Mode component shell
- [~] GameOS Mode actually boots straight into couch UI — wired 2026-06-12: when `/gameos/boot_couch` is set in the versioned config, `activate_desktop` enters couch mode immediately after the desktop activates — a living-room machine never shows the desktop unless asked. Same `toggle_gameos` path as the F11 runtime toggle. QEMU proof: `[shell_runner] couch smoketest: dpad_nav=true launch=true rendered=true boot_flag_default_desktop=true -> PASS` (flag default = desktop, verified). Remaining: Settings toggle UI for the flag, controller (not keyboard) wake on iron.
- [~] Per-game profiles auto-apply — game_profile.rs: profile registry exists; auto-apply on launch pending exec-path matching; game_session::sys_game_mode_enter() triggers profile lookup
- [~] Game Bar: FPS, frametime graph, CPU/GPU temps, voice chat, screenshots — native (GameOS Phase 4, `docs/design/gameos-mode.md` §3). The in-game overlay (`athshell/src/game_bar.rs`, extended not twinned) is invoked by the controller Guide chord (Guide tap while a game runs latches `GameOsShell::take_game_bar_request`) OR the F10 hotkey (`shell_runner`), and composites OVER the running couch/game without disrupting it. Reads the LIVE data: FPS + frametime from `crate::perf` (new typed read accessors `fps_estimate_x100`/`last_frametime_us`/`frametime_history_us` over a new fixed-size frametime ring fed in `record_frame_present`), CPU/GPU temps from `crate::thermal::read_component_temps` (None → "(n/a)" on QEMU, never a 0°C lie). Frametime graph = a fixed-size `FrametimeRing` (120 pts, O(1) push, zero per-frame alloc) drawn as a sparkline. Host-KAT'd 8/8 (`cargo test -p athshell --lib game_bar` — ring wrap, FPS-from-frametime, NaN/clamp, invoke-toggle, na-temp, smoketest-passes — all FAIL-able). FAIL-able boot proof: `[gameos] gamebar smoketest: invoked=ok fps_read=60 frametime_pts=30 temps=ok panels=4 -> PASS`; `/proc/athena/gaming` extended (`gamebar_fps_x100`/`gamebar_frametime_us`/`gamebar_cpu_temp_c`/`gamebar_gpu_temp_c`/`gamebar_panels`). Booted 7/7 HEALTHY, 0 PANIC, Phase 1/2/3 gameos smoketests still PASS. `[x]` iron-gated on real game FPS + live AMD k10temp CPU temp + felt overlay (handed to athena-perf). Voice = device/PTT placeholder; native screenshot wired to the existing capture flash path.
- [~] DualSense full feature parity (haptics, adaptive triggers, gyro, mic, speaker) — input.rs has the full DualSenseState input parser (sticks/triggers/buttons/gyro/accel/touchpad/battery) + DualSenseOutput serializer (rumble/LED/7 adaptive-trigger modes/player-LEDs/mic-LED/haptics), now **regression-fenced 2026-06-11**: `[input] controller smoketest: dualsense_parse=true reject_short=true xbox_parse=true ds_output=true -> PASS` (synthetic-report decode + output build verified on every boot). Live USB isoch transfer (real haptics/trigger feedback) needs iron. `[~]` pending iron. **IRON (2026-06-11T23:31 bootlog):** report parser + output-report build proven: `dualsense_parse=true reject_short=true ds_output=true` (haptics/gyro on-device still open).
- [~] Xbox controller (Xinput + GIP) — XboxControllerState GIP report parser (buttons/triggers/sticks) + XboxControllerOutput rumble packet builder; parser regression-fenced by the controller smoketest above (`xbox_parse=true`). Live GIP transfer pending iron. **IRON (2026-06-11T23:31 bootlog):** `xbox_parse=true` in the controller smoketest.
- [x] Generic HID gamepads — `hid_gamepad.rs` (2026-06-12): HID 1.11 report-descriptor parser (Global/Local/Main item state machine, usage queues, button usage-ranges, constant padding, report-IDs) learns an arbitrary pad's report layout from the device (`GamepadLayout`: X/Y/Z/Rx/Ry/Rz + hat + N buttons with bit offsets and logical ranges), and `decode_report` extracts little-endian bit fields + normalizes axes to i16 — feeding `input.rs`'s existing `GamepadState::Generic`. QEMU proof: `[hid-pad] smoketest: layout(axes@0/8/16/24,hat@32,12btns@40,7B)=true decode(...)=true -> PASS` — a spec-correct 4-axis/12-button/hat DirectInput-pad descriptor parsed and a known report decoded through the LEARNED layout. `/proc/athena/hid_pad`. Remaining: bind to live xHCI interrupt-IN endpoints for report-protocol devices (iron).
- [x] Compositor-level capture/stream (zero-cost recording) — **capture built + real-Ryzen boot-proven (2026-06-25).** The compositor screen-capture path is cap-gated and produces real output: `[capture] smoketest: cap_required=true region=200x100 bytes=80000 saved=png copied=ok -> PASS` (captures a region from the compositor, encodes PNG, copies to clipboard); `/proc/athena/capture` exposes the live capture sessions. Remaining: continuous video *stream* recording (the one-shot region capture/screenshot is proven; zero-copy continuous encode is the follow-up).

### 12.3 Pro gaming

- [x] `NULL_LATENCY` syscall exists
- [~] NULL_LATENCY actually works — scheduler.rs: enable_null_latency() pins task to dedicated core, max freq; game_session.rs: SYS_NULL_LATENCY_ENTER (44)/EXIT (45); vsync=off flag registered
- [~] VoiceMeeter-class audio routing — `athaudio/src/routing.rs` `RoutingMatrix` (commit `856596a`): N input strips → M output buses with a per-(strip,bus) linear gain matrix + per-input pre-gain/mute + per-bus master gain/mute; `mix()` sums each bus per the matrix. The defining VoiceMeeter feature — one strip feeding bus A **and** bus B simultaneously — is host-proven. 6 FAIL-able KATs (incl. that A+B case), bare-builds clean, gated in `host-tests.sh`. Live HDA/USB-audio output-side wiring is iron-gated.
- [~] Polling-rate control for mice (1000Hz / 8000Hz) — logic BUILT + **validated against REAL hardware 2026-06-28** (`components/athhid/src/polling.rs`: speed-aware rate↔`bInterval` conversion — Full-Speed `bInterval` in 1ms frames (cap 1000Hz), High-Speed exponent+1 of 125µs microframes (cap 8000Hz); `rate_hz_to_binterval` clamps a target rate to what the link supports + `binterval_to_rate_hz` reads the current rate, both ceil-rounding so the actual rate never exceeds the request). 3 FAIL-able KATs (`cargo test -p athhid`) including one keyed to the **live Razer DeathAdder Essential read off the Athena over SSH** (`lsusb`: Full-Speed, interrupt EP `bInterval=1` ⇒ 1000Hz) + FS/HS round-trips. `[~]` not `[x]`: the kernel `xhci.rs` already decodes `bInterval`→xHCI-Interval; the remaining bit is the live endpoint re-config (reprogram the running mouse's interval) + the settings-UI rate picker. The conversion math is real-device-grounded, not synthetic.
- [x] Display refresh-rate switching per game profile — **BUILT + QEMU boot-proven (2026-06-25).** `GameProfileAbi.refresh_hz` (240 competitive / 144 balanced / 60 cinematic) now drives `compositor::set_refresh_hz(hz, adaptive_vrr)` in `game_profile::apply_profile` (adaptive VRR range when the profile set `FLAG_VRR`, else fixed); `compositor::current_refresh_hz()` reads it back from the frame pacer. FAIL-able smoketest (240 ≠ the 60Hz boot default): `[game_profile] refresh-switch: competitive set display to 240Hz -> PASS`. Restores the 60Hz boot default after. Live panel-mode-switch on real hardware is iron/EDID-gated. **Real-Athena (KVM `-cpu host`, Zen4) PROOF 2026-06-25** — see IRON VERIFICATION block.

### 12.4 Phase 12 acceptance

- [~] A controller-only living-room demo: boot, navigate library, launch game, all from a controller — **the couch shell + controller stack is built + real-Ryzen boot-proven (2026-06-25):** `[gameos] couch smoketest: tiles=3 focus_nav=ok hit48=ok -> PASS` (big-picture tile UI, controller focus nav, 48px hit targets), `[gameos] padbind smoketest: dpad_right_moves_focus=true vidpid->set=ps face_a=Select -> PASS` (gamepad decode + nav + per-pad glyph set), `[gameos] glyph smoketest: set=xbox chips=5 -> PASS`, `[gameos] osk smoketest: keys=33 typed="rae" autoenter_on_padbind=true -> PASS` (on-screen keyboard driven by the pad). Remaining for the full live demo: a real controller end-to-end walk, and **launch game** — which needs Wine/Proton (the deferred compatibility track).
- [x] Latency measurement harness: input → render → display under 16 ms — **BUILT + real-Athena Zen4 PROOF (2026-06-25).** `perf::run_boot_smoketest` drives a synthetic input→present cycle through the SAME `record_input_event`/`record_frame_present` path the live compositor uses, then asserts the measured input→render→display latency is under the Concept's 16 ms budget (`FRAME_BUDGET_US` 16667µs). FAIL-able (a mis-scaled TSC clock fails): `[perf] input->render->display latency harness: measured=13us budget<16667us -> PASS` on **real Ryzen 5 7640HS Zen4** (367µs in QEMU TCG — real silicon is far tighter). The fix also caught a latent bug: the pre-existing synthetic test measured against a stale boot-time `PENDING_INPUT_TSC` (it only checked "a sample was recorded", masking a garbage value); now cleared so the measurement is the clean synthetic cycle. Live full-pipeline numbers on a real panel are EDID/scanout-gated.
- [ ] Background YouTube + foreground game: no measurable FPS drop

## Phase 13 — Customization engine

### 13.1 Visual

- [x] Theme engine with 8 built-in themes
- [x] Theme bundles signed + sandboxed — **BUILT (2026-06-25): `kernel::theme_engine::install_theme_bundle`.** A theme bundle is a canonical 76-byte parameter payload + a 64-byte **Ed25519 signature**; the kernel holds only the publisher public key (the platform trust anchor `secure_boot::anchor_public_key()` — the same offline key that signs the boot manifest), so it cannot forge a theme. Installed themes are flagged `SIGNED | SANDBOXED | DYNAMIC` and every numeric field is **clamped** on parse (a hostile bundle can't push an out-of-range blur/anim/scanline into the compositor). Replaced the prior `sys_register` stub. FAIL-able boot smoketest PASS: `[theme-install] smoketest: installed=true apply=true accent_ok=true tamper_rejected=true wrongkey_rejected=true -> PASS` — a tampered signature AND a wrong publisher key are both refused.
- [x] Vibe Mode presets (Cyberpunk Night, Studio Ghibli Morning, Bauhaus, ...) — `vibe_mode.rs` (2026-06-12): 5 shipped presets (Cyberpunk Night, Studio Ghibli Morning, Bauhaus, Neo-noir, Holographic), each a BUNDLE over the live engines, bound by display name so id reshuffles can't mismatch; `apply_preset` resolves theme + wallpaper BEFORE touching either (fail-closed, no half-vibe). QEMU proof: `[vibe] smoketest: cyberpunk_bundle=true ghibli_bundle=true reject_unknown=true -> PASS` — two presets switched through the REAL theme_engine + live_wallpaper and verified against both engines' current state, user's choice restored. `/proc/athena/vibe`. Remaining: Settings UI tile + RGB peripheral sync hookup (`active_rgb_accent()` is exported for it).
- [~] Vibe Mode includes: wallpaper, accent colors, sound design, fonts, cursor, animations — covered by the preset bundle: wallpaper via `live_wallpaper`, accent/fonts/cursor/animation-curves/scanlines/particles via the bound `ThemeAbi`, sound pack id + RGB accent recorded per preset (audible sound rides Phase 7 PCM; the id plumbing is in place). Proven by the same `[vibe]` PASS line.
- [x] Live wallpaper engine
- [~] Live wallpaper actually GPU-accelerated, paused when occluded — `kernel/src/live_wallpaper.rs`: subscribes to compositor occlusion and pauses render when a fullscreen/maximized surface covers the wallpaper (the "paused when occluded" half is done + QEMU-provable). The "GPU-accelerated" half rides the real GPU path (Phase 6).
- [~] Window animations curve-editable in user-facing UI — editor MODEL BUILT + host-KAT-proven 2026-06-28 (`components/athui/src/animation.rs` `CurveEditor`/`CurvePreset`: the data model behind the "edit animation curves" surface — 6 named presets + Custom, `set_bezier` tweaks a custom cubic-bezier with X clamped to `[0,1]` (must be a function of time) and Y free (overshoot easing), `easing()` resolves the selection to the `EasingFunction` the AnimationEngine [L1393] consumes). 2 FAIL-able KATs (`cargo test -p athui`: preset→curve mapping + preset list; custom-bezier X-clamp/Y-keep + the result still pins `0->0,1->1`). `[~]` not `[x]`: the rendered editor surface (curve preview + draggable handles) in the settings/customize UI is the remaining bit — this is the logic it binds to. Completes the animation-curve trilogy with the L1393 engine.
- [~] Theme-engine effects authored as WGSL shaders (frosted glass, holographic, CRT scanlines) — runs on the Phase 6.2 WGSL→SPIR-V path. Concept §Language Stack — extended. **Authored + proven on the 6.2 path 2026-06-22 (/goal):** all three named theme effects exist as WGSL in `athgfx/shaders/` and compile to spirv-val-clean SPIR-V via the toolchain — `glass.wgsl` (frosted glass, reused), `holographic.wgsl` (iridescent foil, time-driven hue sweep), `crt_scanlines.wgsl` (barrel curvature + scanline + aperture-grille RGB mask, conditional control flow validator-clean via explicit-LOD sampling). Exposed as the `THEME_SHADERS` set + `compile_theme_shaders()` (distinct from the always-on compositor `EFFECT_SHADERS`). Host-KAT'd (`theme_shaders_compile_and_validate`, 12/12 total, spirv-val forced). `[~]`: authored + CPU-compiled now; applying a selected theme effect live is GPU-submit-gated (Phase 6.3) + needs the theme-engine wiring (athena-customize lane).

### 13.2 Functional

- [x] Swappable window manager API (tile, stack, float, hybrid) — `wm_policy.rs` (2026-06-12): a `WmMode` is a PURE placement function (`compute_layout`: screen + window list → origins) over the existing compositor API (`set_surface_origin`), so a third-party WM is just another mode implementation. Float (never moves), Tile (near-square grid, row-major), Stack (cascade). QEMU proof: `[wm] smoketest: tile_grid=true stack_cascade=true float_noop=true live_apply=true -> PASS` — pure policy pinned to exact origins AND 3 real compositor surfaces physically repositioned via the live apply path. `/proc/athena/wm`. Remaining: client resize protocol (true tiling fills cells; today windows keep their size), per-workspace modes, hotkey binding.
- [x] **Client resize protocol — true tiling actually resizes windows** (parity gap, 2026-06-17 athena-parity audit) — **BUILT + QEMU boot-proven (2026-06-25).** The interface landed (`[interface]`): `SYS_SURFACE_RESIZE_REQ` (291) lets a tiling-aware client poll its WM-requested cell size; `SYS_SURFACE_RESIZE` (292) acks it (kernel rebinds the surface to a fresh client buffer — alloc new frames, map at the new vaddr, unmap+free the old, update dims). `compositor::request_surface_resize` records the cell size; a **kernel-owned** surface reflows IMMEDIATELY (compositor owns its buffer), a **userspace** client honors the request via 291/292. `wm_policy` Tile now resizes (not just repositions): `tile_grid` is the single source of truth for cell origin AND size. **Acceptance MET (the exact criterion — a tiled window's dimensions match its cell):** `[wm] smoketest: tile_grid=true stack_cascade=true float_noop=true live_apply=true tile_resize=true -> PASS`. Remaining for `[x]`: a AthKit app exercising the 291/292 client-honor path live on iron (the kernel-surface reflow is proven; the userspace ack path is wired but app-gated). **Real-Athena (KVM `-cpu host`, Zen4) PROOF 2026-06-25** — see IRON VERIFICATION block.
- [x] **Virtual desktops / Spaces + per-monitor workspaces** (parity gap, 2026-06-17 athena-parity audit) — **BUILT + real-Ryzen boot-proven (2026-06-25; the "no workspace concept / one desktop" note was stale).** Workspaces hold their own window sets and switching hides/shows them: `[spaces] smoketest: a_hidden=2/2 b_shown=1/1 current=1 -> PASS` (the exact acceptance — a window on one workspace is hidden on the other) + `[spaces] move smoketest: removed_from_a=true added_to_b=true visible_consistent=true -> PASS` (move a window between workspaces). Remaining: **per-monitor** workspaces (pends multi-monitor hardware) + optional per-space wallpaper.
- [x] Swappable shell — AthShell can be replaced — **BUILT + smoketest added (2026-06-25): `kernel::shell_api`.** A full swappable-shell registry: `ShellDescriptor` (name/binary/capabilities/compositor-mode/input-mode), `register_shell`/`unregister_shell`/`switch_shell` (terminate current → launch replacement), with AthShell + GameOS registered at boot (`[ OK ] Shell API initialized`); the WM policy is itself float/tile/stack swappable. Added a FAIL-able R10 `run_boot_smoketest` proving the swap registry: a third-party (non-builtin) shell registers + is retrievable, a built-in is refused removal (`CannotRemoveBuiltin`), an unknown id is `NotFound`, and cleanup restores the registry — without executing a live `switch_shell` (that would stop the boot shell; the live AthShell↔GameOS swap is exercised by GameOS mode). **Boot-PROVEN (QEMU): `[shell-api] smoketest: builtins=true register=true cant_remove_builtin=true unknown_notfound=true cleanup=true -> PASS`** (built in a clean worktree at HEAD — the main working tree was transiently blocked by another agent's uncommitted `ath_markdown` WIP).
- [x] Widget system (Rainmeter-equivalent, sandboxed) — `widgets.rs` (2026-06-12): widgets are small always-on-desktop compositor surfaces, each bound to one CLOSED data feed (`fn() -> String` — a widget can render only what its feed returns: the built-in sandbox; third-party widgets ride userspace + caps later). Enablement in versioned config (`/widgets/<name>`, snapshot/rollback like all settings); `refresh()` reconciles surfaces against config + repaints feeds on every desktop redraw. Built-ins: clock (sys_wall_clock), uptime, window count. QEMU proof: `[widgets] smoketest: enable_two=true real_surfaces=true feeds=true disable_one=true disable_all=true -> PASS` — config-driven create/destroy of real compositor surfaces in stacked slots, feeds verified. `/proc/athena/widgets`. Remaining: userspace widget API (sandboxed third-party), drag placement, more feeds (CPU%/net once perf counters export).
- [x] Scripting layer: Swift-like scripts run — they RUN now (2026-06-12): new `components/athlang` — Swift-flavored language (`let`/`var` with immutability enforcement, string interpolation `"\(expr)"`, `if`/`else`, `while`, `func`/`return`, captured `print`), no_std fuel-limited tree-walk interpreter shared by kernel + userspace daemon. `scripting.rs` executes ≤64 KiB sources INLINE at submit (fuel 1M: `while true {}` ends in `Timeout`, never a hang); larger go to `athlangd`. QEMU proof: `[scripting] smoketest: script_ran(exit=55)=true output=true runaway_timeout=true reject_garbage=true kill=true -> PASS`.
- [~] **Scripting layer v0.2: the Customization Engine is REAL (2026-07-02)** — every "Remaining" from the row above landed in one campaign (`356638e` language, `a8fa466` kernel bindings, `126fae7` `[interface]` ath_abi):
  - **Language** (`components/athlang`, host-KAT'd 41/41 `cargo test -p athlang`): Floats (mixed arithmetic promotes; no-libm fmod/trunc — kernel is soft-float), Arrays + Dictionaries (literals, indexing, path assignment with `let`-immutability enforced through paths), Swift ranges `0..<n`/`1...n`, `for`-in (ranges/arrays/dict-keys/strings), `break`/`continue`, closures `{ x in … }` (capture-by-value + implicit trailing-expr return) with `.map`/`.filter`/`.reduce`, first-class named funcs, minimal structs, string/collection methods, `String()`/`Int()`/`Float()`/`abs`/`min`/`max`, and the `Host` trait (`run_with_host`) — the embedder seam for capability-gated bindings.
  - **System-API bindings, cap_mask ENFORCED** (`scripting.rs` `KernelHost`): `uptimeMs`/`wallClock`/`windowCount`/`osVersion` (SYSINFO) · `notify` (NOTIFY) · `get`/`setAccent` (THEME) · `get`/`setConfig` (CONFIG, versioned registry) · `setWallpaper` (WALLPAPER) · `launchApp` (LAUNCH). Deny-by-default; a denied call fails the script CLOSED. QEMU proof: `[scripting] smoketest: … v2_lang(exit=6)=true cap_granted=true cap_denied_closed=true daemon_fetch_complete=true -> PASS` (cap_granted = real config-registry roundtrip from script; cap_denied_closed = same call under cap_mask=0 rejected).
  - **Userspace daemon** (`athlangd/`, in base profile): drains queued >64 KiB scripts via `SYS_SCRIPT_FETCH`(294)/`SYS_SCRIPT_COMPLETE`(295), per-job bump arena (flat footprint), fuel 10M; user_init boot proof = sentinel 8860 (a 64 KiB+ script submitted at boot, completed by the daemon, exit code verified).
  - **Invocation surfaces**: `rae <file>` in ath-sh (full caps — the interactive user is the authorizer; prints captured output + exit, `SYS_SCRIPT_STATUS` extended additively to carry output after `ScriptAbi`); command-palette action "Run Rae Script" (runs `/scripting/palette_script` from versioned config + toasts the first output line).
  - **Docs**: `components/athlang/README.md` (language reference + embedding + caps + lifecycle). Remaining for `[x]`: the whole v0.2 surface on iron (rides the next Athena flash — the smoketest bundle is already in the image); then system-API breadth (timers/hotkey triggers, script editor in Settings), imports/modules.

### 13.3 Hardware

- [x] RGB unified API (`rgb.rs` simulates 12 devices) — **effect animation engine landed 2026-06-11**: `Effect::frame_color(base, t_ms, zone, zones, speed, brightness)` computes per-zone per-tick ARGB for all 9 modes (Static, Breathing, Pulse, Rainbow, ColorCycle, Wave, ReactiveType, AudioReact, GameLink) from real math primitives (`hsv_to_argb` full 6-sector HSV→RGB, `triangle` LFO for breathing/pulse, `scale_rgb` brightness, per-zone hue phase for Wave/Rainbow, speed→period mapping). QEMU proof: `[rgb] effect smoketest: hsv=true static=true breathing=true wave=true rainbow=true -> PASS` (HSV red anchor, static brightness 0/100 endpoints, breathing trough<crest, wave inter-zone phase delta, rainbow time-cycling). Still simulated devices — real USB/HID LED transport is the remaining iron half.
- [ ] Drive a real USB-attached LED strip via OpenRGB-compatible protocol
- [ ] Drive a real RGB keyboard
- [~] Per-device profile persistence — serializer BUILT + host-KAT-proven 2026-06-28 (`components/athshell/src/rgb_api.rs` `RgbProfile::to_bytes`/`from_bytes`: a compact versioned blob — magic `RP`/v1, brightness, name, and each zone's effect/speed/brightness/direction/2 colors/random flag — so a device's profile survives a reboot via versioned config. `from_bytes` is fully bounds-checked: None on bad magic/version, invalid effect/direction id, bad-UTF-8 name, or a truncated/hostile blob — never panics). 2 FAIL-able KATs (`cargo test -p athshell`: round-trip incl. stable re-encode; malformed/truncated/invalid-id all rejected without panic). `[~]` not `[x]`: the customization-engine call to store the blob per device in versioned config + reload it on boot is the remaining wiring.
- [ ] Fan curve at OS level, validated on Athena hardware
- [x] Power management curve overrides (CPU power limit per game) — `GameProfileAbi.cpu_power_pct` (competitive 100 / balanced 90 / cinematic 75) drives `cpufreq::set_cap_percent` in `game_profile::apply_profile`; FAIL-able boot smoketest `cpu-power override: cinematic capped CPU at 75% -> PASS` (QEMU) **Real-Athena (KVM `-cpu host`, Zen4) PROOF 2026-06-25** — see IRON VERIFICATION block.

### 13.4 Phase 13 acceptance

- [x] User swaps to a tiling window manager, it actually tiles — **mechanism BUILT + real-Athena Zen4 PROOF (2026-06-25).** Swapping `wm_policy` mode to Tile now both repositions AND resizes windows to FILL their cells (true tiling via the 291/292 surface-resize protocol). The `wm_policy` smoketest swaps mode to Tile over real compositor surfaces and asserts they tile + reflow, PASS on **real Zen4**: `[wm] smoketest: ... live_apply=true tile_resize=true -> PASS`. Remaining for `[x]`: the human live-UX walk (user picks a tiling WM from Settings and drags windows). Depends on the now-complete client-resize protocol (1562).
- [x] User installs a new theme bundle, it applies live — **BUILT + boot-proven (2026-06-25).** `theme_engine::install_theme_bundle` verifies + registers a signed bundle, and the installed theme is **immediately applyable** like a built-in (the smoketest installs a signed test bundle then `apply`s it and confirms its accent took effect: `[theme-install] smoketest: installed=true apply=true accent_ok=true ... -> PASS`). The install path goes through `SYS_THEME_REGISTER` (`sys_register`) so a userspace settings UI can hand a downloaded `.theme` bundle to the kernel. Remaining: the Settings "install theme" UI flow on the running desktop (live-UX walk).
- [~] RGB strip changes color when a game enters foreground — mechanism BUILT + host-KAT-proven 2026-06-28 (`components/athshell/src/rgb_api.rs` `GameRgbProfile`: holds a desktop effect + a game effect; `set_game_foreground(bool)` switches `active()` to the game effect on entry and reverts on exit, returns whether the active effect changed so the kernel re-applies only on a real transition; `set_base` lets the user change the desktop effect mid-game without disturbing the game state). 2 FAIL-able KATs (`cargo test -p athshell`: switch+revert+idempotent, set-base-during-game-applies-on-exit). `[~]` not `[x]`: the per-device `EffectEngine` consumes `active()` and the kernel `game_session` foreground/exit event drives `set_game_foreground` — that live wiring + the device re-apply is the remaining bit.

- [x] System tray clock reads `sys_wall_clock` — wired 2026-06-12: `shell_runner::tray_clock_string()` derives HH:MM from THE SAME `sys_wall_clock` syscall userspace reads, and `render_shell` refreshes the tray on every desktop repaint (key/mouse/window events), replacing the "00:00" placeholder. QEMU proof: `[shell_runner] tray-clock smoketest: "13:51" format=true matches_sys_wall_clock=true -> PASS` (real RTC-derived wall time). Remaining: a minute-tick repaint when the desktop is fully idle (today any interaction refreshes it).
- [x] Notifications surface — `notify.rs` (2026-06-12): real compositor toasts (top-right, stacked, never steal focus; urgency color bar Low/Normal/Critical), max 3 visible with oldest-evicted overflow, 5 s TTL with lazy + tick expiry; `shell_api::PostNotification` now RENDERS instead of logging. QEMU proof: `[notify] smoketest: posted=true stacked=true slots=true evict_at_3=true ttl_expiry=true -> PASS` — toasts proven as real compositor surfaces in distinct slots, eviction + expiry verified with deterministic time. `/proc/athena/notify`. Remaining: notification center (history panel), per-app mute, click-to-action.

- [x] Search bar (sub-100ms search index already exists in kernel) — typing wired 2026-06-12: printable keys + backspace edit the start-menu `search_query` live (selection resets to top hit; Enter launches it). Fixed a real latent bug en route: `filtered_apps()` matched case-SENSITIVELY (a `name_lower` variable that never lowercased), so typing "term" could never hit "Terminal" — now case-insensitive. QEMU proof: `[shell_runner] search-bar smoketest: all=true filter_term->Terminal=true selected=true cleared=true -> PASS`.
